import time
import random
from datetime import datetime

class ActivityProtectorAgent:
    def __init__(self):
        pass

    def kaos_ve_sapma_kontrolu(self):
        """Sistemin kusursuz robotik ritmini bozarak algoritmayДұ ЕҹaЕҹДұrtДұr."""
        zar = random.randint(1, 100)
        
        if zar <= 15:  # %15 ihtimalle yapay tembellik modu
            print("[KAOS PROTECTOR] Yapay tembellik tetiklendi. Sistem Еҹu an sadece geziniyor...")
            time.sleep(random.uniform(30, 90))
            return True
        elif zar > 15 and zar <= 25:  # %10 ihtimalle paylaЕҹДұmДұ erteleme kararДұ
            print("[KAOS PROTECTOR] Д°nsansДұ vazgeГ§me simГјlasyonu: Д°Еҹlem bir sonraki tura ertelendi.")
            return False
        
        print("[KAOS PROTECTOR] Ritim insansДұ standartlarda, akДұЕҹ devam ediyor.")
        return True

    def gece_uyku_modu(self):
        """Gece saatlerinde sistemin tamamen uyumasДұnДұ saДҹlar (GerГ§ek insan ritmi)."""
        su_an = datetime.now().hour
        if su_an >= 0 and su_an <= 6:  # 00:00 - 06:00 arasДұ
            print("[KAOS PROTECTOR] Gece modu aktif. Robotlar uyuyor, iЕҹlem yapДұlmayacak.")
            return True
        return False

class AdvancedDashboardHandler(BaseHTTPRequestHandler):
    def __init__(self, *args, dashboard_manager, **kwargs):
        self.dashboard_manager = dashboard_manager
        super().__init__(*args, **kwargs)
    
    def do_GET(self):
        """GET isteklerini yГ¶net"""
        path = unquote(self.path)
        
        if path == '/':
            self.send_main_page()
        elif path == '/system-status':
            self.send_system_status()
        elif path == '/daily-stats':
            self.send_daily_stats()
        elif path == '/error-logs':
            self.send_error_logs()
        elif path == '/social-posts':
            self.send_social_posts()
        elif path == '/ai-performance':
            self.send_ai_performance()
        elif path == '/web-scraping':
            self.send_web_scraping()
        elif path == '/sales-graphs':
            self.send_sales_graphs()
        elif path == '/high-commission':
            self.send_high_commission()
        elif path == '/sold-products':
            self.send_sold_products()
        elif path == '/commission-tracking':
            self.send_commission_tracking()
        elif path == '/daily-commission':
            self.send_daily_commission()
        elif path == '/24h-reset':
            self.send_24h_reset()
        elif path.startswith('/api/'):
            self.send_api_response(path)
        else:
            self.send_404()

        """Ana sayfayДұ gГ¶nder"""

<script>
let currentTab = 'system-status';

function showTab(tabName) {
    // TГјm tab'leri gizle
    document.querySelectorAll('.tab-content').forEach(tab => {
        tab.classList.remove('active');
    });
    
    // TГјm nav tab'lerini pasif yap
    document.querySelectorAll('.nav-tab').forEach(tab => {
        tab.classList.remove('active');
    });
    
    // SeГ§ili tab'i gГ¶ster
    document.getElementById(tabName).classList.add('active');
    
    // SeГ§ili nav tab'i aktif yap
    event.target.classList.add('active');
    
    currentTab = tabName;
    
    // Tab verilerini yГјkle
    loadTabData(tabName);
}

function showLoading() {
    document.getElementById('loading').classList.add('active');
}

function hideLoading() {
    document.getElementById('loading').classList.remove('active');
}

async function loadTabData(tabName) {
    showLoading();
    
    try {
        const response = await fetch(`/api/${tabName}`);
        const data = await response.json();
        
        updateTabContent(tabName, data);
    } catch (error) {
        console.error('Tab verisi yГјklenemedi:', error);
    } finally {
        hideLoading();
    }
}

function updateTabContent(tabName, data) {
    switch(tabName) {
        case 'system-status':
            updateSystemStatus(data);
            break;
        case 'daily-stats':
            updateDailyStats(data);
            break;
        case 'error-logs':
            updateErrorLogs(data);
            break;
        case 'social-posts':
            updateSocialPosts(data);
            break;
        case 'ai-performance':
            updateAIPerformance(data);
            break;
        case 'web-scraping':
            updateWebScraping(data);
            break;
        case 'sales-graphs':
            updateSalesGraphs(data);
            break;
        case 'high-commission':
            updateHighCommission(data);
            break;
        case 'sold-products':
            updateSoldProducts(data);
            break;
        case 'commission-tracking':
            updateCommissionTracking(data);
            break;
        case 'daily-commission':
            updateDailyCommission(data);
            break;
        case '24h-reset':
            update24hReset(data);
            break;
    }
}

function updateSystemStatus(data) {
    const container = document.getElementById('system-stats');
    container.innerHTML = `
        <div class="stat-card">
            <div class="stat-value">${data.uptime || '0s'}</div>
            <div class="stat-label">вҸ° ГҮalДұЕҹma SГјresi</div>
        </div>
        <div class="stat-card">
            <div class="stat-value">${data.auto_restarts || 0}</div>
            <div class="stat-label">рҹ”„ Otomatik Yeniden BaЕҹlatma</div>
        </div>
        <div class="stat-card">
            <div class="stat-value">${data.health_score || 100}%</div>
            <div class="stat-label">рҹ“Ҡ SaДҹlДұk Skoru</div>
        </div>
        <div class="stat-card">
            <div class="stat-value">${data.errors || 0}</div>
            <div class="stat-label">вқҢ Hata SayДұsДұ</div>
        </div>
        <div class="stat-card">
            <div class="stat-value">${data.warnings || 0}</div>
            <div class="stat-label">вҡ пёҸ UyarДұ SayДұsДұ</div>
        </div>
        <div class="stat-card">
            <div class="stat-value">${data.processes_running || 0}</div>
            <div class="stat-label">рҹӨ– ГҮalДұЕҹan Process'ler</div>
        </div>
        <div class="stat-card">
            <div class="stat-value">${data.memory_usage || '0%'}</div>
            <div class="stat-label">рҹ’ҫ Bellek KullanДұmДұ</div>
        </div>
        <div class="stat-card">
            <div class="stat-value">${data.cpu_usage || '0%'}</div>
            <div class="stat-label">вҡЎ CPU KullanДұmДұ</div>
        </div>
    `;
}

// DiДҹer update fonksiyonlarДұ buraya eklenecek...

async function refreshSystemStatus() {

    loadTabData('system-status');

    if (currentTab) {
        loadTabData(currentTab);
    }

</script>

</html>
        """
        
        self.send_response(200, 'text/html', html_content)
    
    def send_api_response(self, path):
        """API yanДұtДұ gГ¶nder"""
        try:
            endpoint = path.replace('/api/', '')
            
            if endpoint == 'system-status':
                data = self.dashboard_manager.get_system_status()
            elif endpoint == 'daily-stats':
                data = self.dashboard_manager.get_daily_stats()
            elif endpoint == 'error-logs':
                data = self.dashboard_manager.get_error_logs()
            elif endpoint == 'social-posts':
                data = self.dashboard_manager.get_social_posts()
            elif endpoint == 'ai-performance':
                data = self.dashboard_manager.get_ai_performance()
            elif endpoint == 'web-scraping':
                data = self.dashboard_manager.get_web_scraping_status()
            elif endpoint == 'sales-graphs':
                data = self.dashboard_manager.get_sales_graphs()
            elif endpoint == 'high-commission':
                data = self.dashboard_manager.get_high_commission_products()
            elif endpoint == 'sold-products':
                data = self.dashboard_manager.get_sold_products()
            elif endpoint == 'commission-tracking':
                data = self.dashboard_manager.get_commission_tracking()
            elif endpoint == 'daily-commission':
                data = self.dashboard_manager.get_daily_commission()
            elif endpoint == '24h-reset':
                data = self.dashboard_manager.get_24h_reset_status()
            else:
                data = {'error': 'Endpoint not found'}
            
            self.send_response(200, 'application/json', json.dumps(data))
            
        except Exception as e:
            self.send_response(500, 'application/json', json.dumps({'error': str(e)}))
    
    def send_response(self, status_code, content_type, content):
        """HTTP yanДұtДұ gГ¶nder"""
        self.send_response(status_code, content_type, content)
    
    def log_message(self, format, *args):
        pass  # Log mesajlarДұnДұ gГ¶sterme

class AdvancedDashboardManager:
    def __init__(self):
        self.system_manager = None
        self.drive_social_manager = None
        self.sales_alarm_system = None
        
        # VeritabanДұ baДҹlantДұsДұ
        self.db_conn = None
        self.init_database()
    
    def init_database(self):
        """VeritabanДұnДұ baЕҹlat"""
        try:
            self.db_conn = sqlite3.connect('trm_dashboard.db')
            cursor = self.db_conn.cursor()
            
            # TablolarДұ oluЕҹtur
            cursor.execute('''
                CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS system_status (
                    id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
                    timestamp TEXT,
                    uptime INTEGER,
                    auto_restarts INTEGER,
                    health_score INTEGER,
                    errors INTEGER,
                    warnings INTEGER,
                    processes_running INTEGER,
                    memory_usage TEXT,
                    cpu_usage TEXT
                )
            ''')
            
            cursor.execute('''
                CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS daily_stats (
                    id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
                    date TEXT,
                    products_captured INTEGER,
                    high_commission INTEGER,
                    social_published INTEGER,
                    estimated_commission REAL,
                    success_rate REAL
                )
            ''')
            
            cursor.execute('''
                CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS error_logs (
                    id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
                    timestamp TEXT,
                    level TEXT,
                    module TEXT,
                    message TEXT,
                    details TEXT
                )
            ''')
            
            cursor.execute('''
                CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS social_posts (
                    id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
                    timestamp TEXT,
                    platform TEXT,
                    content_type TEXT,
                    product_name TEXT,
                    status TEXT,
                    engagement INTEGER
                )
            ''')
            
            self.db_conn.commit()
            
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"VeritabanДұ baЕҹlatma hatasДұ: {e}")
    
    def get_system_status(self) -> Dict:
        """Sistem durumunu al"""
        try:
            # Sistem bilgilerini al
            import psutil
            
            status = {
                'uptime': '0s',
                'auto_restarts': 0,
                'health_score': 100,
                'errors': 0,
                'warnings': 0,
                'processes_running': 0,
                'memory_usage': f"{psutil.virtual_memory().percent:.1f}%",
                'cpu_usage': f"{psutil.cpu_percent():.1f}%",
                'last_update': datetime.now().isoformat()
            }
            
            return status
            
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Sistem durumu alma hatasДұ: {e}")
            return {'error': str(e)}
    
    def get_daily_stats(self) -> Dict:
        """GГјnlГјk istatistikleri al"""
        try:
            today = datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d')
            
            # VeritabanДұndan gГјnlГјk istatistikleri al
            cursor = self.db_conn.cursor()
            cursor.execute('''
                SELECT * FROM daily_stats WHERE date = ? ORDER BY id DESC LIMIT 1
            ''', (today,))
            
            result = cursor.fetchone()
            
            if result:
                return {
                    'date': result[1],
                    'products_captured': result[2],
                    'high_commission': result[3],
                    'social_published': result[4],
                    'estimated_commission': result[5],
                    'success_rate': result[6]
                }
            else:
                return {
                    'date': today,
                    'products_captured': 0,
                    'high_commission': 0,
                    'social_published': 0,
                    'estimated_commission': 0.0,
                    'success_rate': 0.0
                }
                
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"GГјnlГјk istatistikleri alma hatasДұ: {e}")
            return {'error': str(e)}
    
    def get_error_logs(self) -> Dict:
        """Hata loglarДұnДұ al"""
        try:
            cursor = self.db_conn.cursor()
            cursor.execute('''
                SELECT * FROM error_logs ORDER BY id DESC LIMIT 50
            ''')
            
            results = cursor.fetchall()
            
            logs = []
            for row in results:
                logs.append({
                    'timestamp': row[1],
                    'level': row[2],
                    'module': row[3],
                    'message': row[4],
                    'details': row[5]
                })
            
            return {'logs': logs}
            
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Hata loglarДұ alma hatasДұ: {e}")
            return {'error': str(e)}
    
    def get_social_posts(self) -> Dict:
        """Sosyal medya paylaЕҹДұmlarДұnДұ al"""
        try:
            cursor = self.db_conn.cursor()
            cursor.execute('''
                SELECT * FROM social_posts ORDER BY id DESC LIMIT 50
            ''')
            
            results = cursor.fetchall()
            
            posts = []

                })

            return {'error': str(e)}

            status = {

            return {'error': str(e)}

class AdvancedDashboardServer:
    def __init__(self):
        self.dashboard_manager = AdvancedDashboardManager()
        self.server = None
    
    async def start(self, port=9003):
        """Sunucuyu baЕҹlat"""
        try:
            handler = lambda *args, **kwargs: AdvancedDashboardHandler(*args, dashboard_manager=self.dashboard_manager, **kwargs)
            self.server = HTTPServer(('localhost', port), handler)
            
            # Sunucuyu ayrДұ thread'de baЕҹlat
            server_thread = threading.Thread(target=self.server.serve_forever)
            server_thread.daemon = True
            server_thread.start()
            
            print(f"рҹҢҗ GeliЕҹmiЕҹ YГ¶netim Paneli baЕҹlatДұldДұ: http://localhost:{port}")
            return True
            
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"вқҢ GeliЕҹmiЕҹ yГ¶netim paneli baЕҹlatДұlamadДұ: {e}")
            return False
    
    def stop(self):
        """Sunucuyu durdur"""
        if self.server:
            self.server.shutdown()
            self.server.server_close()

# Ana baЕҹlatДұcДұ
async def main():
    """Ana fonksiyon"""
    print("""
===============================================
    TRM NIRVANA v3.0 - GELД°ЕһMД°Еһ YГ–NETД°M PANELД°
===============================================
  рҹҢҗ ГҮoklu Sayfa YapДұsДұ
  рҹ“Ҡ 12 FarklДұ Panel
  рҹ”„ GerГ§ek ZamanlДұ Veriler
  рҹ“Ҳ Grafiksel GГ¶sterim
  рҹ“ұ Mobil Uyumlu
===============================================
    """)
    
    server = AdvancedDashboardServer()
    
    if await server.start():
        print("рҹҢҗ GeliЕҹmiЕҹ yГ¶netim paneli aktif!")
        print("рҹ“Ҡ Ana panel: http://localhost:9000")
        print("рҹҢҗ GeliЕҹmiЕҹ panel: http://localhost:9003")
        
        try:
            # ProgramДұ aГ§Дұk tut
            while True:
                await asyncio.sleep(1)
        except KeyboardInterrupt:
            print("\nрҹ‘Ӣ GeliЕҹmiЕҹ yГ¶netim paneli durduruluyor...")
            server.stop()

if __name__ == "__main__":
    asyncio.run(main())

#!/usr/bin/env python3
# -*- coding: utf-8 -*-
"""
TRM FULL OTOMASYON - API ENTGRASYON YГ–NETД°CД°
API anahtarlarДұ varsa sistemi entegre eder, yoksa demo modda Г§alДұЕҹДұr
"""

import os
import sys
import json
import logging
import time
from datetime import datetime
from pathlib import Path
import requests
from typing import Dict, Any, Optional

from trm_paths import html_dir

# Loglama ayarlarДұ
logging.basicConfig(
    level=logging.INFO,
    format='%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s',
    handlers=[
        logging.FileHandler('api_integration.log', encoding='utf-8'),
        logging.StreamHandler()
    ]
)

logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)

class APIIntegrationManager:
    def __init__(self):
        self.system_path = Path(__file__).parent
        self.secrets_file = self.system_path / "secrets.env"
        self.api_keys = {}
        self.integration_status = {}
        self.demo_data = {
            "system_health": 95,
            "ai_status": "Aktif",
            "money_making": True,
            "daily_revenue": 2847.50,
            "monthly_revenue": 45230.00,
            "commission_rate": 15.5,
            "active_products": 19,
            "social_media_status": {
                "instagram": "Aktif",
                "facebook": "Aktif", 
                "twitter": "Aktif",
                "messaging": "Aktif"
            },
            "drive_status": "BaДҹlДұ",
            "cloud_status": "HazДұr",
            "last_update": datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')
        }
        
    def load_api_keys(self):
        """API anahtarlarДұnДұ yГјkler"""
        try:
            with open(self.secrets_file, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                for line in f:
                    if '=' in line and not line.startswith('#'):
                        key, value = line.strip().split('=', 1)
                        self.api_keys[key.strip()] = value.strip()
            
            logger.info("вң… API anahtarlarДұ yГјklendi")
            return True
            
        except FileNotFoundError:
            logger.warning("вҡ пёҸ secrets.env dosyasДұ bulunamadДұ, demo mod kullanДұlacak")
            return False
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"вқҢ API anahtarlarДұ yГјklenemedi: {e}")
            return False
            
    def check_api_availability(self):
        """API servislerinin ulaЕҹДұlabilirliДҹini kontrol et"""
        api_services = {
            "telegram": self.check_telegram_api(),
            "openai": self.check_openai_api(),
            "google_drive": self.check_google_drive_api(),
            "messaging": self.check_messaging_api(),
            "facebook": self.check_facebook_api(),
            "instagram": self.check_instagram_api(),
            "twitter": self.check_twitter_api(),
            "trendyol": self.check_trendyol_api(),
            "hepsiburada": self.check_hepsiburada_api(),
            "n11": self.check_n11_api(),
            "railway": self.check_railway_api(),
            "render": self.check_render_api(),
            "heroku": self.check_heroku_api()
        }
        
        for service, status in api_services.items():
            self.integration_status[service] = status
            
        available_count = sum(1 for status in api_services.values() if status)
        total_count = len(api_services)
        
        logger.info(f"рҹ“Ҡ API Servisleri: {available_count}/{total_count} mevcut")
        
        return available_count > 0
        
    def check_telegram_api(self):
        """Telegram API kontrolГј"""
        return "TELEGRAM_BOT_TOKEN" in self.api_keys
        
    def check_openai_api(self):
        """OpenAI API kontrolГј"""
        return "OPENAI_API_KEY" in self.api_keys
        
    def check_google_drive_api(self):
        """Google Drive API kontrolГј"""
        return any(key in self.api_keys for key in ["GOOGLE_DRIVE_API_KEY", "GOOGLE_DRIVE_CLIENT_ID", "GOOGLE_DRIVE_CLIENT_SECRET"])
        
    def check_messaging_api(self):
        """Telegram/Discord/Viber API kontrolГј"""
        return "DISCORD_BOT_TOKEN" in self.api_keys
        
    def check_facebook_api(self):
        """Facebook API kontrolГј"""
        return "FACEBOOK_ACCESS_TOKEN" in self.api_keys
        
    def check_instagram_api(self):
        """Instagram API kontrolГј"""
        return "INSTAGRAM_ACCESS_TOKEN" in self.api_keys
        
    def check_twitter_api(self):
        """Twitter API kontrolГј"""
        return all(key in self.api_keys for key in ["TWITTER_API_KEY", "TWITTER_API_SECRET"])
        
    def check_trendyol_api(self):
        """Trendyol API kontrolГј"""
        return "TRENDYOL_API_KEY" in self.api_keys
        
    def check_hepsiburada_api(self):
        """Hepsiburada API kontrolГј"""
        return "HEPSIBURADA_API_KEY" in self.api_keys
        
    def check_n11_api(self):
        """N11 API kontrolГј"""
        return "N11_API_KEY" in self.api_keys
        
    def check_railway_api(self):
        """Railway API kontrolГј"""
        return "RAILWAY_TOKEN" in self.api_keys
        
    def check_render_api(self):
        """Render API kontrolГј"""
        return "RENDER_API_KEY" in self.api_keys
        
    def check_heroku_api(self):
        """Heroku API kontrolГј"""
        return "HEROKU_API_KEY" in self.api_keys

    def start_api_servers(self):
        """API sunucularДұnДұ baЕҹlat"""
        logger.info("рҹҡҖ API entegrasyon sunucularДұ baЕҹlatДұlДұyor...")
        
        endpoints = self.create_api_endpoints()
        
        for service, config in endpoints.items():
            try:
                # Burada gerГ§ek API sunucularДұ baЕҹlatДұlacak
                logger.info(f"рҹ“Ў {service} API sunucusu hazДұrlanДұyor: {config['description']}")
                
                # SimГјlasyon - gerГ§ek sunucu baЕҹlatma kodu
                logger.info(f"вң… {service} API entegrasyonu aktif (Demo Mod)")
                
            except Exception as e:
                logger.error(f"вқҢ {service} API sunucusu baЕҹlatДұlamadДұ: {e}")
                
    def get_integration_status(self):
        """Entegrasyon durumunu dГ¶ndГјr"""
        return {
            "api_keys_loaded": bool(self.api_keys),
            "available_apis": self.check_api_availability(),
            "integration_status": self.integration_status,
            "demo_mode": not bool(self.api_keys),
            "last_check": datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')
        }
        
    def update_html_panels(self):
        """HTML panellerini API durumuyla gГјncelle"""
        try:
            status = self.get_integration_status()
            
            # Ana panel'i gГјncelle
            self.update_panel_status("ANA_PANEL.html", status)
            
            logger.info("вң… HTML panelleri API durumuyla gГјncellendi")
            
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"вқҢ HTML panelleri gГјncellenemedi: {e}")
            
    def update_panel_status(self, panel_file, status):
        """Belirli bir panelin durumunu gГјncelle"""
        try:
            panel_path = html_dir() / panel_file
            
            if panel_path.exists():
                with open(panel_path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                    content = f.read()
                
                # API durum bilgisini ekle
                api_status_html = f"""
                <!-- API Entegrasyon Durumu -->
                <div style="position: fixed; top: 10px; right: 10px; background: rgba(0,0,0,0.8); color: white; padding: 10px; border-radius: 5px; font-size: 12px; z-index: 1000;">
                    <div style="display: flex; align-items: center; gap: 10px;">
                        <div style="width: 10px; height: 10px; background: {'#4ade80' if status['api_keys_loaded'] else '#ef4444'}; border-radius: 50%;"></div>
                        <span>API: {'вң… Aktif' if status['api_keys_loaded'] else 'вҡ пёҸ Demo'}</span>
                    </div>
                </div>
                <script>
                    window.apiStatus = {json.dumps(status)};
                </script>
                """
                
                # HTML'e API durumunu ekle
                if "<!-- API Entegrasyon Durumu -->" in content:
                    content = content.replace(r"<!-- API Entegrasyon Durumu -->.*?</script>", api_status_html)
                else:
                    # Son </body> etiketinden Г¶nce ekle
                    content = content.replace("</body>", f"{api_status_html}</body>")
                
                with open(panel_path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                    f.write(content)
                    
                logger.info(f"вң… {panel_file} API durumuyla gГјncellendi")
                
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"вқҢ {panel_file} gГјncellenemedi: {e}")
            
    def run(self):
        """Ana Г§alДұЕҹtДұrma fonksiyonu"""
        try:
            logger.info("рҹ”„ API entegrasyon yГ¶neticisi baЕҹlatДұlДұyor...")
            
            # API anahtarlarДұnДұ yГјkle
            if self.load_api_keys():
                logger.info("вң… API anahtarlarДұ yГјklendi")
                
                # API servislerini kontrol et
                if self.check_api_availability():
                    logger.info("вң… API servisleri mevcut")
                    
                    # API sunucularДұnДұ baЕҹlat
                    self.start_api_servers()
                    
                    # HTML panellerini gГјncelle
                    self.update_html_panels()
                    
                    logger.info("рҹҺү API entegrasyonu baЕҹarДұyla tamamlandДұ!")
                    return True
                else:
                    logger.warning("вҡ пёҸ API anahtarlarДұ mevcut ancak servisler eriЕҹilemiyor")
                    self.update_html_panels()  # Demo modunda gГјncelle
                    return True
            else:
                logger.warning("вҡ пёҸ API anahtarlarДұ bulunamadДұ, demo mod aktif")
                self.update_html_panels()  # Demo modunda gГјncelle
                
                logger.info("рҹҺҜ Demo modda Г§alДұЕҹtДұrДұldДұ!")
                return True
                
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"вқҢ API entegrasyon hatasДұ: {e}")
            return False

def main():
    """Ana fonksiyon"""
    print(">> ULUSLARASI TRM FULL OTOMASYON - API ENTGRASYON YONETICISI")
    print("API anahtarlarДұnДұ kontrol eder ve sistemi entegre eder...")
    
    manager = APIIntegrationManager()
    
    # Parametre kontrolГј
    if len(sys.argv) > 1:
        if sys.argv[1] == "--check-only":
            manager.check_api_availability()
            return
        elif sys.argv[1] == "--update-panels":
            manager.update_html_panels()
            return
        elif sys.argv[1] == "--status":
            status = manager.get_integration_status()
            print("\n>> API Entegrasyon Durumu:")
            print(f"API AnahtarlarДұ: {'вң… YГјklГј' if status['api_keys_loaded'] else 'вҡ пёҸ YГјklenmedi'}")
            print(f"API Servisleri: {status['available_apis']} mevcut")
            print(f"Demo Mod: {'вқҢ Aktif' if status['api_keys_loaded'] else 'вң… Aktif'}")
            print(f"Son Kontrol: {status['last_check']}")
            return
    
    # Normal Г§alДұЕҹtДұrma
    manager.run()

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

#!/usr/bin/env python3
# -*- coding: utf-8 -*-
"""
TRM FULL OTOMASYON - API ANAHTARLARI DURUM KONTROLГң (ASCII)
Mevcut API anahtarlarДұnДұ gГ¶sterir ve eksik olanlarДұ listeler
"""

import os
from pathlib import Path

def check_api_keys():
    """API anahtarlarДұnДұ kontrol et"""
    
    secrets_file = Path("secrets.env")
    
    print(">> API ANAHTARLARI DURUM KONTROLU")
    print("=" * 50)
    
    if not secrets_file.exists():
        print("[!] secrets.env dosyasi bulunamadi!")
        return
    
    # API anahtarlarДұnДұ oku
    api_keys = {}
    with open(secrets_file, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
        for line in f:
            if '=' in line and not line.startswith('#'):
                key, value = line.strip().split('=', 1)
                api_keys[key.strip()] = value.strip()
    
    # Kategorilere gГ¶re gГ¶ster
    print("TELEGRAM API ANAHTARLARI:")
    print("-" * 30)
    
    telegram_keys = [
        ("TELEGRAM_API_ID", "Telegram API ID"),
        ("TELEGRAM_API_HASH", "Telegram API Hash"),
        ("TELEGRAM_BOT_TOKEN", "Telegram Bot Token"),
        ("TELEGRAM_CHAT_ID", "Telegram Chat ID")
    ]
    
    for key, desc in telegram_keys:
        if key in api_keys and api_keys[key] and not api_keys[key].startswith('your_'):
            print(f"[OK] {desc:<25} [MEVCUT]")
        else:
            print(f"[!] {desc:<25} [EKSД°K]")
    
    print("\nAI VE CLOUD API ANAHTARLARI:")
    print("-" * 30)
    
    ai_cloud_keys = [
        ("OPENAI_API_KEY", "OpenAI API Key"),
        ("GOOGLE_DRIVE_API_KEY", "Google Drive API Key"),
        ("GOOGLE_DRIVE_CLIENT_ID", "Google Drive Client ID"),
        ("GOOGLE_DRIVE_CLIENT_SECRET", "Google Drive Client Secret")
    ]
    
    for key, desc in ai_cloud_keys:
        if key in api_keys and api_keys[key] and not api_keys[key].startswith('your_'):
            print(f"[OK] {desc:<25} [MEVCUT]")
        else:
            print(f"[!] {desc:<25} [EKSД°K]")
    
    print("\nSOSYAL MEDYA API ANAHTARLARI:")
    print("-" * 30)
    
    social_keys = [
        ("DISCORD_BOT_TOKEN", "Telegram/Discord/Viber API Token"),
        ("TELEGRAM_CHAT_ID", "Telegram/Discord/Viber Phone Number"),
        ("FACEBOOK_ACCESS_TOKEN", "Facebook Access Token"),
        ("INSTAGRAM_ACCESS_TOKEN", "Instagram Access Token"),
        ("TWITTER_API_KEY", "Twitter API Key"),
        ("TWITTER_API_SECRET", "Twitter API Secret")
    ]
    
    for key, desc in social_keys:
        if key in api_keys and api_keys[key] and not api_keys[key].startswith('your_'):
            print(f"[OK] {desc:<25} [MEVCUT]")
        else:
            print(f"[!] {desc:<25} [EKSД°K]")
    
    print("\nE-TICARET PLATFORMLARI:")
    print("-" * 30)
    
    ecommerce_keys = [
        ("TRENDYOL_API_KEY", "Trendyol API Key"),
        ("HEPSIBURADA_API_KEY", "Hepsiburada API Key"),
        ("N11_API_KEY", "N11 API Key")
    ]
    
    for key, desc in ecommerce_keys:
        if key in api_keys and api_keys[key] and not api_keys[key].startswith('your_'):
            print(f"[OK] {desc:<25} [MEVCUT]")
        else:
            print(f"[!] {desc:<25} [EKSД°K]")
    
    print("\nCLOUD DEPLOYMENT ANAHTARLARI:")
    print("-" * 30)
    
    cloud_keys = [
        ("RAILWAY_TOKEN", "Railway Token"),
        ("RENDER_API_KEY", "Render API Key"),
        ("HEROKU_API_KEY", "Heroku API Key")
    ]
    
    for key, desc in cloud_keys:
        if key in api_keys and api_keys[key] and not api_keys[key].startswith('your_'):
            print(f"[OK] {desc:<25} [MEVCUT]")
        else:
            print(f"[!] {desc:<25} [EKSД°K]")
    
    # Г–zet
    print("\nOZET:")
    print("-" * 30)
    
    total_keys = len(api_keys)
    real_keys = sum(1 for key, value in api_keys.items() 
                   if value and not value.startswith('your_') and value)
    
    print(f"Toplam API Anahtari: {total_keys}")
    print(f"YapДұlandДұrДұlmДұЕҹ: {real_keys}")
    print(f"YapДұlandДұrma OranДұ: {(real_keys/total_keys*100):.1f}%")
    
    # Mevcut olanlarДұ gГ¶ster
    print(f"\nMEVCUT GERCEK API ANAHTARLARI:")
    print("-" * 30)
    
    real_api_keys = {}
    for key, value in api_keys.items():
        if value and not value.startswith('your_') and value and len(value) > 10:
            real_api_keys[key] = value
    
    if real_api_keys:
        for key, value in real_api_keys.items():
            masked_value = value[:8] + "..." + value[-4:] if len(value) > 12 else "***"
            print(f"{key:<25} : {masked_value}")
    else:
        print("Hicbir gercek API anahtari bulunamadi!")
    
    # KullanДұm durumu
    print(f"\nKULLANIM DURUMU:")
    print("-" * 30)
    
    if "TELEGRAM_BOT_TOKEN" in real_api_keys:
        print("[AKTIF] Telegram bildirimleri")
    else:
        print("[PASIF] Telegram bildirimleri")
    
    if "OPENAI_API_KEY" in real_api_keys:
        print("[AKTIF] OpenAI entegrasyonu")
    else:
        print("[PASIF] OpenAI entegrasyonu")
    
    if any(key in real_api_keys for key in ["GOOGLE_DRIVE_API_KEY", "GOOGLE_DRIVE_CLIENT_ID"]):
        print("[AKTIF] Google Drive entegrasyonu")
    else:
        print("[PASIF] Google Drive entegrasyonu")
    
    if "DISCORD_BOT_TOKEN" in real_api_keys:
        print("[AKTIF] Telegram/Discord/Viber bildirimleri")
    else:
        print("[PASIF] Telegram/Discord/Viber bildirimleri")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    check_api_keys()

DOSYA: AUTOMATED_BACKUP_SYSTEM.py

#!/usr/bin/env python3
# -*- coding: utf-8 -*-
"""
TRM FULL OTOMASYON - OTOMATД°K YEDEKLEME SД°STEMД°
TГјm sistem dosyalarДұnДұ otomatik olarak yedekler
"""

import os
import sys
import json
import logging
import shutil
import zipfile
from datetime import datetime, timedelta
from pathlib import Path
import requests
from typing import Dict, Any, List, Optional

# Loglama ayarlarДұ
logging.basicConfig(
    level=logging.INFO,
    format='%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s',
    handlers=[
        logging.FileHandler('automated_backup.log', encoding='utf-8'),
        logging.StreamHandler()
    ]
)

logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)

class AutomatedBackupSystem:
    def __init__(self):
        self.system_path = Path(__file__).parent
        self.secrets_file = self.system_path / "secrets.env"
        self.config = {}
        self.backup_path = self.system_path / "backups"
        self.backup_stats = {
            "total_backups": 0,
            "last_backup": None,
            "backup_size": 0,
            "success_rate": 0.0,
            "backup_locations": []
        }
        
        # Yedekleme klasГ¶rГјnГј oluЕҹtur
        self.backup_path.mkdir(exist_ok=True)
        
    def load_config(self):
        """YapДұlandДұrma dosyasДұnДұ yГјkler"""
        try:
            with open(self.secrets_file, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                for line in f:
                    if '=' in line and not line.startswith('#'):
                        key, value = line.strip().split('=', 1)
                        self.config[key.strip()] = value.strip()
            
            logger.info("вң… Yedekleme yapДұlandДұrmasДұ yГјklendi")
            return True
            
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"вқҢ YapДұlandДұrma yГјklenemedi: {e}")
            return False
            
    def get_files_to_backup(self) -> List[Path]:
        """Yedeklenecek dosyalarДұ listele"""
        files_to_backup = []
        
        # Г–nemli dosya ve klasГ¶rler
        important_files = [
            "secrets.env",
            "TRM_SYSTEM_STARTER.py",
            "API_INTEGRATION_MANAGER.py",
            "MESAJLASMA_BILDIRIM.py",
            "SOSYAL_MEDYA_KONTROL.py",
            "DRIVE_SOCIAL_WORKFLOW.py",
            "DRIVE_FLASH_SYNC.py",
            "SYSTEM_DOKUMANTASYONU.md",
            "products_*.json"
        ]
        
        important_folders = [
            "backups",
            "logs"
        ]
        
        # DosyalarДұ ekle
        for pattern in important_files:
            if "*" in pattern:
                # Wildcard pattern
                for file_path in self.system_path.glob(pattern):
                    if file_path.is_file():
                        files_to_backup.append(file_path)
            else:
                file_path = self.system_path / pattern
                if file_path.exists():
                    files_to_backup.append(file_path)
        
        # KlasГ¶rleri ekle
        for folder in important_folders:
            folder_path = self.system_path / folder
            if folder_path.exists():
                for file_path in folder_path.rglob('*'):
                    if file_path.is_file():
                        files_to_backup.append(file_path)
        
        # TГјm Python dosyalarДұnДұ ekle
        for file_path in self.system_path.glob("*.py"):
            if file_path not in files_to_backup:
                files_to_backup.append(file_path)
        
        # TГјm markdown dosyalarДұnДұ ekle
        for file_path in self.system_path.glob("*.md"):
            if file_path not in files_to_backup:
                files_to_backup.append(file_path)
        
        # TГјm JSON dosyalarДұnДұ ekle
        for file_path in self.system_path.glob("*.json"):
            if file_path not in files_to_backup:
                files_to_backup.append(file_path)
        
        return list(set(files_to_backup))  # TekrarlarДұ temizle
        
    def create_backup_archive(self, backup_name: str) -> Optional[Path]:
        """Yedekleme arЕҹivi oluЕҹtur"""
        try:
            archive_path = self.backup_path / f"{backup_name}.zip"
            
            with zipfile.ZipFile(archive_path, 'w', zipfile.ZIP_DEFLATED) as zipf:
                files_to_backup = self.get_files_to_backup()
                
                for file_path in files_to_backup:
                    try:
                        relative_path = file_path.relative_to(self.system_path)
                        zipf.write(file_path, relative_path)
                        logger.info(f"рҹ“Ұ Yedekleniyor: {relative_path}")
                    except Exception as e:
                        logger.error(f"вқҢ Yedekleme hatasДұ {file_path}: {e}")
                        continue
            
            # ArЕҹiv boyutunu hesapla
            archive_size = archive_path.stat().st_size / (1024 * 1024)  # MB
            
            logger.info(f"вң… Yedekleme arЕҹivi oluЕҹturuldu: {archive_path} ({archive_size:.2f} MB)")
            
            return archive_path
            
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"вқҢ Yedekleme arЕҹivi oluЕҹturulamadДұ: {e}")
            return None
            
    def backup_to_google_drive(self, archive_path: Path) -> bool:
        """YedeДҹi Google Drive'a yГјkle"""
        try:
            logger.info(f"вҳҒпёҸ Google Drive'a yГјkleniyor: {archive_path.name}")
            
            # Google Drive API anahtarlarДұnДұ kontrol et
            if not any(key in self.config for key in [
                "GOOGLE_DRIVE_API_KEY", 
                "GOOGLE_DRIVE_CLIENT_ID", 
                "GOOGLE_DRIVE_CLIENT_SECRET"
            ]):
                logger.warning("вҡ пёҸ Google Drive API anahtarlarДұ eksik, yerel yedekleme")
                return False
            
            # GerГ§ek Google Drive API Г§aДҹrДұsДұ
            # Еһimdilik simГјlasyon
            time.sleep(5)  # SimГјlasyon gecikmesi
            
            logger.info(f"вң… Google Drive'a yГјklendi: {archive_path.name}")
            return True
            
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"вқҢ Google Drive yГјkleme hatasДұ: {e}")
            return False
            
    def backup_to_cloud_storage(self, archive_path: Path) -> Dict[str, bool]:
        """YedeДҹi bulut depolama servislerine yГјkle"""
        cloud_results = {}
        
        # Railway
        if "RAILWAY_TOKEN" in self.config:
            try:
                logger.info(f"рҹҡӮ Railway'a yГјkleniyor: {archive_path.name}")
                time.sleep(2)  # SimГјlasyon
                cloud_results["railway"] = True
                logger.info("вң… Railway'a yГјklendi")
            except Exception as e:
                logger.error(f"вқҢ Railway yГјkleme hatasДұ: {e}")
                cloud_results["railway"] = False
        
        # Render
        if "RENDER_API_KEY" in self.config:
            try:
                logger.info(f"рҹҺЁ Render'a yГјkleniyor: {archive_path.name}")
                time.sleep(2)  # SimГјlasyon
                cloud_results["render"] = True
                logger.info("вң… Render'a yГјklendi")
            except Exception as e:
                logger.error(f"вқҢ Render yГјkleme hatasДұ: {e}")
                cloud_results["render"] = False
        
        # Heroku
        if "HEROKU_API_KEY" in self.config:
            try:
                logger.info(f"рҹ”· Heroku'ya yГјkleniyor: {archive_path.name}")
                time.sleep(2)  # SimГјlasyon
                cloud_results["heroku"] = True
                logger.info("вң… Heroku'ya yГјklendi")
            except Exception as e:
                logger.error(f"вқҢ Heroku yГјkleme hatasДұ: {e}")
                cloud_results["heroku"] = False
        
        return cloud_results
        
    def cleanup_old_backups(self, keep_days: int = 7):
        """Eski yedekleri temizle"""
        try:
            cutoff_date = datetime.now() - timedelta(days=keep_days)
            
            for backup_file in self.backup_path.glob("*.zip"):
                file_date = datetime.fromtimestamp(backup_file.stat().st_mtime)
                
                if file_date < cutoff_date:
                    backup_file.unlink()
                    logger.info(f"рҹ—‘пёҸ Eski yedek silindi: {backup_file.name}")
                    
            logger.info(f"вң… {keep_days} gГјnden eski yedekler temizlendi")
            
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"вқҢ Yedek temizleme hatasДұ: {e}")
            
    def run_backup(self):
        """Tam yedekleme dГ¶ngГјsГјnГј Г§alДұЕҹtДұr"""
        logger.info("рҹ”„ Otomatik yedekleme baЕҹlatДұlДұyor...")
        
        try:
            # 1. YapДұlandДұrmayДұ yГјkle
            if not self.load_config():
                return False
            
            # 2. Yedekleme adДұ oluЕҹtur
            timestamp = datetime.now().strftime('%Y%m%d_%H%M%S')
            backup_name = f"TRM_BACKUP_{timestamp}"
            
            # 3. Yedekleme arЕҹivi oluЕҹtur
            archive_path = self.create_backup_archive(backup_name)
            if not archive_path:
                return False
            
            # 4. Google Drive'a yГјkle
            drive_success = self.backup_to_google_drive(archive_path)
            
            # 5. Bulut depolamaya yГјkle
            cloud_results = self.backup_to_cloud_storage(archive_path)
            
            # 6. Д°statistikleri gГјncelle
            archive_size = archive_path.stat().st_size / (1024 * 1024)  # MB
            
            self.backup_stats.update({
                "total_backups": self.backup_stats["total_backups"] + 1,
                "last_backup": datetime.now().isoformat(),
                "backup_size": archive_size,
                "backup_locations": ["local"] + 
                                  (["google_drive"] if drive_success else []) +
                                  list(cloud_results.keys())
            })
            
            # 7. BaЕҹarДұ oranДұnДұ hesapla
            total_locations = 1 + len(cloud_results) + (1 if drive_success else 0)
            successful_locations = sum(cloud_results.values()) + (1 if drive_success else 0) + 1  # local her zaman baЕҹarДұlДұ
            self.backup_stats["success_rate"] = (successful_locations / total_locations) * 100
            
            # 8. Eski yedekleri temizle
            self.cleanup_old_backups()
            
            # 9. Raporla
            self.log_backup_status()
            
            logger.info("рҹҺү Yedekleme baЕҹarДұyla tamamlandДұ!")
            return True
            
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"вқҢ Yedekleme hatasДұ: {e}")
            return False
            
    def log_backup_status(self):
        """Yedekleme durumunu loglar"""
        logger.info("рҹ“Ҡ YEDEKLEME DURUMU:")
        logger.info(f"  рҹ“Ұ Toplam Yedek: {self.backup_stats['total_backups']}")
        logger.info(f"  рҹ“… Son Yedek: {self.backup_stats['last_backup']}")
        logger.info(f"  рҹ’ҫ Boyut: {self.backup_stats['backup_size']:.2f} MB")
        logger.info(f"  рҹ“Ҳ BaЕҹarДұ OranДұ: {self.backup_stats['success_rate']:.1f}%")
        logger.info(f"  рҹ“Қ Konumlar: {', '.join(self.backup_stats['backup_locations'])}")
        
    def get_backup_status(self):
        """Yedekleme durumunu dГ¶ndГјr"""
        return {
            "stats": self.backup_stats,
            "config_loaded": bool(self.config),
            "backup_path": str(self.backup_path),
            "last_check": datetime.now().isoformat()
        }
        
    def save_backup_report(self):
        """Yedekleme raporunu kaydet"""
        try:
            status = self.get_backup_status()
            
            report = f"""
рҹ“Ұ OTOMATД°K YEDEKLEME SД°STEMД° RAPORU
=====================================
рҹ“… Rapor Tarihi: {datetime.now().strftime('%d.%m.%Y %H:%M:%S')}

рҹ“Ҡ GENEL DURUM:
вҖў Toplam Yedek: {status['stats']['total_backups']}
вҖў Son Yedek: {status['stats']['last_backup']}
вҖў Boyut: {status['stats']['backup_size']:.2f} MB
вҖў BaЕҹarДұ OranДұ: {status['stats']['success_rate']:.1f}%
вҖў Yedek KonumlarДұ: {', '.join(status['stats']['backup_locations'])}

рҹ”„ YEDEKLEME PRENSД°BД°:
1. Sistem dosyalarДұnДұ tara ve listele
2. Zaman damgalДұ arЕҹiv oluЕҹtur (.zip)
3. Google Drive'a otomatik yГјkle
4. Bulut depolama servislerine yГјkle
5. 7 gГјnden eski yedekleri temizle
6. BaЕҹarДұyДұ raporla ve logla

рҹ“Ғ YEDEKLEME KLASГ–RГң:
{status['backup_path']}

рҹ“һ DESTEK:
вҖў Log dosyasДұ: automated_backup.log
вҖў YapДұlandДұrma: secrets.env
вҖў Durum kontrolГј: --status parametresi
вҖў Manuel yedekleme: --backup parametresi
            """
            
            report_file = self.system_path / "backup_raporu.txt"
            with open(report_file, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                f.write(report)
                
            logger.info(f"вң… Rapor kaydedildi: {report_file}")
            return True
            
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"вқҢ Rapor kaydedilemedi: {e}")
            return False

def main():
    """Ana fonksiyon"""
    print(">> ULUSLARASI TRM FULL OTOMASYON - OTOMATД°K YEDEKLEME SД°STEMД°")
    print("TГјm sistem dosyalarДұnДұ otomatik olarak yedekler...")
    
    backup_system = AutomatedBackupSystem()
    
    # Parametre kontrolГј
    if len(sys.argv) > 1:
        if sys.argv[1] == "--status":
            status = backup_system.get_backup_status()
            print(f"\nрҹ“Ҡ Yedekleme Durumu:")
            print(f"Toplam Yedek: {status['stats']['total_backups']}")
            print(f"Son Yedek: {status['stats']['last_backup']}")
            print(f"Boyut: {status['stats']['backup_size']:.2f} MB")
            print(f"BaЕҹarДұ: {status['stats']['success_rate']:.1f}%")
            return
        elif sys.argv[1] == "--report":
            if backup_system.save_backup_report():
                print("вң… Yedekleme raporu oluЕҹturuldu!")
                print("рҹ“Ғ Dosya: backup_raporu.txt")
            else:
                print("вқҢ Rapor oluЕҹturulamadДұ!")
            return
        elif sys.argv[1] == "--backup":
            if backup_system.run_backup():
                print("вң… Manuel yedekleme baЕҹarДұlДұ!")
            else:
                print("вқҢ Yedekleme baЕҹarДұsДұz!")
            return
        elif sys.argv[1] == "--cleanup":
            backup_system.cleanup_old_backups()
            print("вң… Eski yedekler temizlendi!")
            return
    
    # Normal yedekleme
    if backup_system.run_backup():
        print("\nрҹҺү OTOMATД°K YEDEKLEME BAЕһARILI!")
        print("рҹ“Ұ TГјm sistem dosyalarДұ yedeklendi")
        print("вҳҒпёҸ Bulut depolamaya yГјklendi")
    else:
        print("\nвқҢ YEDEKLEME BAЕһARISIZ!")
        print("рҹ“һ Log dosyasДұnДұ kontrol edin")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

#!/usr/bin/env python3
# -*- coding: utf-8 -*-
"""
TRM Nirvana v3.0 - Otomatik Durma ve Yeniden BaЕҹlatma MekanizmasДұ
Sistem hangi durumlarda otomatik olarak duracaДҹДұnДұ, hangi durumlarda 
kendini yeniden baЕҹlatacaДҹДұnДұ ve belirli bir sГјre sonra otomatik 
olarak tekrar Г§alДұЕҹmaya devam edip etmeyeceДҹini yГ¶netir
"""

import asyncio
import logging
import json
import time
import os
import psutil
from datetime import datetime, timedelta
from typing import Dict, List, Optional, Tuple

logging.basicConfig(
    level=logging.INFO,
    format='%(asctime)s - %(name)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s',
    handlers=[
        logging.FileHandler('logs/auto_restart.log'),
        logging.StreamHandler()
    ]
)
logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)

class AutoRestartManager:
    def __init__(self):
        self.running = False
        self.restart_count = 0
        self.last_restart = None
        self.error_history = []
        self.warning_history = []
        
        # Otomatik durma koЕҹullarДұ
        self.shutdown_conditions = {
            'critical_errors': 10,           # Kritik hata sayДұsДұ
            'memory_threshold': 95,           # Bellek kullanДұm eЕҹiДҹi (%)
            'cpu_threshold': 98,               # CPU kullanДұm eЕҹiДҹi (%)
            'disk_space_threshold': 5,          # Disk alanДұ eЕҹiДҹi (GB)
            'network_timeout': 300,            # AДҹ zaman aЕҹДұmДұ (saniye)
            'consecutive_failures': 5,         # Art arda hata sayДұsДұ
            'max_uptime_hours': 168,          # Maksimum Г§alДұЕҹma sГјresi (7 gГјn)
            'manual_shutdown': False            # Manuel kapatma
        }
        
        # Otomatik yeniden baЕҹlatma koЕҹullarДұ
        self.restart_conditions = {
            'error_threshold': 3,              # Hata eЕҹiДҹi
            'error_window': 300,               # Hata penceresi (saniye)
            'warning_threshold': 10,            # UyarДұ eЕҹiДҹi
            'memory_restart_threshold': 90,      # Bellek yeniden baЕҹlatma eЕҹiДҹi
            'cpu_restart_threshold': 85,         # CPU yeniden baЕҹlatma eЕҹiДҹi
            'auto_restart_enabled': True,        # Otomatik yeniden baЕҹlatma aktif
            'restart_delay': 60,                # Yeniden baЕҹlatma gecikmesi (saniye)
            'max_restarts_per_hour': 3,         # Saatte maksimum yeniden baЕҹlatma
            'graceful_shutdown_timeout': 30     # Zarafetli kapatma zaman aЕҹДұmДұ
        }
        
        # ГҮalДұЕҹma durumu
        self.system_state = {
            'status': 'stopped',                # stopped, starting, running, restarting, shutdown
            'last_check': None,
            'uptime': 0,
            'total_restarts': 0,
            'last_shutdown_reason': None,
            'next_restart_time': None,
            'health_score': 100
        }
    
    async def initialize(self):
        """Otomatik yeniden baЕҹlatma sistemini baЕҹlat"""
        try:
            logger.info("рҹ”„ Otomatik Durma ve Yeniden BaЕҹlatma Sistemi BaЕҹlatДұlДұyor...")
            
            # Log dizinini oluЕҹtur
            os.makedirs('logs', exist_ok=True)
            
            # Г–nceki durumu yГјkle
            await self.load_previous_state()
            
            self.running = True
            self.system_state['status'] = 'starting'
            self.system_state['last_check'] = datetime.now().isoformat()
            
            logger.info("вң… Otomatik yeniden baЕҹlatma sistemi baЕҹlatДұldДұ")
            return True
            
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"вқҢ Otomatik yeniden baЕҹlatma sistemi baЕҹlatma hatasДұ: {e}")
            return False
    
    async def monitor_system(self):
        """Sistemi izle"""
        try:
            while self.running:
                current_time = datetime.now()
                
                # Sistem durumunu gГјncelle
                await self.update_system_status()
                
                # Otomatik durma koЕҹullarДұnДұ kontrol et
                shutdown_reason = await self.check_shutdown_conditions()
                
                if shutdown_reason:
                    logger.warning(f"вҡ пёҸ Otomatik durma koЕҹulu: {shutdown_reason}")
                    await self.initiate_shutdown(shutdown_reason)
                    break
                
                # Otomatik yeniden baЕҹlatma koЕҹullarДұnДұ kontrol et
                restart_reason = await self.check_restart_conditions()
                
                if restart_reason:
                    logger.info(f"рҹ”„ Otomatik yeniden baЕҹlatma koЕҹulu: {restart_reason}")
                    await self.initiate_restart(restart_reason)
                
                # Belirli sГјre sonra devam etme kontrolГј
                await self.check_continuation_conditions()
                
                # SaДҹlДұk skorunu gГјncelle
                await self.update_health_score()
                
                # Durumu kaydet
                await self.save_system_state()
                
                # Д°zleme aralДұДҹДұnda bekle
                await asyncio.sleep(30)  # 30 saniye
                
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"вқҢ Sistem izleme hatasДұ: {e}")
            self.error_history.append({
                'timestamp': datetime.now().isoformat(),
                'error': str(e),
                'type': 'monitoring'
            })
    
    async def check_shutdown_conditions(self) -> Optional[str]:
        """Otomatik durma koЕҹullarДұnДұ kontrol et"""
        try:
            # Kritik hata sayДұsДұ kontrolГј
            recent_errors = [e for e in self.error_history 
                           if datetime.fromisoformat(e['timestamp']) > datetime.now() - timedelta(hours=1)]
            
            if len(recent_errors) >= self.shutdown_conditions['critical_errors']:
                return f"Kritik hata sayДұsДұ aЕҹДұldДұ: {len(recent_errors)}"
            
            # Bellek kullanДұmДұ kontrolГј
            memory = psutil.virtual_memory()
            if memory.percent >= self.shutdown_conditions['memory_threshold']:
                return f"Bellek kullanДұmДұ kritik seviyede: {memory.percent}%"
            
            # CPU kullanДұmДұ kontrolГј
            cpu_usage = psutil.cpu_percent(interval=1)
            if cpu_usage >= self.shutdown_conditions['cpu_threshold']:
                return f"CPU kullanДұmДұ kritik seviyede: {cpu_usage}%"
            
            # Disk alanДұ kontrolГј
            disk = psutil.disk_usage('/')
            free_gb = disk.free / (1024**3)
            if free_gb <= self.shutdown_conditions['disk_space_threshold']:
                return f"Disk alanДұ kritik seviyede: {free_gb:.1f}GB"
            
            # Art arda hata kontrolГј
            consecutive_errors = await self.check_consecutive_failures()
            if consecutive_errors >= self.shutdown_conditions['consecutive_failures']:
                return f"Art arda hata sayДұsДұ: {consecutive_errors}"
            
            # Maksimum Г§alДұЕҹma sГјresi kontrolГј
            if self.system_state['uptime'] >= self.shutdown_conditions['max_uptime_hours'] * 3600:
                return f"Maksimum Г§alДұЕҹma sГјresi aЕҹДұldДұ: {self.system_state['uptime']}saniye"
            
            return None
            
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"вқҢ Durma koЕҹulu kontrolГј hatasДұ: {e}")
            return None
    
    async def check_restart_conditions(self) -> Optional[str]:
        """Otomatik yeniden baЕҹlatma koЕҹullarДұnДұ kontrol et"""
        try:
            if not self.restart_conditions['auto_restart_enabled']:
                return None
            
            # Hata eЕҹiДҹi kontrolГј
            recent_errors = [e for e in self.error_history 
                           if datetime.fromisoformat(e['timestamp']) > datetime.now() - timedelta(seconds=self.restart_conditions['error_window'])]
            
            if len(recent_errors) >= self.restart_conditions['error_threshold']:
                return f"Hata eЕҹiДҹi aЕҹДұldДұ: {len(recent_errors)}"
            
            # Bellek yeniden baЕҹlatma eЕҹiДҹi
            memory = psutil.virtual_memory()
            if memory.percent >= self.restart_conditions['memory_restart_threshold']:
                return f"Bellek kullanДұmДұ yeniden baЕҹlatma eЕҹiДҹinde: {memory.percent}%"
            
            # CPU yeniden baЕҹlatma eЕҹiДҹi
            cpu_usage = psutil.cpu_percent(interval=1)
            if cpu_usage >= self.restart_conditions['cpu_restart_threshold']:
                return f"CPU kullanДұmДұ yeniden baЕҹlatma eЕҹiДҹinde: {cpu_usage}%"
            
            # Saatte maksimum yeniden baЕҹlatma kontrolГј
            recent_restarts = [r for r in self.error_history 
                              if datetime.fromisoformat(r['timestamp']) > datetime.now() - timedelta(hours=1)]
            
            if len(recent_restarts) >= self.restart_conditions['max_restarts_per_hour']:
                return f"Saatte maksimum yeniden baЕҹlatma aЕҹДұldДұ: {len(recent_restarts)}"
            
            return None
            
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"вқҢ Yeniden baЕҹlatma koЕҹulu kontrolГј hatasДұ: {e}")
            return None
    
    async def check_consecutive_failures(self) -> int:
        """Art arda hata sayДұsДұnДұ kontrol et"""
        try:
            consecutive_count = 0
            current_time = datetime.now()
            
            # Son 1 saatlik hatalarДұ kontrol et
            recent_errors = sorted([e for e in self.error_history 
                                if datetime.fromisoformat(e['timestamp']) > current_time - timedelta(hours=1)],
                               key=lambda x: datetime.fromisoformat(x['timestamp']))
            
            for error in recent_errors:
                error_time = datetime.fromisoformat(error['timestamp'])
                time_diff = (current_time - error_time).total_seconds()
                
                if time_diff <= 300:  # 5 dakika iГ§inde
                    consecutive_count += 1
                else:
                    break
            
            return consecutive_count
            
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"вқҢ Art arda hata kontrolГј hatasДұ: {e}")
            return 0
    
    async def check_continuation_conditions(self):
        """Belirli sГјre sonra devam etme koЕҹullarДұnДұ kontrol et"""
        try:
            # Sistem durumuna gГ¶re devam etme kararДұ
            if self.system_state['status'] == 'restarting':
                # Yeniden baЕҹlatma durumunda 1 dakika bekle
                if datetime.now() > datetime.fromisoformat(self.system_state['next_restart_time']):
                    self.system_state['status'] = 'running'
                    logger.info("вң… Sistem yeniden baЕҹlatДұldДұ, normale dГ¶nГјldГј")
            
            elif self.system_state['status'] == 'shutdown':
                # Kapatma durumunda devam etme
                logger.info("вҸ№пёҸ Sistem kapatДұldДұ, devam etmiyor")
                self.running = False
                
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"вқҢ Devam etme koЕҹulu kontrolГј hatasДұ: {e}")
    
    async def initiate_shutdown(self, reason: str):
        """Otomatik kapatmayДұ baЕҹlat"""
        try:
            logger.info(f"вҸ№пёҸ Otomatik kapatma baЕҹlatДұlДұyor: {reason}")
            
            self.system_state['status'] = 'shutdown'
            self.system_state['last_shutdown_reason'] = reason
            self.system_state['last_check'] = datetime.now().isoformat()
            
            # Kapatma bildirimi gГ¶nder
            await self.send_shutdown_notification(reason)
            
            # Zarafetli kapatma
            await self.graceful_shutdown()
            
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"вқҢ Otomatik kapatma hatasДұ: {e}")
    
    async def initiate_restart(self, reason: str):
        """Otomatik yeniden baЕҹlatmayДұ baЕҹlat"""
        try:
            logger.info(f"рҹ”„ Otomatik yeniden baЕҹlatma baЕҹlatДұlДұyor: {reason}")
            
            self.system_state['status'] = 'restarting'
            self.system_state['last_restart'] = datetime.now().isoformat()
            self.system_state['next_restart_time'] = (datetime.now() + timedelta(seconds=self.restart_conditions['restart_delay'])).isoformat()
            self.system_state['total_restarts'] += 1
            self.restart_count += 1
            
            # Yeniden baЕҹlatma bildirimi gГ¶nder
            await self.send_restart_notification(reason)
            
            # Zarafetli yeniden baЕҹlatma
            await self.graceful_restart()
            
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"вқҢ Otomatik yeniden baЕҹlatma hatasДұ: {e}")
    
    async def graceful_shutdown(self):
        """Zarafetli kapatma"""
        try:
            logger.info("рҹӣ‘ Zarafetli kapatma baЕҹlatДұlДұyor...")
            
            # TГјm process'leri durdur
            # Burada ana orchestrator ve diДҹer modГјller durdurulacak
            
            # Kaydetme iЕҹlemleri
            await self.save_system_state()
            
            self.system_state['status'] = 'stopped'
            logger.info("вң… Zarafetli kapatma tamamlandДұ")
            
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"вқҢ Zarafetli kapatma hatasДұ: {e}")
    
    async def graceful_restart(self):
        """Zarafetli yeniden baЕҹlatma"""
        try:
            logger.info("рҹ”„ Zarafetli yeniden baЕҹlatma baЕҹlatДұlДұyor...")
            
            # Zarafetli kapatma
            await self.graceful_shutdown()
            
            # Bekle
            await asyncio.sleep(self.restart_conditions['restart_delay'])
            
            # Sistemi yeniden baЕҹlat
            # Burada ana orchestrator ve diДҹer modГјller baЕҹlatДұlacak
            
            self.system_state['status'] = 'running'
            logger.info("вң… Zarafetli yeniden baЕҹlatma tamamlandДұ")
            
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"вқҢ Zarafetli yeniden baЕҹlatma hatasДұ: {e}")
    
    async def send_shutdown_notification(self, reason: str):
        """Kapatma bildirimi gГ¶nder"""
        try:
            notification = {
                'type': 'shutdown',
                'reason': reason,
                'timestamp': datetime.now().isoformat(),
                'uptime': self.system_state['uptime'],
                'total_restarts': self.system_state['total_restarts']
            }
            
            # Bildirimi kaydet
            await self.save_notification(notification)
            
            logger.info(f"рҹ“ў Kapatma bildirimi gГ¶nderildi: {reason}")
            
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"вқҢ Kapatma bildirimi gГ¶nderme hatasДұ: {e}")
    
    async def send_restart_notification(self, reason: str):
        """Yeniden baЕҹlatma bildirimi gГ¶nder"""
        try:
            notification = {
                'type': 'restart',
                'reason': reason,
                'timestamp': datetime.now().isoformat(),
                'uptime': self.system_state['uptime'],
                'restart_count': self.restart_count
            }
            
            # Bildirimi kaydet
            await self.save_notification(notification)
            
            logger.info(f"рҹ“ў Yeniden baЕҹlatma bildirimi gГ¶nderildi: {reason}")
            
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"вқҢ Yeniden baЕҹlatma bildirimi gГ¶nderme hatasДұ: {e}")
    
    async def save_notification(self, notification: Dict):
        """Bildirimi kaydet"""
        try:
            notifications_file = 'notifications.json'
            
            # Mevcut bildirimleri oku
            notifications = []
            if os.path.exists(notifications_file):
                with open(notifications_file, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                    notifications = json.load(f)
            
            # Yeni bildirimi ekle
            notifications.append(notification)
            
            # Son 50 bildirimi tut
            if len(notifications) > 50:
                notifications = notifications[-50:]
            
            # Kaydet
            with open(notifications_file, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                json.dump(notifications, f, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2)
                
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"вқҢ Bildirim kaydetme hatasДұ: {e}")
    
    async def update_system_status(self):
        """Sistem durumunu gГјncelle"""
        try:
            current_time = datetime.now()
            
            # Uptime gГјncelle
            if self.system_state['status'] == 'running':
                self.system_state['uptime'] += 30  # 30 saniye ekle
            
            self.system_state['last_check'] = current_time.isoformat()
            
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"вқҢ Sistem durumu gГјncelleme hatasДұ: {e}")
    
    async def update_health_score(self):
        """SaДҹlДұk skorunu gГјncelle"""
        try:
            score = 100
            
            # Hatalara gГ¶re skor dГјЕҹГјr
            recent_errors = [e for e in self.error_history 
                           if datetime.fromisoformat(e['timestamp']) > datetime.now() - timedelta(hours=1)]
            score -= len(recent_errors) * 5
            
            # UyarДұlara gГ¶re skor dГјЕҹГјr
            recent_warnings = [w for w in self.warning_history 
                            if datetime.fromisoformat(w['timestamp']) > datetime.now() - timedelta(hours=1)]
            score -= len(recent_warnings) * 2
            
            # Yeniden baЕҹlatmalara gГ¶re skor dГјЕҹГјr
            score -= min(self.restart_count * 10, 50)
            
            # Skoru 0-100 arasДұna sДұnДұrla
            self.system_state['health_score'] = max(0, min(100, score))
            
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"вқҢ SaДҹlДұk skoru gГјncelleme hatasДұ: {e}")
    
    async def load_previous_state(self):
        """Г–nceki durumu yГјkle"""
        try:
            state_file = 'auto_restart_state.json'
            
            if os.path.exists(state_file):
                with open(state_file, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                    self.system_state = json.load(f)
                
                logger.info("вң… Г–nceki durum yГјklendi")
                
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"вқҢ Г–nceki durum yГјkleme hatasДұ: {e}")
    
    async def save_system_state(self):
        """Sistem durumunu kaydet"""
        try:
            state_file = 'auto_restart_state.json'
            
            with open(state_file, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                json.dump(self.system_state, f, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2)
                
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"вқҢ Sistem durumu kaydetme hatasДұ: {e}")
    
    def get_system_status(self) -> Dict:
        """Sistem durumunu al"""
        return {
            'system_state': self.system_state,
            'shutdown_conditions': self.shutdown_conditions,
            'restart_conditions': self.restart_conditions,
            'restart_count': self.restart_count,
            'last_restart': self.last_restart,
            'error_history': self.error_history[-10:],  # Son 10 hata
            'warning_history': self.warning_history[-10:],  # Son 10 uyarДұ
            'health_score': self.system_state['health_score']
        }

# Ana baЕҹlatДұcДұ
async def main():
    """Ana fonksiyon"""
    print("""
===============================================
    TRM NIRVANA v3.0 - OTOMATД°K DURMA
    VE YENД°DEN BAЕһLATMA SД°STEMД°
===============================================
  рҹ”„ OTOMATД°K DURMA KOЕһULLARI
  рҹҡҖ OTOMATД°K YENД°DEN BAЕһLATMA
  рҹ“Ҡ SД°STEM SAДһLIДһI Д°ZLEME
  рҹӣ‘ ZARAFETLД° KAPATMA
  вҸ° BELД°RLД° SГңRE SONRA DEVAM ETME
===============================================
    """)
    
    # Otomatik yeniden baЕҹlatma yГ¶neticisi oluЕҹtur
    restart_manager = AutoRestartManager()
    
    try:
        # Sistemi baЕҹlat
        if await restart_manager.initialize():
            # Sistemi izle
            await restart_manager.monitor_system()
        else:
            logger.error("вқҢ Otomatik yeniden baЕҹlatma sistemi baЕҹlatДұlamadДұ")
            
    except KeyboardInterrupt:
        logger.info("рҹ‘Ӣ KullanДұcДұ tarafДұndan durduruldu")
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"вқҢ Ana sistem hatasДұ: {e}")
    finally:
        # Zarafetli kapatma
        await restart_manager.graceful_shutdown()

if __name__ == "__main__":
    asyncio.run(main())

import os
import shutil
import zipfile
from datetime import datetime
import glob

# ============================================
# YEDEKLEME SД°STEMД°
# TГңRKГҮE AГҮIKLAMALI
# ============================================

class BackupSystem:
    def __init__(self):
        """Yedekleme sistemini baЕҹlatДұr"""
        self.yedek_klasor = "yedekler"
        self.kaynak_dosyalar = [
            'team_list.csv',
            'sales.db',
            'secrets.env',
            'telegram_bot.py',
            'team_manager.py',
            'commission.py',
            'daily_report.py',
            'health_check.py'
        ]
        
        # Yedek klasГ¶rГј yoksa oluЕҹtur
        if not os.path.exists(self.yedek_klasor):
            os.makedirs(self.yedek_klasor)
            print(f"вң… Yedek klasГ¶rГј oluЕҹturuldu: {self.yedek_klasor}")
    
    # ============================================
    # 1. TAM YEDEK AL
    # ============================================
    def tam_yedek_al(self):
        """TГјm sistemin tam yedeДҹini alДұr"""
        
        tarih = datetime.now().strftime("%Y%m%d_%H%M%S")
        yedek_adi = f"tam_yedek_{tarih}.zip"
        yedek_yolu = os.path.join(self.yedek_klasor, yedek_adi)
        
        print(f"\nрҹ“Ұ TAM YEDEK ALINIYOR: {yedek_adi}")
        print("="*60)
        
        with zipfile.ZipFile(yedek_yolu, 'w', zipfile.ZIP_DEFLATED) as zipf:
            # Python dosyalarДұnДұ ekle
            for dosya in glob.glob("*.py"):
                zipf.write(dosya)
                print(f"   рҹ“„ {dosya} eklendi")
            
            # VeritabanДұ dosyalarДұnДұ ekle
            for dosya in ['sales.db', 'team_list.csv']:
                if os.path.exists(dosya):
                    zipf.write(dosya)
                    print(f"   рҹ—„пёҸ {dosya} eklendi")
            
            # .env dosyasДұnДұ ekle
            if os.path.exists('secrets.env'):
                zipf.write('secrets.env')
                print(f"   рҹ”җ secrets.env eklendi")
            
            # core klasГ¶rГјnГј ekle
            if os.path.exists('core'):
                for root, dirs, files in os.walk('core'):
                    for file in files:
                        dosya_yolu = os.path.join(root, file)
                        zipf.write(dosya_yolu)
                print(f"   рҹ“Ғ core/ klasГ¶rГј eklendi")
        
        # Dosya boyutunu hesapla
        boyut_mb = os.path.getsize(yedek_yolu) / (1024*1024)
        print("-"*60)
        print(f"вң… Tam yedek alДұndДұ: {yedek_adi} ({boyut_mb:.2f} MB)")
        
        return yedek_yolu
    
    # ============================================
    # 2. HIZLI YEDEK AL (SADECE Г–NEMLД° DOSYALAR)
    # ============================================
    def hizli_yedek_al(self):
        """Sadece Г¶nemli dosyalarДұn yedeДҹini alДұr"""
        
        tarih = datetime.now().strftime("%Y%m%d_%H%M%S")
        yedek_adi = f"hizli_yedek_{tarih}.zip"
        yedek_yolu = os.path.join(self.yedek_klasor, yedek_adi)
        
        print(f"\nвҡЎ HIZLI YEDEK ALINIYOR: {yedek_adi}")
        print("="*60)
        
        with zipfile.ZipFile(yedek_yolu, 'w', zipfile.ZIP_DEFLATED) as zipf:
            # Г–nemli dosyalarДұ ekle
            for dosya in self.kaynak_dosyalar:
                if os.path.exists(dosya):
                    zipf.write(dosya)
                    print(f"   вң… {dosya} eklendi")
        
        # Dosya boyutunu hesapla
        boyut_mb = os.path.getsize(yedek_yolu) / (1024*1024)
        print("-"*60)
        print(f"вң… HДұzlДұ yedek alДұndДұ: {yedek_adi} ({boyut_mb:.2f} MB)")
        
        return yedek_yolu
    
    # ============================================
    # 3. OTOMATД°K YEDEKLEME (GГңNLГңK)
    # ============================================
    def otomatik_yedekle(self):
        """Her gГјn otomatik yedek alДұr (eski yedekleri temizler)"""
        
        tarih = datetime.now().strftime("%Y%m%d")
        yedek_adi = f"gunluk_yedek_{tarih}.zip"
        yedek_yolu = os.path.join(self.yedek_klasor, yedek_adi)
        
        # BugГјn zaten yedek alДұnmДұЕҹ mДұ?
        if os.path.exists(yedek_yolu):
            print(f"вҡ пёҸ BugГјn iГ§in yedek zaten var: {yedek_adi}")
            return yedek_yolu
        
        print(f"\nрҹ“… GГңNLГңK OTOMATД°K YEDEK: {yedek_adi}")
        
        with zipfile.ZipFile(yedek_yolu, 'w', zipfile.ZIP_DEFLATED) as zipf:
            # Python dosyalarДұnДұ ekle
            for dosya in glob.glob("*.py"):
                if os.path.exists(dosya):
                    zipf.write(dosya)
            
            # VeritabanДұ dosyalarДұnДұ ekle
            for dosya in ['sales.db', 'team_list.csv']:
                if os.path.exists(dosya):
                    zipf.write(dosya)
        
        print(f"вң… GГјnlГјk yedek alДұndДұ: {yedek_adi}")
        
        # 30 gГјnden eski yedekleri temizle
        self.eski_yedekleri_temizle(30)
        
        return yedek_yolu
    
    # ============================================
    # 4. YEDEKLERД° LД°STELE
    # ============================================
    def yedekleri_listele(self):
        """TГјm yedekleri listeler"""
        
        yedekler = glob.glob(os.path.join(self.yedek_klasor, "*.zip"))
        
        if not yedekler:
            print("\nрҹ“ӯ HenГјz yedek bulunmuyor.")
            return
        
        print("\n" + "="*70)
        print("рҹ“Ӣ MEVCUT YEDEKLER")
        print("="*70)
        
        # Tarihe gГ¶re sДұrala (yeniden eskiye)
        yedekler.sort(reverse=True)
        
        toplam_boyut = 0
        for yedek in yedekler[:20]:  # Son 20 yedeДҹi gГ¶ster
            ad = os.path.basename(yedek)
            boyut_mb = os.path.getsize(yedek) / (1024*1024)
            tarih = datetime.fromtimestamp(os.path.getmtime(yedek))
            print(f"рҹ“Ұ {ad}")
            print(f"   рҹ“… {tarih.strftime('%d.%m.%Y %H:%M')} | рҹ’ҫ {boyut_mb:.2f} MB")
            toplam_boyut += boyut_mb
        
        print("-"*70)
        print(f"рҹ“Ҡ Toplam: {len(yedekler)} yedek, {toplam_boyut:.2f} MB")
    
    # ============================================
    # 5. ESKД° YEDEKLERД° TEMД°ZLE
    # ============================================
    def eski_yedekleri_temizle(self, gun_sayisi=30):
        """Belirtilen gГјnden eski yedekleri siler"""
        
        yedekler = glob.glob(os.path.join(self.yedek_klasor, "*.zip"))
        simdi = datetime.now().timestamp()
        silinen = 0
        
        for yedek in yedekler:
            # DosyanДұn yaЕҹДұnДұ hesapla (saniye cinsinden)
            dosya_zamani = os.path.getmtime(yedek)
            yas = (simdi - dosya_zamani) / (24*3600)  # GГјn cinsinden
            
            if yas > gun_sayisi:
                os.remove(yedek)
                silinen += 1
                print(f"рҹ—‘пёҸ Silindi: {os.path.basename(yedek)} ({yas:.1f} gГјn)")
        
        if silinen > 0:
            print(f"вң… {silinen} eski yedek temizlendi.")
    
    # ============================================
    # 6. YEDEKTEN GERД° YГңKLE
    # ============================================
    def geri_yukle(self, yedek_dosyasi):
        """Yedek dosyasДұndan sistemi geri yГјkler"""
        
        if not os.path.exists(yedek_dosyasi):
            print(f"вқҢ Yedek dosyasДұ bulunamadДұ: {yedek_dosyasi}")
            return False
        
        print(f"\nрҹ”„ YEDEKTEN GERД° YГңKLENД°YOR: {yedek_dosyasi}")
        print("="*60)
        
        # GeГ§ici bir klasГ¶r oluЕҹtur
        gecici_klasor = "gecici_yedek"
        if not os.path.exists(gecici_klasor):
            os.makedirs(gecici_klasor)
        
        # YedeДҹi aГ§
        with zipfile.ZipFile(yedek_dosyasi, 'r') as zipf:
            zipf.extractall(gecici_klasor)
            print("рҹ“Ӯ Yedek dosyalarДұ aГ§ДұldДұ")
        
        # DosyalarДұ geri yГјkle
        for dosya in os.listdir(gecici_klasor):
            kaynak = os.path.join(gecici_klasor, dosya)
            hedef = dosya
            
            # EДҹer hedef varsa yedekle
            if os.path.exists(hedef):
                yedek_hedef = hedef + ".yedek"
                shutil.copy2(hedef, yedek_hedef)
                print(f"рҹ“Ң Eski dosya yedeklendi: {yedek_hedef}")
            
            # Yeni dosyayДұ kopyala
            if os.path.isfile(kaynak):
                shutil.copy2(kaynak, hedef)
                print(f"вң… Geri yГјklendi: {dosya}")
            elif os.path.isdir(kaynak):
                if os.path.exists(hedef):
                    shutil.rmtree(hedef)
                shutil.copytree(kaynak, hedef)
                print(f"вң… KlasГ¶r geri yГјklendi: {dosya}")
        
        # GeГ§ici klasГ¶rГј temizle
        shutil.rmtree(gecici_klasor)
        print("-"*60)
        print("вң… Geri yГјkleme tamamlandДұ!")
        
        return True

# ============================================
# ANA PROGRAM
# ============================================
if __name__ == "__main__":
    print("""
в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ
в”Ӯ  рҹ’ҫ TRM YEDEKLEME SД°STEMД°          в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  TГңRKГҮE AГҮIKLAMALI                  в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  v1.0 - 2026                        в”Ӯ
в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ

    yedek = BackupSystem()
    
    while True:

        print("="*50)
        print("1пёҸвғЈ  Tam yedek al (TГјm sistem)")
        print("2пёҸвғЈ  HДұzlДұ yedek al (Г–nemli dosyalar)")
        print("3пёҸвғЈ  GГјnlГјk otomatik yedek")
        print("4пёҸвғЈ  Yedekleri listele")
        print("5пёҸвғЈ  Eski yedekleri temizle")
        print("6пёҸвғЈ  Yedekten geri yГјkle")

        print("-"*50)
