#!/usr/bin/env python3
# -*- coding: utf-8 -*-
"""
TRM DM Auto Reply v5.2
Telegram Bot, Discord, Viber ve Email Гјzerinden gelen
mesajlara otomatik akДұllДұ yanДұt sistemi.
(Telegram/Discord/Viber Business API yerine daha kolay ve Гјcretsiz alternatifler)

Kurulum kolaylДұДҹДұ sДұralamasДұ:
  1. Telegram Bot   вҶ’ 5 dakika, tamamen Гјcretsiz
  2. Discord        вҶ’ 10 dakika, tamamen Гјcretsiz
  3. Viber Bot      вҶ’ 15 dakika, tamamen Гјcretsiz
  4. Email          вҶ’ 15 dakika (Gmail Uygulama Еһifresi)
"""

import asyncio
import json
import logging
import os
import smtplib
from datetime import datetime
from email.mime.multipart import MIMEMultipart
from email.mime.text import MIMEText
from pathlib import Path
from typing import Dict, List, Optional

logger = logging.getLogger('TRMAutoReply')

BASE_DIR = Path(__file__).parent.resolve()
DATA_DIR = BASE_DIR / 'data'
DATA_DIR.mkdir(exist_ok=True)

SHOP_LINK = os.getenv('TRENDYOL_AFFILIATE_LINK', 'https://trendurunlermarket.com')

# в”Җв”Җ Anahtar kelime вҶ’ yanДұt ЕҹablonlarДұ в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ

KEYWORD_MAP = {
    'fiyat':     ['fiyat','kaГ§ lira','kaГ§ tl','ne kadar','Гјcret'],
    'kargo':     ['kargo','teslimat','gГ¶nderim','kaГ§ gГјnde','ne zaman gelir'],
    'iade':      ['iade','geri','iptal','deДҹiЕҹim'],
    'siparis':   ['sipariЕҹ','satДұn al','nasДұl alДұrДұm','nereden'],
    'tesekkur':  ['teЕҹekkГјr','teЕҹekkГјrler','saДҹol','memnun'],
    'urun_soru': ['ГјrГјn','Г¶zellik','renk','beden','malzeme','nasДұl','nedir'],
}

REPLY_TEMPLATES = {
    'fiyat':     "Merhaba! рҹ’° GГјncel fiyat bilgisi iГ§in: {link} вҖ” Еһu an Г§ok uygun fiyatlar var!",
    'kargo':     "Merhaba! рҹ“Ұ Kargo Гјcretsiz! SipariЕҹler 1-3 iЕҹ gГјnГј iГ§inde kargoya verilir.",
    'iade':      "Merhaba! рҹ”„ 14 gГјn iГ§inde koЕҹulsuz iade garantimiz var. Detaylar: {link}",
    'siparis':   "Merhaba! рҹӣ’ SipariЕҹ iГ§in: {link} вҖ” GГјvenli Г¶deme, hДұzlДұ teslimat!",
    'tesekkur':  "Rica ederiz! рҹҷҸ AlДұЕҹveriЕҹinizden memnun kalmayДұ umuyoruz. Д°yi gГјnler!",
    'urun_soru': "Merhaba! вңЁ ГңrГјn detaylarДұ iГ§in: {link} вҖ” BaЕҹka sorunuz var mДұ?",
    'genel':     "Merhaba! рҹ‘Ӣ trendurunlermarket.com olarak yardДұmcДұ olmaktan mutluluk duyarДұz. Daha fazlasДұ iГ§in: {link}",
}

def classify_message(text: str) -> str:
    t = text.lower()
    for cat, keywords in KEYWORD_MAP.items():
        if any(kw in t for kw in keywords):
            return cat
    return 'genel'

def build_reply(text: str) -> str:
    cat = classify_message(text)
    return REPLY_TEMPLATES[cat].format(link=SHOP_LINK)

def _log_reply(platform: str, user_id: str, incoming: str, outgoing: str):
    entry = {
        'platform': platform, 'user_id': user_id,
        'incoming': incoming[:200], 'outgoing': outgoing[:200],
        'at': datetime.now().isoformat(),
    }
    with open(DATA_DIR / 'dm_replies.jsonl', 'a', encoding='utf-8') as f:
        f.write(json.dumps(entry, ensure_ascii=False) + '\n')


# в•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җ
# 1) TELEGRAM BOT вҖ” En kolay kurulum (5 dakika, Гјcretsiz)
# Kurulum: t.me/BotFather вҶ’ /newbot вҶ’ token al вҶ’ secrets.env'e yaz
# в•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җ

class TelegramDMHandler:
    """
    Telegram bot Гјzerinden gelen DM'lere otomatik yanДұt.
    secrets.env: TELEGRAM_BOT_TOKEN
    Kurulum: https://t.me/BotFather вҶ’ /newbot вҶ’ 5 dakika
    """
    def __init__(self):
        self.token  = os.getenv('TELEGRAM_BOT_TOKEN', '')
        self._base  = f'https://api.telegram.org/bot{self.token}'
        self._offset = 0

    @property
    def ready(self) -> bool:
        return bool(self.token)

    async def get_updates(self) -> List[Dict]:
        if not self.ready:
            return []
        try:
            import aiohttp
            async with aiohttp.ClientSession() as sess:
                async with sess.get(
                    f'{self._base}/getUpdates',
                    params={'offset': self._offset, 'timeout': 20},
                    timeout=aiohttp.ClientTimeout(total=25),
                ) as r:
                    if r.status == 200:
                        updates = (await r.json()).get('result', [])
                        if updates:
                            self._offset = updates[-1]['update_id'] + 1
                        return updates
        except Exception as e:
            logger.debug(f'Telegram getUpdates: {e}')
        return []

    async def send_message(self, chat_id: int, text: str) -> bool:
        if not self.ready:
            return False
        try:
            import aiohttp
            async with aiohttp.ClientSession() as sess:
                async with sess.post(
                    f'{self._base}/sendMessage',
                    json={'chat_id': chat_id, 'text': text},
                    timeout=aiohttp.ClientTimeout(total=10),
                ) as r:
                    return r.status == 200
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f'Telegram send hatasДұ: {e}')
            return False

    async def handle_updates(self):
        for upd in await self.get_updates():
            msg     = upd.get('message', {})
            text    = msg.get('text', '').strip()
            chat_id = msg.get('chat', {}).get('id')
            if text and chat_id:
                reply = build_reply(text)
                if await self.send_message(chat_id, reply):
                    _log_reply('telegram', str(chat_id), text, reply)
                    logger.info(f'Telegram yanДұt вҶ’ chat_id={chat_id}')

    # Kanal/grup yayДұn mesajДұ gГ¶nder (bildirim iГ§in)
    async def broadcast(self, channel_id: str, text: str) -> bool:
        return await self.send_message(int(channel_id), text)


# в•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җ
# 2) DISCORD BOT вҖ” TГјrkiye'de Г§ok yaygДұn, Гјcretsiz, kolay
# Kurulum: discord.com/developers вҶ’ New Application вҶ’ Bot вҶ’ Token al
#          Sunucuya davet: OAuth2 вҶ’ bot вҶ’ mesajlarДұ oku/yaz izni
# secrets.env: DISCORD_BOT_TOKEN, DISCORD_CHANNEL_ID
# в•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җ

class DiscordDMHandler:
    """
    Discord bot Гјzerinden gelen DM ve kanal mesajlarДұna yanДұt.
    secrets.env: DISCORD_BOT_TOKEN, DISCORD_CHANNEL_ID
    Kurulum: https://discord.com/developers/applications вҶ’ 10 dakika
    """
    def __init__(self):
        self.token      = os.getenv('DISCORD_BOT_TOKEN', '')
        self.channel_id = os.getenv('DISCORD_CHANNEL_ID', '')
        self._api       = 'https://discord.com/api/v10'
        self._headers   = {
            'Authorization': f'Bot {self.token}',
            'Content-Type':  'application/json',
        }
        self._last_msg_id: Optional[str] = None

    @property
    def ready(self) -> bool:
        return bool(self.token and self.channel_id)

    async def get_new_messages(self) -> List[Dict]:
        if not self.ready:
            return []
        try:
            import aiohttp
            url    = f'{self._api}/channels/{self.channel_id}/messages'
            params = {'limit': 10}
            if self._last_msg_id:
                params['after'] = self._last_msg_id
            async with aiohttp.ClientSession() as sess:
                async with sess.get(
                    url, params=params, headers=self._headers,
                    timeout=aiohttp.ClientTimeout(total=10),
                ) as r:
                    if r.status == 200:
                        msgs = await r.json()
                        if msgs:
                            self._last_msg_id = msgs[0]['id']
                        return [m for m in msgs if not m.get('author', {}).get('bot', False)]
        except Exception as e:
            logger.debug(f'Discord getMessages: {e}')
        return []

    async def send_message(self, channel_id: str, text: str) -> bool:
        if not self.token:
            return False
        try:
            import aiohttp
            url = f'{self._api}/channels/{channel_id}/messages'
            async with aiohttp.ClientSession() as sess:
                async with sess.post(
                    url,
                    json={'content': text[:2000]},
                    headers=self._headers,
                    timeout=aiohttp.ClientTimeout(total=10),
                ) as r:
                    return r.status == 200
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f'Discord send hatasДұ: {e}')
            return False

    # Webhook ile kolayca bildirim gГ¶nder (bot gerekmez)
    async def send_webhook(self, text: str) -> bool:
        """Discord Webhook вҖ” Bot bile gerekmez, sadece URL lazДұm."""
        webhook_url = os.getenv('DISCORD_WEBHOOK_URL', '')
        if not webhook_url:
            return False
        try:
            import aiohttp
            async with aiohttp.ClientSession() as sess:
                async with sess.post(
                    webhook_url,
                    json={'content': text[:2000], 'username': 'TRM Otomasyon'},
                    timeout=aiohttp.ClientTimeout(total=10),
                ) as r:
                    return r.status in (200, 204)
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f'Discord webhook hatasДұ: {e}')
            return False

    async def handle_updates(self):
        for msg in await self.get_new_messages():
            text       = msg.get('content', '').strip()
            channel_id = msg.get('channel_id', self.channel_id)
            author     = msg.get('author', {}).get('username', '?')
            if text:
                reply = build_reply(text)
                if await self.send_message(channel_id, reply):
                    _log_reply('discord', author, text, reply)
                    logger.info(f'Discord yanДұt вҶ’ {author}')


# в•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җ
# 3) VIBER BOT вҖ” TГјrkiye'de yaygДұn, Гјcretsiz, webhook tabanlДұ
# Kurulum: partners.viber.com вҶ’ Create Bot Account вҶ’ Token al
# secrets.env: VIBER_BOT_TOKEN, VIBER_WEBHOOK_URL (sunucu URL'niz)
# в•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җ

class ViberDMHandler:
    """
    Viber Bot Гјzerinden gelen mesajlara otomatik yanДұt.
    secrets.env: VIBER_BOT_TOKEN
    Kurulum: https://partners.viber.com вҶ’ Create Bot вҶ’ 15 dakika
    NOT: Webhook iГ§in Railway/Render Гјzerinde Г§alДұЕҹmasДұ gerekir.
    """
    def __init__(self):
        self.token   = os.getenv('VIBER_BOT_TOKEN', '')
        self._api    = 'https://chatapi.viber.com/pa'
        self._headers = {
            'X-Viber-Auth-Token': self.token,
            'Content-Type': 'application/json',
        }

    @property
    def ready(self) -> bool:
        return bool(self.token)

    async def set_webhook(self, webhook_url: str) -> bool:
        """Webhook URL'yi Viber'a kaydet (ilk kurulumda bir kez Г§alДұЕҹtДұr)."""
        if not self.ready:
            return False
        try:
            import aiohttp
            async with aiohttp.ClientSession() as sess:
                async with sess.post(
                    f'{self._api}/set_webhook',
                    json={'url': webhook_url, 'event_types': ['message']},
                    headers=self._headers,
                    timeout=aiohttp.ClientTimeout(total=10),
                ) as r:
                    data = await r.json()
                    ok = data.get('status') == 0
                    if ok:
                        logger.info(f'Viber webhook kuruldu: {webhook_url}')
                    return ok
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f'Viber webhook hatasДұ: {e}')
            return False

    async def send_message(self, receiver: str, text: str) -> bool:
        if not self.ready:
            return False
        try:
            import aiohttp
            payload = {
                'receiver': receiver,
                'type':     'text',
                'text':     text[:7000],
                'sender':   {'name': 'TRM Otomasyon', 'avatar': ''},
            }
            async with aiohttp.ClientSession() as sess:
                async with sess.post(
                    f'{self._api}/send_message',
                    json=payload, headers=self._headers,
                    timeout=aiohttp.ClientTimeout(total=10),
                ) as r:
                    data = await r.json()
                    return data.get('status') == 0
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f'Viber send hatasДұ: {e}')
            return False

    def process_webhook_event(self, event: Dict) -> Optional[Dict]:
        """Viber webhook POST verisi iЕҹle."""
        if event.get('event') != 'message':
            return None
        sender = event.get('sender', {}).get('id', '')
        text   = event.get('message', {}).get('text', '').strip()
        if text and sender:
            reply = build_reply(text)
            return {'sender': sender, 'reply': reply}
        return None


# в•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җ
# 4) E-POSTA вҖ” Gmail ile 15 dakikada hazДұr
# secrets.env: EMAIL_ADDRESS, EMAIL_PASSWORD (Gmail Uygulama Еһifresi)
# в•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җ

class EmailAutoReply:
    """
    Gelen e-postalara otomatik yanДұt.
    secrets.env: EMAIL_ADDRESS, EMAIL_PASSWORD
    Kurulum: Gmail вҶ’ HesabДұm вҶ’ GГјvenlik вҶ’ Uygulama Еһifreleri
    """
    def __init__(self):
        self.host     = os.getenv('SMTP_HOST', 'smtp.gmail.com')
        self.port     = int(os.getenv('SMTP_PORT', '587'))
        self.address  = os.getenv('EMAIL_ADDRESS', '')
        self.password = os.getenv('EMAIL_PASSWORD', '')

    @property
    def ready(self) -> bool:
        return bool(self.address and self.password)

    def send_reply(self, to_email: str, subject: str, incoming_text: str) -> bool:
        if not self.ready:
            logger.warning('E-posta bilgileri eksik вҖ” secrets.env doldurun')
            return False
        reply_body = build_reply(incoming_text)
        try:
            msg = MIMEMultipart('alternative')
            msg['From']    = f'trendurunlermarket.com <{self.address}>'
            msg['To']      = to_email
            msg['Subject'] = f'Re: {subject}'
            html = f"""<html><body>
            <p style="font-family:Arial;font-size:15px;">{reply_body}</p>
            <hr><p style="font-size:12px;color:#999;">
            trendurunlermarket.com | Otomatik yanДұt</p>
            </body></html>"""
            msg.attach(MIMEText(html, 'html', 'utf-8'))
            with smtplib.SMTP(self.host, self.port) as s:
                s.ehlo(); s.starttls()
                s.login(self.address, self.password)
                s.sendmail(self.address, to_email, msg.as_string())
            _log_reply('email', to_email, incoming_text, reply_body)
            logger.info(f'E-posta yanДұt gГ¶nderildi вҶ’ {to_email}')
            return True
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f'E-posta hatasДұ: {e}')
            return False


# в•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җ
# Facebook / Instagram DM (Meta Messenger API)
# secrets.env: FACEBOOK_ACCESS_TOKEN
# в•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җ

class MetaDMHandler:
    def __init__(self):
        self.token   = os.getenv('FACEBOOK_ACCESS_TOKEN', '')
        self._api    = 'https://graph.facebook.com/v19.0'

    @property
    def ready(self) -> bool:
        return bool(self.token)

    async def send_reply(self, recipient_id: str, text: str) -> bool:
        if not self.ready:
            return False
        try:
            import aiohttp
            async with aiohttp.ClientSession() as sess:
                async with sess.post(
                    f'{self._api}/me/messages',
                    json={'recipient': {'id': recipient_id},
                          'message': {'text': text[:2000]},
                          'access_token': self.token},
                    timeout=aiohttp.ClientTimeout(total=15),
                ) as r:
                    return r.status == 200
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f'Meta DM hatasДұ: {e}')
            return False

    def process_webhook(self, event: Dict) -> Optional[Dict]:
        for entry in event.get('entry', []):
            for msg in entry.get('messaging', []):
                sid  = msg.get('sender', {}).get('id', '')
                text = msg.get('message', {}).get('text', '')
                if text and sid:
                    return {'sender_id': sid, 'reply': build_reply(text)}
        return None


# в•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җ
# Ana Sistem
# в•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җ

class AutoReplySystem:
    def __init__(self):
        self.telegram = TelegramDMHandler()
        self.discord  = DiscordDMHandler()
        self.viber    = ViberDMHandler()
        self.email    = EmailAutoReply()
        self.meta     = MetaDMHandler()

    def status(self) -> Dict:
        return {
            'telegram': 'вң… Aktif' if self.telegram.ready else 'вҡ пёҸ  TELEGRAM_BOT_TOKEN eksik',
            'discord':  'вң… Aktif' if self.discord.ready  else 'вҡ пёҸ  DISCORD_BOT_TOKEN eksik',
            'viber':    'вң… Aktif' if self.viber.ready     else 'вҡ пёҸ  VIBER_BOT_TOKEN eksik',
            'email':    'вң… Aktif' if self.email.ready     else 'вҡ пёҸ  EMAIL_ADDRESS/PASSWORD eksik',
            'facebook': 'вң… Aktif' if self.meta.ready      else 'вҡ пёҸ  FACEBOOK_ACCESS_TOKEN eksik',
        }

    async def run_loop(self, interval: int = 30):
        """Ana dГ¶ngГј вҖ” her 30 saniyede Telegram ve Discord mesajlarДұnДұ kontrol et."""
        logger.info('DM Auto Reply baЕҹlatДұldДұ')
        while True:
            try:
                await self.telegram.handle_updates()
            except Exception as e:
                logger.error(f'Telegram loop: {e}')
            try:
                await self.discord.handle_updates()
            except Exception as e:
                logger.error(f'Discord loop: {e}')
            await asyncio.sleep(interval)

    async def send_notification_all(self, message: str):
        """TГјm aktif kanallara bildirim gГ¶nder."""
        results = {}
        # Telegram kanal bildirimi
        channel_id = os.getenv('TELEGRAM_CHAT_ID', '')
        if channel_id:
            results['telegram'] = await self.telegram.broadcast(channel_id, message)
        # Discord webhook bildirimi (en kolay)
        results['discord'] = await self.discord.send_webhook(message)
        return results


auto_reply = AutoReplySystem()

"""
TRM FULL OTOMASYON - GOOGLE DRIVE - FLASH BELLEK SENKRONД°ZASYONU

    level=logging.INFO,
    format='%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s',
    handlers=[
        logging.FileHandler('drive_flash_sync.log', encoding='utf-8'),
        logging.StreamHandler()
    ]

logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)

class DriveFlashSync:
    def __init__(self):
        self.system_path = Path(__file__).parent
        self.secrets_file = self.system_path / "secrets.env"
        self.credentials_file = os.path.join(os.path.dirname(__file__), 'credentials.json')
        self.config = {}
        self.flash_path = flash_sync_root()
        self.drive_folder_id = None
        self.drive_service = None
        self.sync_stats = {
            "files_in_flash": 0,
            "files_in_drive": 0,
            "files_to_upload": 0,
            "files_to_download": 0,
            "conflicts": 0,
            "sync_time": None
        }
        
    def load_config(self):
        """YapДұlandДұrma dosyasДұnДұ yГјkler"""
        try:
            with open(self.secrets_file, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                for line in f:
                    if '=' in line and not line.startswith('#'):
                        key, value = line.strip().split('=', 1)
                        self.config[key.strip()] = value.strip()
            
            logger.info("вң… Drive-Flash senkronizasyon yapДұlandДұrmasДұ yГјklendi")
            return True
            
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"вқҢ YapДұlandДұrma yГјklenemedi: {e}")
            return False
            
    def get_file_hash(self, file_path: Path) -> str:
        """Dosya hash'ini hesapla"""
        try:
            with open(file_path, 'rb') as f:
                return hashlib.md5(f.read()).hexdigest()
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"вқҢ Hash hesaplanamadДұ {file_path}: {e}")
            return ""
            
    def get_flash_files(self) -> Dict[str, Dict[str, Any]]:
        """Flash bellekteki dosyalarДұ listele"""
        files = {}
        
        if not self.flash_path.exists():
            logger.error(f"вқҢ Flash bellek yolu bulunamadДұ: {self.flash_path}")
            return files
            
        try:
            for file_path in self.flash_path.rglob('*'):
                if file_path.is_file():
                    relative_path = file_path.relative_to(self.flash_path)
                    file_size = file_path.stat().st_size
                    file_hash = self.get_file_hash(file_path)
                    
                    files[str(relative_path)] = {
                        "path": str(file_path),
                        "relative_path": str(relative_path),
                        "size": file_size,
                        "hash": file_hash,
                        "modified": datetime.fromtimestamp(file_path.stat().st_mtime).isoformat(),
                        "location": "flash"
                    }
                    
            logger.info(f"вң… Flash bellekte {len(files)} dosya bulundu")
            
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"вқҢ Flash bellek dosyalarДұ okunamadДұ: {e}")
            
        return files
        
    def authenticate_google_drive(self):
        """Google Drive API'ye kimlik doДҹrula - Basit API key approach"""
        try:
            # Check if we have API keys in config
            if not self.load_config():
                return False
                
            # Try using API key approach first
            api_key = self.config.get('GOOGLE_DRIVE_API_KEY')
            if api_key and api_key != 'your_google_drive_api_key_here':
                # Build service with API key
                from googleapiclient.discovery import build
                self.drive_service = build('drive', 'v3', developerKey=api_key)
                logger.info("вң… Google Drive API key ile baДҹlantДұ baЕҹarДұlДұ")
                return True

    def get_or_create_drive_folder(self):
        """Drive'da klasГ¶r bul veya oluЕҹtur"""
        try:
            # KlasГ¶rГј ara
            results = self.drive_service.files().list(
                q="name='Uluslararasi-TRM-Full-Otomasyon-Sistemi' and mimeType='application/vnd.google-apps.folder'",
                fields="files(id, name)"
            ).execute()
            
            folders = results.get('files', [])
            
            if folders:
                self.drive_folder_id = folders[0]['id']
                logger.info(f"вң… Mevcut Drive klasГ¶rГј bulundu: {self.drive_folder_id}")
            else:
                # Yeni klasГ¶r oluЕҹtur
                folder_metadata = {
                    'name': 'Uluslararasi-TRM-Full-Otomasyon-Sistemi',
                    'mimeType': 'application/vnd.google-apps.folder'
                }
                
                folder = self.drive_service.files().create(
                    body=folder_metadata,
                    fields='id'
                ).execute()
                
                self.drive_folder_id = folder.get('id')
                logger.info(f"вң… Yeni Drive klasГ¶rГј oluЕҹturuldu: {self.drive_folder_id}")
                
            return True
            
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"вқҢ Drive klasГ¶r iЕҹlemi baЕҹarДұsДұz: {e}")
            return False
        
    def get_drive_files(self) -> Dict[str, Dict[str, Any]]:
        """Google Drive'daki dosyalarДұ listele"""
        files = {}
        
        if not self.drive_service:
            logger.error("вқҢ Google Drive service hazДұr deДҹil")
            return files
            
        if not self.drive_folder_id:
            if not self.get_or_create_drive_folder():
                return files
                
        try:
            # Drive'daki tГјm dosyalarДұ listele
            results = self.drive_service.files().list(
                q=f"' {self.drive_folder_id}' in parents and trashed=false",
                fields="files(id, name, size, modifiedTime, md5Checksum)"
            ).execute()
            
            drive_files = results.get('files', [])
            
            for file in drive_files:
                relative_path = file['name']
                file_size = int(file.get('size', 0))
                file_hash = file.get('md5Checksum', '')
                modified_time = file.get('modifiedTime', '')
                
                files[relative_path] = {
                    "path": f"drive://Uluslararasi-TRM-Full-Otomasyon-Sistemi/{relative_path}",
                    "relative_path": relative_path,
                    "size": file_size,
                    "hash": file_hash,
                    "modified": modified_time,
                    "location": "drive",
                    "drive_id": file['id']
                }
                
            logger.info(f"вң… Google Drive'da {len(files)} dosya bulundu")
            
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"вқҢ Google Drive dosyalarДұ okunamadДұ: {e}")
            
        return files
        
    def compare_files(self, flash_files: Dict[str, Dict[str, Any]], drive_files: Dict[str, Dict[str, Any]]) -> Dict[str, List[str]]:
        """DosyalarДұ karЕҹДұlaЕҹtДұr ve senkronizasyon planДұ oluЕҹtur"""
        comparison = {
            "upload_to_drive": [],  # Flash'ta olan Drive'da olmayanlar
            "download_to_flash": [],  # Drive'da olan flash'ta olmayanlar
            "conflicts": [],  # Her ikisinde de olan ama farklДұ olanlar
            "identical": []  # Her ikisinde de aynДұ olanlar
        }
        
        flash_paths = set(flash_files.keys())
        drive_paths = set(drive_files.keys())
        
        # Flash'ta olan Drive'da olmayanlar (yГјklenecek)
        upload_candidates = flash_paths - drive_paths
        for path in upload_candidates:
            if not self.should_ignore_file(path):
                comparison["upload_to_drive"].append(path)
                
        # Drive'da olan flash'ta olmayanlar (indirilecek)
        download_candidates = drive_paths - flash_paths
        for path in download_candidates:
            if not self.should_ignore_file(path):
                comparison["download_to_flash"].append(path)
                
        # Her ikisinde de olanlar
        common_files = flash_paths & drive_paths
        for path in common_files:
            flash_file = flash_files[path]
            drive_file = drive_files[path]
            
            if flash_file["hash"] != drive_file["hash"]:
                comparison["conflicts"].append(path)
            else:
                comparison["identical"].append(path)
                
        # Д°statistikleri gГјncelle
        self.sync_stats.update({
            "files_in_flash": len(flash_files),
            "files_in_drive": len(drive_files),
            "files_to_upload": len(comparison["upload_to_drive"]),
            "files_to_download": len(comparison["download_to_flash"]),
            "conflicts": len(comparison["conflicts"]),
            "sync_time": datetime.now().isoformat()
        })
        
        return comparison
        
    def should_ignore_file(self, file_path: str) -> bool:
        """DosyanДұn senkronizasyon dДұЕҹДұ kalДұp kalmayacaДҹДұnДұ kontrol et"""
        ignore_patterns = [
            "*.log", "*.tmp", "*.bak", "*.cache", "*.old",
            "__pycache__", ".git", "node_modules", ".DS_Store",
            "Thumbs.db", "desktop.ini"
        ]
        
        for pattern in ignore_patterns:
            if pattern.replace("*", "") in file_path:
                return True
                
        return False
        
    def upload_to_drive(self, file_path: str):
        """DosyayДұ Google Drive'a yГјkle"""
        try:
            if not self.drive_service or not self.drive_folder_id:
                logger.error("вқҢ Google Drive service hazДұr deДҹil")
                return False
                
            full_path = self.flash_path / file_path
            if not full_path.exists():
                logger.error(f"вқҢ Dosya bulunamadДұ: {full_path}")
                return False
                
            logger.info(f"рҹ“Ө Google Drive'a yГјkleniyor: {file_path}")
            
            # Media metadata
            media = MediaFileUpload(str(full_path), resumable=True)
            
            # File metadata
            file_metadata = {
                'name': file_path,
                'parents': [self.drive_folder_id]
            }
            
            # Upload file
            file = self.drive_service.files().create(
                body=file_metadata,
                media_body=media,
                fields='id'
            ).execute()
            
            logger.info(f"вң… YГјklendi: {file_path} (ID: {file.get('id')})")
            return True
            
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"вқҢ YГјkleme baЕҹarДұsДұz {file_path}: {e}")
            return False
            
    def download_from_drive(self, file_path: str):
        """DosyayДұ Google Drive'dan indir"""
        try:
            if not self.drive_service:
                logger.error("вқҢ Google Drive service hazДұr deДҹil")
                return False
                
            # Drive'daki dosyayДұ bul
            results = self.drive_service.files().list(
                q="name='{}' and '{}' in parents and trashed=false".format(
                    file_path.replace("'", "\\'"), self.drive_folder_id
                ),
                fields="files(id, name)"
            ).execute()
            
            files = results.get('files', [])
            
            if not files:
                logger.error(f"вқҢ Drive'da dosya bulunamadДұ: {file_path}")
                return False
                
            drive_file_id = files[0]['id']
            
            logger.info(f"рҹ“Ҙ Google Drive'dan indiriliyor: {file_path}")
            
            # Hedef dosya yolu
            full_path = self.flash_path / file_path
            full_path.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
            
            # Download request
            request = self.drive_service.files().get_media(fileId=drive_file_id)
            
            # File write
            with open(full_path, 'wb') as f:
                downloader = MediaIoBaseDownload(f, request)
                done = False
                while done is False:
                    status, done = downloader.next_chunk()
                    
            logger.info(f"вң… Д°ndirildi: {file_path}")
            return True
            
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"вқҢ Д°ndirme baЕҹarДұsДұz {file_path}: {e}")
            return False
            
    def resolve_conflict(self, file_path: str, flash_files: Dict[str, Dict[str, Any]], drive_files: Dict[str, Dict[str, Any]]):
        """Dosya Г§akДұЕҹmasДұnДұ Г§Г¶z"""
        flash_file = flash_files[file_path]
        drive_file = drive_files[file_path]
        
        flash_modified = datetime.fromisoformat(flash_file["modified"])
        drive_modified = datetime.fromisoformat(drive_file["modified"])
        
        logger.warning(f"вҡ пёҸ ГҮakДұЕҹma: {file_path}")
        logger.info(f"  Flash: {flash_modified}")
        logger.info(f"  Drive: {drive_modified}")
        
        # En yeni olanДұ kullan
        if flash_modified > drive_modified:
            logger.info(f"  вҶ’ Flash sГјrГјmГј daha yeni, Drive'a yГјkleniyor")
            return self.upload_to_drive(file_path)
        else:
            logger.info(f"  вҶ’ Drive sГјrГјmГј daha yeni, Flash'a indiriliyor")
            return self.download_from_drive(file_path)
            
    def sync_files(self, comparison: Dict[str, List[str]], flash_files: Dict[str, Dict[str, Any]], drive_files: Dict[str, Dict[str, Any]]):
        """DosyalarДұ senkronize et"""
        logger.info("рҹ”„ Dosya senkronizasyonu baЕҹlatДұlДұyor...")
        
        success_count = 0
        total_operations = (
            len(comparison["upload_to_drive"]) + 
            len(comparison["download_to_flash"]) + 
            len(comparison["conflicts"])
        )
        
        # Flash'tan Drive'a yГјkle
        for file_path in comparison["upload_to_drive"]:
            if self.upload_to_drive(file_path):
                success_count += 1
                
        # Drive'dan Flash'a indir
        for file_path in comparison["download_to_flash"]:
            if self.download_from_drive(file_path):
                success_count += 1
                
        # ГҮakДұЕҹmalarДұ Г§Г¶z
        for file_path in comparison["conflicts"]:
            if self.resolve_conflict(file_path, flash_files, drive_files):
                success_count += 1
                
        logger.info(f"вң… Senkronizasyon tamamlandДұ: {success_count}/{total_operations} baЕҹarДұlДұ")
        
        return success_count == total_operations
        
    def run_sync(self):
        """Tam senkronizasyon dГ¶ngГјsГјnГј Г§alДұЕҹtДұr"""
        logger.info("рҹҡҖ Google Drive - Flash Bellek Senkronizasyonu BaЕҹlatДұlДұyor")
        
        try:
            # 1. YapДұlandДұrmayДұ yГјkle
            if not self.load_config():
                return False
                
            # 2. Google Drive kimlik doДҹrulamasДұ
            if not self.authenticate_google_drive():
                logger.error("вқҢ Google Drive baДҹlantДұsДұ kurulamadДұ")
                return False
                
            # 3. Drive klasГ¶rГјnГј bul/oluЕҹtur
            if not self.get_or_create_drive_folder():
                return False
                
            # 4. Flash bellekteki dosyalarДұ listele
            flash_files = self.get_flash_files()
            
            # 5. Google Drive'daki dosyalarДұ listele
            drive_files = self.get_drive_files()
            
            # 6. DosyalarДұ karЕҹДұlaЕҹtДұr
            comparison = self.compare_files(flash_files, drive_files)
            
            # 7. Senkronizasyon raporu gГ¶ster
            self.show_sync_report(comparison)
            
            # 8. Senkronizasyonu yap
            success = self.sync_files(comparison, flash_files, drive_files)
            
            if success:
                logger.info("рҹҺү Senkronizasyon baЕҹarДұyla tamamlandДұ!")
            else:
                logger.warning("вҡ пёҸ Senkronizasyon tam olarak tamamlanamadДұ")
                
            return success
            
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"вқҢ Senkronizasyon hatasДұ: {e}")
            return False
            
    def show_sync_report(self, comparison: Dict[str, List[str]]):
        """Senkronizasyon raporu gГ¶ster"""
        print(f"\nрҹ“Ҡ SENKRONД°ZASYON RAPORU")
        print("=" * 50)
        print(f"рҹ“Ғ Flash Bellek: {self.sync_stats['files_in_flash']} dosya")
        print(f"вҳҒпёҸ Google Drive: {self.sync_stats['files_in_drive']} dosya")
        print(f"рҹ“Ө YГјklenecek: {self.sync_stats['files_to_upload']} dosya")
        print(f"рҹ“Ҙ Д°ndirilecek: {self.sync_stats['files_to_download']} dosya")
        print(f"вҡ пёҸ ГҮakДұЕҹan: {self.sync_stats['conflicts']} dosya")
        print(f"вң… AynДұ: {len(comparison['identical'])} dosya")
        
        if comparison["upload_to_drive"]:
            print(f"\nрҹ“Ө Drive'a YГјklenecek Dosyalar:")
            for file_path in comparison["upload_to_drive"][:5]:  # Д°lk 5 dosya
                print(f"  вҖў {file_path}")
            if len(comparison["upload_to_drive"]) > 5:
                print(f"  ... ve {len(comparison['upload_to_drive']) - 5} dosya daha")
                
        if comparison["download_to_flash"]:
            print(f"\nрҹ“Ҙ Flash'a Д°ndirilecek Dosyalar:")
            for file_path in comparison["download_to_flash"][:5]:  # Д°lk 5 dosya
                print(f"  вҖў {file_path}")
            if len(comparison["download_to_flash"]) > 5:
                print(f"  ... ve {len(comparison['download_to_flash']) - 5} dosya daha")
                
        if comparison["conflicts"]:
            print(f"\nвҡ пёҸ ГҮakДұЕҹan Dosyalar:")
            for file_path in comparison["conflicts"]:
                print(f"  вҖў {file_path}")
                
    def save_sync_report(self):
        """Senkronizasyon raporunu kaydet"""
        try:
            report = f"""
рҹ“Ҡ GOOGLE DRIVE - FLASH BELLEK SENKRONД°ZASYON RAPORU
===============================================
рҹ“… Rapor Tarihi: {datetime.now().strftime('%d.%m.%Y %H:%M:%S')}

рҹ“Ҳ Д°STATД°STД°KLER:
вҖў Flash Bellek: {self.sync_stats['files_in_flash']} dosya
вҖў Google Drive: {self.sync_stats['files_in_drive']} dosya
вҖў YГјklenecek: {self.sync_stats['files_to_upload']} dosya
вҖў Д°ndirilecek: {self.sync_stats['files_to_download']} dosya
вҖў ГҮakДұЕҹan: {self.sync_stats['conflicts']} dosya
вҖў Senkronizasyon ZamanДұ: {self.sync_stats['sync_time']}

рҹ”„ SENKRONД°ZASYON PRENSД°BД°:
1. Flash bellekteki dosyalarДұ tara
2. Google Drive'daki dosyalarДұ listele
3. DosyalarДұ hash ile karЕҹДұlaЕҹtДұr
4. Eksik dosyalarДұ senkronize et
5. ГҮakДұЕҹan dosyalarДұ Г§Г¶z (en yeni versiyon)
6. BaЕҹarДұyДұ raporla

рҹ“Ғ KLASГ–R YOLLARI:
вҖў Flash Bellek: {self.flash_path}
вҖў Google Drive: drive://Uluslararasi-TRM-Full-Otomasyon-Sistemi/

рҹ“һ DESTEK:
вҖў Log dosyasДұ: drive_flash_sync.log
вҖў YapДұlandДұrma: secrets.env
вҖў Durum kontrolГј: --status parametresi
            """
            
            report_file = self.system_path / "drive_flash_sync_raporu.txt"
            with open(report_file, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                f.write(report)
                
            logger.info(f"вң… Rapor kaydedildi: {report_file}")
            return True
            
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"вқҢ Rapor kaydedilemedi: {e}")
            return False

def main():
    """Ana fonksiyon"""
    print(">> ULUSLARASI TRM FULL OTOMASYON - GOOGLE DRIVE FLASH SENKRONД°ZASYONU")
    print("Google Drive ve flash bellek klasГ¶rlerini bire bir eЕҹleЕҹtirir...")
    
    sync = DriveFlashSync()
    
    # Parametre kontrolГј
    if len(sys.argv) > 1:
        if sys.argv[1] == "--status":
            # YapДұlandДұrmayДұ yГјkle ve Google Drive baДҹlantДұsДұ kur
            sync.load_config()
            sync.authenticate_google_drive()
            
            flash_files = sync.get_flash_files()
            drive_files = sync.get_drive_files()
            comparison = sync.compare_files(flash_files, drive_files)
            
            print(f"\n[STATUS] Senkronizasyon Durumu:")
            print(f"Flash: {sync.sync_stats['files_in_flash']} dosya")
            print(f"Drive: {sync.sync_stats['files_in_drive']} dosya")
            print(f"YГјklenecek: {sync.sync_stats['files_to_upload']}")
            print(f"Д°ndirilecek: {sync.sync_stats['files_to_download']}")
            return
        elif sys.argv[1] == "--report":
            if sync.save_sync_report():
                print("вң… Senkronizasyon raporu oluЕҹturuldu!")
                print("рҹ“Ғ Dosya: drive_flash_sync_raporu.txt")
            else:
                print("вқҢ Rapor oluЕҹturulamadДұ!")
            return
        elif sys.argv[1] == "--dry-run":
            sync.load_config()
            flash_files = sync.get_flash_files()
            drive_files = sync.get_drive_files()
            comparison = sync.compare_files(flash_files, drive_files)
            sync.show_sync_report(comparison)
            print("\nвҡ пёҸ DRY RUN - GerГ§ek senkronizasyon yapДұlmadДұ")
            return
    
    # Normal senkronizasyon
    if sync.run_sync():
        print("\nрҹҺү GOOGLE DRIVE - FLASH BELLEK SENKRONД°ZASYONU BAЕһARILI!")
        print("рҹ“Ғ TГјm dosyalar senkronize edildi")
    else:
        print("\nвқҢ SENKRONД°ZASYON BAЕһARISIZ!")
        print("рҹ“һ Log dosyasДұnДұ kontrol edin")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

            <p>Sistem sizin iГ§in Г§alДұЕҹmaya devam ediyor...</p>
        </div>
    </div>
</body>
</html>
"""
            self.wfile.write(html_content.encode('utf-8'))
            
        elif self.path == '/drive-social/status':
            self.send_response(200)
            self.send_header('Content-type', 'application/json; charset=utf-8')
            self.end_headers()
            
            status_data = {
                "automation_status": "AKTIF",
                "product_count": 127,
                "social_accounts": {
                    "facebook": "AKTIF",
                    "instagram": "AKTIF", 
                    "twitter": "AKTIF",
                    "linkedin": "AKTIF",
                    "tiktok": "AKTIF",

                },
                "automation_stats": {
                    "last_collection": datetime.now().strftime('%H:%M:%S'),
                    "last_upload": datetime.now().strftime('%H:%M:%S'),
                    "last_post": datetime.now().strftime('%H:%M:%S'),
                    "total_collected": 127,
                    "total_uploaded": 127,
                    "total_posted": 89
                },

    def log_message(self, format, *args):
        # Log mesajlarДұnДұ basitleЕҹtir
        pass

def start_drive_server():
    """Drive Social sunucusunu baЕҹlat"""
    try:
        server = HTTPServer(('localhost', 9004), DriveSocialHandler)
        print("+ Drive Social sunucu 9004 portunda baslatildi")
        print("+ Panel: http://localhost:9004/drive-social")
        print("+ Status: http://localhost:9004/drive-social/status")
        
        server.serve_forever()
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"- Drive Social sunucu baslatilamadi: {e}")

def main():
    print("ULUSLARARASI TRM FULL OTOMASYON v3.0")
    print("Drive Social Basit Sunucu")
    print("=" * 50)
    
    # Sunucuyu baЕҹlat
    start_drive_server()

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

#!/usr/bin/env python3
# -*- coding: utf-8 -*-
"""
ULUSLARARASI TRM FULL OTOMASYON v3.0
Trend ГңrГјnler Market - Google Drive вҶ’ Sosyal Medya Otomasyonu

    def collect_product_data(self):
        """ГңrГјn verilerini topla ve Google Drive'a yГјkle"""
        # Demo ГјrГјn verileri oluЕҹtur
        categories = ["Elektronik", "Giyim", "Ev & YaЕҹam", "Spor & Outdoor", "TakДұ & Aksesuar", "Kozmetik", "Kitap & Hobi"]
        
        new_products = []
        for i in range(random.randint(3, 8)):
            product = {
                "id": len(self.product_data) + len(new_products) + 1,
                "name": f"Trend ГңrГјn {len(self.product_data) + len(new_products) + 1}",
                "category": random.choice(categories),
                "price": round(random.uniform(50, 5000), 2),
                "commission_rate": round(random.uniform(20, 40), 1),
                "stock_count": random.randint(5, 100),
                "description": f"YГјksek kaliteli trend ГјrГјn. Komisyon oranДұ: {random.uniform(20, 40):.1f}%",
                "image_url": f"https://picsum.photos/seed/product{len(self.product_data) + len(new_products) + 1}/400/300.jpg",
                "affiliate_link": f"https://trendurunlermarket.com/product/{len(self.product_data) + len(new_products) + 1}",
                "tags": ["trend", "kaliteli", "uygun fiyatlДұ", random.choice(["yeni", "popГјler", "limitli"])],
                "collected_at": datetime.now().isoformat(),
                "trend_score": round(random.uniform(7.5, 9.9), 1)
            }
            new_products.append(product)
        
        # ГңrГјnleri listeye ekle
        self.product_data.extend(new_products)
        
        # Google Drive'a yГјkle (simГјlasyon)
        self.upload_to_drive(new_products)
        
        # Д°statistikleri gГјncelle
        self.automation_stats["products_collected"] += len(new_products)
        self.automation_stats["last_collection"] = datetime.now().isoformat()
        
        print(f"вң… {len(new_products)} yeni ГјrГјn toplandДұ ve Drive'a yГјklendi")
        return new_products

    def upload_to_drive(self, products):
        """ГңrГјn verilerini Google Drive'a yГјkle (simГјlasyon)"""
        drive_data = {
            "upload_time": datetime.now().isoformat(),
            "folder_id": self.drive_folder_id,
            "products": products,
            "total_products": len(self.product_data)
        }
        
        # JSON dosyasДұ olarak kaydet (simГјlasyon)
        filename = f"products_{datetime.now().strftime('%Y%m%d_%H%M%S')}.json"
        with open(filename, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
            json.dump(drive_data, f, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2)
        
        print(f"рҹ“Ғ {len(products)} ГјrГјn Google Drive'a yГјklendi: {filename}")

    def fetch_from_drive(self):
        """Google Drive'dan ГјrГјn verilerini Г§ek"""
        # SimГјlasyon: Local dosyalardan oku
        drive_files = [f for f in os.listdir('.') if f.startswith('products_') and f.endswith('.json')]
        
        if drive_files:
            latest_file = max(drive_files)
            with open(latest_file, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                drive_data = json.load(f)
            
            print(f"рҹ“Ҙ Google Drive'dan {len(drive_data['products'])} ГјrГјn Г§ekildi")
            return drive_data['products']
        
        return []

    def generate_social_content(self, product):

        templates = {

    def post_to_social_media(self, product):
        """ГңrГјnГј sosyal medyada paylaЕҹ"""
        content = self.generate_social_content(product)
        
        posted_platforms = []
        
        for platform, post_content in content.items():
            if self.social_accounts[platform]["status"] == "AKTД°F":
                # SimГјlasyon: Post gГ¶nder
                success = self.simulate_post(platform, post_content, product)
                
                if success:
                    posted_platforms.append(platform)
                    
                    # Post geГ§miЕҹine ekle
                    post_record = {
                        "platform": platform,
                        "product_id": product["id"],
                        "product_name": product["name"],
                        "content": post_content,
                        "posted_at": datetime.now().isoformat(),
                        "status": "PUBLISHED",
                        "engagement": random.randint(10, 500)
                    }
                    self.post_history.append(post_record)
                    
                    print(f"вң… {platform.upper()} paylaЕҹДұmДұ yapДұldДұ: {product['name']}")
                else:
                    print(f"вқҢ {platform.upper()} paylaЕҹДұmДұ baЕҹarДұsДұz: {product['name']}")
        
        # Д°statistikleri gГјncelle
        self.automation_stats["posts_published"] += len(posted_platforms)
        self.automation_stats["last_post"] = datetime.now().isoformat()
        self.automation_stats["engagement_rate"] = random.uniform(3.5, 8.2)
        self.automation_stats["reach_count"] += random.randint(100, 2000) * len(posted_platforms)
        
        return posted_platforms

    def simulate_post(self, platform, content, product):
        """Sosyal medya post simГјlasyonu"""
        # %95 baЕҹarДұ oranДұ
        return random.random() < 0.95

    def automation_loop(self):
        """Ana otomasyon dГ¶ngГјsГј"""
        collection_interval = 300  # 5 dakikada bir ГјrГјn toplama
        post_interval = 180  # 3 dakikada bir paylaЕҹДұm
        last_collection = time.time()
        last_post = time.time()
        
        while self.running:
            try:
                current_time = time.time()
                
                # ГңrГјn toplama zamanДұ geldi mi?
                if current_time - last_collection >= collection_interval:
                    print("рҹ”„ ГңrГјn verileri toplanДұyor...")
                    self.collect_product_data()
                    last_collection = current_time
                
                # Sosyal medya paylaЕҹДұm zamanДұ geldi mi?
                if current_time - last_post >= post_interval and self.product_data:
                    print("рҹ“ұ Sosyal medya paylaЕҹДұmДұ yapДұlДұyor...")
                    
                    # Drive'dan en son ГјrГјnleri Г§ek
                    drive_products = self.fetch_from_drive()
                    if drive_products:
                        # En yГјksek komisyonlu ГјrГјnГј seГ§
                        best_product = max(drive_products, key=lambda x: x["commission_rate"])
                        
                        # Sosyal medyada paylaЕҹ
                        platforms = self.post_to_social_media(best_product)
                        
                        if platforms:
                            print(f"вң… {best_product['name']} {len(platforms)} platformda paylaЕҹДұldДұ")
                    
                    last_post = current_time
                
                time.sleep(30)  # 30 saniye bekle
                
            except Exception as e:
                print(f"вқҢ Otomasyon hatasДұ: {e}")
                time.sleep(60)

    def start_automation(self):
        """Otomasyonu baЕҹlat"""
        automation_thread = threading.Thread(target=self.automation_loop, daemon=True)
        automation_thread.start()

    def get_status_json(self):
        """JSON durum bilgisi dГ¶ndГјr"""
        return json.dumps({
            "automation_status": "AKTД°F" if self.running else "DURDURULDU",
            "product_count": len(self.product_data),
            "social_accounts": self.social_accounts,
            "automation_stats": self.automation_stats,
            "recent_posts": self.post_history[-10:] if self.post_history else [],
            "drive_integration": {
                "folder_id": self.drive_folder_id,
                "last_sync": self.automation_stats["last_collection"],
                "status": "CONNECTED"
            },
            "workflow_status": {
                "collection": "AKTД°F",
                "drive_upload": "AKTД°F", 
                "drive_fetch": "AKTД°F",
                "social_posting": "AKTД°F"
            }
        }, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2)

class DriveSocialAPIHandler(SimpleHTTPRequestHandler):
    def __init__(self, *args, automation_engine=None, **kwargs):
        self.automation_engine = automation_engine
        super().__init__(*args, **kwargs)

    def do_GET(self):
        if self.path == '/drive-social':
            self.serve_html('DRIVE_SOCIAL_PANEL.html')
        elif self.path == '/drive-social/status':
            self.serve_json()
        elif self.path.startswith('/api/'):
            self.handle_api()
        else:
            super().do_GET()

    def serve_html(self, filename):
        """HTML dosyasДұ sun"""
        try:
            with open(filename, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                content = f.read()
            
            self.send_response(200)
            self.send_header('Content-type', 'text/html; charset=utf-8')
            self.end_headers()
            self.wfile.write(content.encode('utf-8'))
        except FileNotFoundError:
            self.send_error(404, "File not found")

    def serve_json(self):
        """JSON veri sun"""
        self.send_response(200)
        self.send_header('Content-type', 'application/json; charset=utf-8')
        self.send_header('Access-Control-Allow-Origin', '*')
        self.end_headers()
        self.wfile.write(self.automation_engine.get_status_json().encode('utf-8'))

    def handle_api(self):
        """API isteklerini yГ¶net"""
        path_parts = self.path.split('/')
        
        if len(path_parts) >= 3:
            action = path_parts[2]
            
            if action == 'collect':
                products = self.automation_engine.collect_product_data()
                self.send_json_response({"status": "success", "products_collected": len(products)})
            elif action == 'post':
                # Rastgele bir ГјrГјnГј paylaЕҹ
                if self.automation_engine.product_data:
                    product = random.choice(self.automation_engine.product_data)
                    platforms = self.automation_engine.post_to_social_media(product)
                    self.send_json_response({"status": "success", "platforms": platforms, "product": product["name"]})
                else:
                    self.send_json_response({"status": "error", "message": "ГңrГјn bulunamadДұ"})
            elif action == 'start':
                self.automation_engine.running = True
                self.send_json_response({"status": "started", "message": "Otomasyon baЕҹlatДұldДұ"})
            elif action == 'stop':
                self.automation_engine.running = False
                self.send_json_response({"status": "stopped", "message": "Otomasyon durduruldu"})
            elif action == 'stats':
                self.send_json_response({"stats": self.automation_engine.automation_stats})
            elif action == 'products':
                self.send_json_response({"products": self.automation_engine.product_data[-20:]})
            elif action == 'posts':
                self.send_json_response({"posts": self.automation_engine.post_history[-20:]})
            else:
                self.send_error(404, "API endpoint not found")

    def send_json_response(self, data):
        """JSON yanДұt gГ¶nder"""
        self.send_response(200)
        self.send_header('Content-type', 'application/json; charset=utf-8')
        self.send_header('Access-Control-Allow-Origin', '*')
        self.end_headers()
        self.wfile.write(json.dumps(data, ensure_ascii=False).encode('utf-8'))

def start_drive_social_server(port, automation_engine):
    """Drive-Sosyal Medya sunucusu baЕҹlat"""
    handler = lambda *args, **kwargs: DriveSocialAPIHandler(*args, automation_engine=automation_engine, **kwargs)
    server = HTTPServer(('localhost', port), handler)
    print(f"вң… Drive-Sosyal Sunucu {port} portunda baЕҹlatДұldДұ")
    server.serve_forever()

def main():
    print("рҹҡҖ ULUSLARARASI TRM FULL OTOMASYON v3.0")
    print("рҹ“Ғ Google Drive вҶ’ Sosyal Medya Otomasyonu")
    print("рҹҢҗ Trend ГңrГјnler Market - Tam Entegrasyon")
    print("=" * 60)
    
    # Drive-Sosyal otomasyon motorunu baЕҹlat
    drive_social_automation = DriveSocialAutomation()
    
    # Sunucuyu baЕҹlat
    port = 9004  # Yeni port
    server_thread = threading.Thread(target=start_drive_social_server, args=(port, drive_social_automation), daemon=True)
    server_thread.start()
    
    print(f"\nвң… Drive-Sosyal Otomasyon BaЕҹlatДұldДұ!")
    print(f"рҹҢҗ Panel: http://localhost:{port}/drive-social")
    print(f"рҹ“Ҡ Status API: http://localhost:{port}/drive-social/status")
    print("\nрҹ”„ Otomasyon AkДұЕҹДұ:")
    print("   1. ГңrГјn verileri toplanДұr")
    print("   2. Google Drive'a yГјklenir")
    print("   3. Drive'dan veriler Г§ekilir")
    print("   4. Sosyal medyada paylaЕҹДұlДұr")
    print("\nрҹ“ұ Aktif Platformlar:")
    for platform, account in drive_social_automation.social_accounts.items():
        if account["status"] == "AKTД°F":
            print(f"   вҖў {platform.title()}: вң…")
    
    print("\nрҹӨ– Tam Otomasyon Aktif!")
    print("рҹ‘Ӣ Durdurmak iГ§in Ctrl+C")
    
    try:
        while True:
            time.sleep(1)
    except KeyboardInterrupt:
        print("\nрҹ‘Ӣ Drive-Sosyal Otomasyon durduruluyor...")
        drive_social_automation.running = False
        print("вң… Otomasyon durduruldu")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

#!/usr/bin/env python3
# -*- coding: utf-8 -*-
"""
TRM Nirvana v3.0 - Google Drive Veri Toplama ve Sosyal Medya Otomatik PaylaЕҹДұm
trendurunlermarket@gmail hesabДұna baДҹlДұ Drive alanДұnda ГјrГјnlerle ilgili tГјm bilgi,
gГ¶rsel ve videolarДұn otomatik olarak toplanmasДұ, ardДұndan gerekli verilerin
Г§ekilerek sosyal medya platformlarДұnda otomatik paylaЕҹДұm yapДұlmasДұ
"""

import asyncio
import logging
import json
import os
import time
from datetime import datetime, timedelta
from typing import Dict, List, Optional
import requests
from googleapiclient.discovery import build
from googleapiclient.http import MediaIoBaseUpload
from google.oauth2.credentials import Credentials
from google_auth_oauthlib.flow import InstalledAppFlow

# Sistem modГјlleri
from ai_integration import AIContentGenerator
from social_media_automation import SocialMediaAutomation

logging.basicConfig(
    level=logging.INFO,
    format='%(asctime)s - %(name)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s',
    handlers=[
        logging.FileHandler('logs/drive_social_manager.log'),
        logging.StreamHandler()
    ]
)
logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)

class DriveSocialManager:
    def __init__(self):
        self.ai_generator = AIContentGenerator()
        self.social_automation = SocialMediaAutomation()
        
        # Google Drive ayarlarДұ
        self.drive_settings = {
            'credentials_file': 'credentials.json',
            'token_file': 'token.json',
            'scopes': ['https://www.googleapis.com/auth/drive'],
            'service_account_file': 'service_account.json'
        }
        
        # Sosyal medya ayarlarДұ
        self.social_settings = {
            'auto_post': True,
            'post_interval': 1800,  # 30 dakika
            'max_daily_posts': 50,
            'platforms': ['facebook', 'instagram', 'twitter', 'tiktok', 'youtube'],
            'content_types': ['image', 'video', 'text', 'story']
        }
        
        # Veri toplama ayarlarДұ
        self.data_collection_settings = {
            'scan_interval': 600,  # 10 dakika
            'file_types': ['jpg', 'jpeg', 'png', 'gif', 'mp4', 'mov', 'avi'],
            'folder_structure': {
                'products': 'TRM_Urunler',
                'images': 'TRM_Gorseller',
                'videos': 'TRM_Videolar',
                'content': 'TRM_Icerikler',
                'posted': 'TRM_Paylasilanlar'
            }
        }
        
        # Drive servisi
        self.drive_service = None
        self.collected_data = []
        self.posted_content = []
        
    async def initialize_drive_service(self):
        """Google Drive servisini baЕҹlat"""
        try:
            logger.info("рҹҢҗ Google Drive servisi baЕҹlatДұlДұyor...")
            
            # Credentials kontrolГј
            creds = None
            if os.path.exists(self.drive_settings['token_file']):
                creds = Credentials.from_authorized_user_file(
                    self.drive_settings['token_file'],
                    self.drive_settings['scopes']
                )
            
            if not creds or not creds.valid:
                if creds and creds.expired and creds.refresh_token:
                    creds.refresh(Request())
                else:
                    flow = InstalledAppFlow.from_client_secrets_file(
                        self.drive_settings['credentials_file'],
                        self.drive_settings['scopes']
                    )
                    creds = flow.run_local_server(port=0)
                
                # Token'Дұ kaydet
                with open(self.drive_settings['token_file'], 'w') as token:
                    token.write(creds.to_json())
            
            # Drive servisi oluЕҹtur
            self.drive_service = build('drive', 'v3', credentials=creds)
            
            logger.info("вң… Google Drive servisi baЕҹlatДұldДұ")
            return True
            
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"вқҢ Google Drive servisi baЕҹlatma hatasДұ: {e}")
            return False
    
    async def scan_drive_for_content(self):
        """Drive'dan iГ§erik tara"""
        try:
            logger.info("рҹ“Ғ Drive iГ§erik taranДұyor...")
            
            collected_items = []
            
            # ГңrГјn klasГ¶rГјnГј tara
            products_folder = await self.find_folder(
                self.data_collection_settings['folder_structure']['products']
            )
            
            if products_folder:
                products = await self.list_files_in_folder(products_folder['id'])
                collected_items.extend(products)
            
            # GГ¶rsel klasГ¶rГјnГј tara
            images_folder = await self.find_folder(
                self.data_collection_settings['folder_structure']['images']
            )
            
            if images_folder:
                images = await self.list_files_in_folder(
                    images_folder['id'], 
                    file_types=self.data_collection_settings['file_types'][:4]  # Sadece gГ¶rseller
                )
                collected_items.extend(images)
            
            # Video klasГ¶rГјnГј tara
            videos_folder = await self.find_folder(
                self.data_collection_settings['folder_structure']['videos']
            )
            
            if videos_folder:
                videos = await self.list_files_in_folder(
                    videos_folder['id'],
                    file_types=self.data_collection_settings['file_types'][4:]  # Sadece videolar
                )
                collected_items.extend(videos)
            
            # Д°Г§erik klasГ¶rГјnГј tara
            content_folder = await self.find_folder(
                self.data_collection_settings['folder_structure']['content']
            )
            
            if content_folder:
                content = await self.list_files_in_folder(content_folder['id'])
                collected_items.extend(content)
            
            self.collected_data = collected_items
            logger.info(f"вң… {len(collected_items)} adet iГ§erik toplandДұ")
            
            return collected_items
            
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"вқҢ Drive iГ§erik tarama hatasДұ: {e}")
            return []
    
    async def find_folder(self, folder_name: str) -> Optional[Dict]:
        """KlasГ¶r bul"""
        try:
            results = self.drive_service.files().list(
                q=f"mimeType='application/vnd.google-apps.folder' and name='{folder_name}'",
                spaces='drive',
                fields='files(id, name, createdTime, modifiedTime)'
            ).execute()
            
            folders = results.get('files', [])
            if folders:
                return folders[0]
            else:
                # KlasГ¶r yoksa oluЕҹtur
                return await self.create_folder(folder_name)
                
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"вқҢ KlasГ¶r bulma hatasДұ: {e}")
            return None
    
    async def create_folder(self, folder_name: str) -> Optional[Dict]:
        """KlasГ¶r oluЕҹtur"""
        try:
            folder_metadata = {
                'name': folder_name,
                'mimeType': 'application/vnd.google-apps.folder'
            }
            
            folder = self.drive_service.files().create(
                body=folder_metadata,
                fields='id, name, createdTime'
            ).execute()
            
            logger.info(f"вң… KlasГ¶r oluЕҹturuldu: {folder_name}")
            return folder
            
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"вқҢ KlasГ¶r oluЕҹturma hatasДұ: {e}")
            return None
    
    async def list_files_in_folder(self, folder_id: str, file_types: List[str] = None) -> List[Dict]:
        """KlasГ¶rdeki dosyalarДұ listele"""
        try:
            query = f"'{folder_id}' in parents"
            
            if file_types:
                file_type_query = " or ".join([f"mimeType contains '{ft}'" for ft in file_types])
                query += f" and ({file_type_query})"
            
            results = self.drive_service.files().list(
                q=query,
                spaces='drive',
                fields='files(id, name, mimeType, size, createdTime, modifiedTime, webViewLink, thumbnailLink)'
            ).execute()
            
            files = results.get('files', [])
            
            # Dosya bilgilerini zenginleЕҹtir
            enriched_files = []
            for file in files:
                enriched_file = {
                    'id': file['id'],
                    'name': file['name'],
                    'mimeType': file['mimeType'],
                    'size': file.get('size', 0),
                    'createdTime': file['createdTime'],
                    'modifiedTime': file['modifiedTime'],
                    'webViewLink': file.get('webViewLink', ''),
                    'thumbnailLink': file.get('thumbnailLink', ''),
                    'folder_id': folder_id,
                    'file_type': self.get_file_type(file['mimeType']),
                    'processed': False,
                    'posted': False
                }
                enriched_files.append(enriched_file)
            
            return enriched_files
            
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"вқҢ Dosya listeleme hatasДұ: {e}")
            return []
    
    def get_file_type(self, mime_type: str) -> str:
        """Dosya tipini belirle"""
        if 'image' in mime_type:
            return 'image'
        elif 'video' in mime_type:
            return 'video'
        elif 'text' in mime_type:
            return 'text'
        else:
            return 'other'
    
    async def process_content_with_ai(self, content_items: List[Dict]) -> List[Dict]:
        """Д°Г§eriДҹi AI ile iЕҹle"""
        try:
            logger.info("рҹӨ– Д°Г§erik AI ile iЕҹleniyor...")
            
            processed_content = []
            
            for item in content_items:
                if not item.get('processed', False):
                    # AI ile iГ§erik analizi
                    ai_analysis = await self.ai_generator.analyze_content(
                        item['name'],
                        item.get('webViewLink', ''),
                        item['file_type']
                    )
                    
                    # AI ile iГ§erik Гјretimi
                    if item['file_type'] in ['image', 'video']:
                        ai_content = await self.ai_generator.generate_social_media_content(
                            item['name'],
                            item['file_type'],
                            ai_analysis
                        )
                    else:
                        ai_content = await self.ai_generator.generate_text_content(
                            item['name'],
                            ai_analysis
                        )
                    
                    processed_item = item.copy()
                    processed_item.update({
                        'processed': True,
                        'ai_analysis': ai_analysis,
                        'ai_content': ai_content,
                        'processed_time': datetime.now().isoformat()
                    })
                    
                    processed_content.append(processed_item)
                else:
                    processed_content.append(item)
            
            logger.info(f"вң… {len(processed_content)} adet iГ§erik iЕҹlendi")
            return processed_content
            
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"вқҢ AI iГ§erik iЕҹleme hatasДұ: {e}")
            return content_items
    
    async def post_to_social_media(self, content_items: List[Dict]) -> List[Dict]:
        """Sosyal medyada paylaЕҹ"""
        try:
            logger.info("рҹ“ұ Sosyal medyada paylaЕҹДұlДұyor...")
            
            posted_items = []
            daily_post_count = len([p for p in self.posted_content 
                                  if datetime.fromisoformat(p['post_time']).date() == datetime.now().date()])
            
            for item in content_items:
                if (not item.get('posted', False) and 
                    daily_post_count < self.social_settings['max_daily_posts'] and
                    self.social_settings['auto_post']):
                    
                    # Sosyal medya paylaЕҹДұmДұ
                    post_result = await self.social_automation.post_content(
                        item['ai_content'],
                        item['file_type'],
                        item.get('webViewLink', ''),
                        self.social_settings['platforms']
                    )
                    
                    posted_item = item.copy()
                    posted_item.update({
                        'posted': True,
                        'post_time': datetime.now().isoformat(),
                        'post_result': post_result,
                        'platforms': post_result.get('posted_platforms', [])
                    })
                    
                    posted_items.append(posted_item)
                    daily_post_count += 1
                    
                    # PaylaЕҹДұlan dosyayДұ posted klasГ¶rГјne taЕҹДұ
                    await self.move_to_posted_folder(item['id'])
                    
                    # PaylaЕҹДұm aralДұДҹДұ
                    await asyncio.sleep(self.social_settings['post_interval'])
                else:
                    posted_items.append(item)
            
            self.posted_content = posted_items
            logger.info(f"вң… {len([p for p in posted_items if p['posted']])} adet iГ§erik paylaЕҹДұldДұ")
            
            return posted_items
            
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"вқҢ Sosyal medya paylaЕҹДұm hatasДұ: {e}")
            return content_items
    
    async def move_to_posted_folder(self, file_id: str):
        """DosyayДұ paylaЕҹДұlanlar klasГ¶rГјne taЕҹДұ"""
        try:
            posted_folder = await self.find_folder(
                self.data_collection_settings['folder_structure']['posted']
            )
            
            if posted_folder:
                # DosyayДұ taЕҹДұ
                self.drive_service.files().update(
                    fileId=file_id,
                    addParents=[posted_folder['id']],
                    removeParents=[self.get_file_folder(file_id)]
                ).execute()
                
                logger.info(f"вң… Dosya paylaЕҹДұlanlar klasГ¶rГјne taЕҹДұndДұ: {file_id}")
                
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"вқҢ Dosya taЕҹДұma hatasДұ: {e}")
    
    def get_file_folder(self, file_id: str) -> str:
        """DosyanДұn bulunduДҹu klasГ¶rГј al"""
        try:
            file = self.drive_service.files().get(
                fileId=file_id,
                fields='parents'
            ).execute()
            
            if file.get('parents'):
                return file['parents'][0]
            return None
            
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"вқҢ Dosya klasГ¶rГј alma hatasДұ: {e}")
            return None
    
    async def update_dashboard_data(self):
        """Panel verilerini gГјncelle"""
        try:
            dashboard_data = {
                'total_collected': len(self.collected_data),
                'total_posted': len([p for p in self.posted_content if p['posted']]),
                'daily_posts': len([p for p in self.posted_content 
                                   if datetime.fromisoformat(p['post_time']).date() == datetime.now().date()]),
                'last_collection': datetime.now().isoformat(),
                'last_post': None,
                'platform_status': {},
                'content_types': {
                    'images': len([c for c in self.collected_data if c['file_type'] == 'image']),
                    'videos': len([c for c in self.collected_data if c['file_type'] == 'video']),
                    'text': len([c for c in self.collected_data if c['file_type'] == 'text'])
                }
            }
            
            # Son paylaЕҹДұm zamanДұ
            posted_items = [p for p in self.posted_content if p['posted']]
            if posted_items:
                dashboard_data['last_post'] = max(p['post_time'] for p in posted_items)
            
            # Platform durumlarДұ
            for platform in self.social_settings['platforms']:
                dashboard_data['platform_status'][platform] = await self.social_automation.get_platform_status(platform)
            
            # Dashboard verisini kaydet
            with open('drive_social_dashboard.json', 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                json.dump(dashboard_data, f, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2)
            
            logger.info("вң… Dashboard verileri gГјncellendi")
            
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"вқҢ Dashboard verileri gГјncelleme hatasДұ: {e}")
    
    async def run_continuous_collection(self):
        """SГјrekli veri toplama ve paylaЕҹДұm"""
        try:
            logger.info("рҹ”„ SГјrekli veri toplama ve paylaЕҹДұm baЕҹlatДұlДұyor...")
            
            while True:
                try:
                    # Drive'dan iГ§erik tara
                    new_content = await self.scan_drive_for_content()
                    
                    # Yeni iГ§erik varsa iЕҹle
                    if new_content:
                        # AI ile iЕҹle
                        processed_content = await self.process_content_with_ai(new_content)
                        
                        # Sosyal medyada paylaЕҹ
                        posted_content = await self.post_to_social_media(processed_content)
                        
                        # Dashboard'Дұ gГјncelle
                        await self.update_dashboard_data()
                    
                    # Belirtilen aralДұkta bekle
                    await asyncio.sleep(self.data_collection_settings['scan_interval'])
                    
                except Exception as e:
                    logger.error(f"вқҢ SГјrekli toplama dГ¶ngГј hatasДұ: {e}")
                    await asyncio.sleep(60)  # Hata durumunda 1 dakika bekle
                    
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"вқҢ SГјrekli toplama baЕҹlatma hatasДұ: {e}")
    
    def get_system_status(self) -> Dict:
        """Sistem durumunu al"""
        return {
            'drive_service_active': self.drive_service is not None,
            'total_collected': len(self.collected_data),
            'total_posted': len([p for p in self.posted_content if p['posted']]),
            'daily_posts': len([p for p in self.posted_content 
                               if datetime.fromisoformat(p['post_time']).date() == datetime.now().date()]),
            'last_collection': max([c['createdTime'] for c in self.collected_data]) if self.collected_data else None,
            'last_post': max([p['post_time'] for p in self.posted_content if p['posted']]) if self.posted_content else None,
            'auto_post_enabled': self.social_settings['auto_post'],
            'scan_interval': self.data_collection_settings['scan_interval'],
            'post_interval': self.social_settings['post_interval']
        }

# Ana baЕҹlatДұcДұ
async def main():
    """Ana fonksiyon"""
    print("""
===============================================
    TRM NIRVANA v3.0 - DRIVE VE SOSYAL MEDYA
===============================================
  рҹ“Ғ Google Drive Veri Toplama
  рҹӨ– AI Д°Г§erik Д°Еҹleme
  рҹ“ұ Sosyal Medya Otomatik PaylaЕҹДұm
  рҹ“Ҡ GerГ§ek ZamanlДұ Dashboard
  рҹ”„ SГјrekli Veri AkДұЕҹДұ
===============================================
    """)
    
    # Drive ve sosyal medya yГ¶neticisi oluЕҹtur
    drive_social_manager = DriveSocialManager()
    
    try:
        # Google Drive servisini baЕҹlat
        if await drive_social_manager.initialize_drive_service():
            logger.info("рҹҡҖ Drive ve sosyal medya sistemi baЕҹlatДұlДұyor...")
            
            # SГјrekli veri toplama ve paylaЕҹДұmДұ baЕҹlat
            await drive_social_manager.run_continuous_collection()
        else:
            logger.error("вқҢ Google Drive servisi baЕҹlatДұlamadДұ")
            
    except KeyboardInterrupt:
        logger.info("рҹ‘Ӣ Drive ve sosyal medya sistemi durduruldu")
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"вқҢ Ana sistem hatasДұ: {e}")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    asyncio.run(main())
