import csv
import os
from datetime import datetime

# ============================================
# ENGELLД° EKД°P YГ–NETД°M SД°STEMД°
# ============================================

TEAM_FILE = "team_list.csv"

# ============================================
# 1. YENД° EKД°P ГңYESД° EKLEME
# ============================================
def add_team_member(name, disability, platform, account, iban, commission_rate):
    """Yeni engelli ekip Гјyesi ekler"""
    
    # Dosya yoksa baЕҹlДұklarДұ oluЕҹtur
    if not os.path.exists(TEAM_FILE):
        with open(TEAM_FILE, 'w', newline='', encoding='utf-8') as f:
            writer = csv.writer(f)
            writer.writerow(['ID', 'Ad Soyad', 'Engel Durumu', 'Platform', 
                            'Hesap', 'IBAN', 'Komisyon %', 'KayДұt Tarihi', 'Toplam KazanГ§'])
    
    # Yeni ID oluЕҹtur
    with open(TEAM_FILE, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
        reader = csv.reader(f)
        next(reader)  # BaЕҹlДұДҹДұ atla
        rows = list(reader)
        new_id = len(rows) + 1001
    
    # Yeni Гјyeyi ekle
    with open(TEAM_FILE, 'a', newline='', encoding='utf-8') as f:
        writer = csv.writer(f)
        writer.writerow([
            new_id, name, disability, platform, account, 
            iban, commission_rate, datetime.now().strftime("%d.%m.%Y"), 0
        ])
    
    print(f"вң… Yeni Гјye eklendi: {name} (ID: {new_id})")
    return new_id

# ============================================
# 2. EKД°P LД°STESД°NД° GГ–STER
# ============================================
def show_team():
    """TГјm ekip Гјyelerini listeler"""
    
    if not os.path.exists(TEAM_FILE):
        print("вҡ пёҸ HenГјz ekip Гјyesi yok!")
        return
    
    with open(TEAM_FILE, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
        reader = csv.reader(f)
        rows = list(reader)
    
    if len(rows) <= 1:
        print("вҡ пёҸ HenГјz ekip Гјyesi yok!")
        return
    
    print("\n" + "="*80)
    print(f"рҹ‘Ҙ ENGELLД° EKД°P LД°STESД° - {len(rows)-1} KД°ЕһД°")
    print("="*80)
    
    for row in rows[1:]:  # BaЕҹlДұДҹДұ atla
        print(f"рҹҶ” {row[0]} | {row[1]} | {row[2]} | {row[3]} | {row[4]} | {row[7]} TL")

# ============================================
# 3. KOMД°SYON EKLE
# ============================================
def add_commission(member_id, sale_amount):
    """SatДұЕҹtan komisyon ekler"""
    
    if not os.path.exists(TEAM_FILE):
        print("вқҢ Ekip listesi bulunamadДұ!")
        return
    
    # DosyayДұ oku
    with open(TEAM_FILE, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
        rows = list(csv.reader(f))
    
    # Гңyeyi bul
    found = False
    for i, row in enumerate(rows):
        if i > 0 and row[0] == str(member_id):  # BaЕҹlДұk deДҹilse ve ID eЕҹleЕҹiyorsa
            commission_rate = float(row[6])
            commission = sale_amount * commission_rate / 100
            current_total = float(row[8])
            row[8] = str(current_total + commission)
            found = True
            print(f"рҹ’° {row[1]}'e {commission} TL komisyon eklendi (Toplam: {row[8]} TL)")
            break
    
    if not found:
        print(f"вқҢ ID {member_id} bulunamadДұ!")
        return
    
    # DosyayДұ gГјncelle
    with open(TEAM_FILE, 'w', newline='', encoding='utf-8') as f:
        writer = csv.writer(f)
        writer.writerows(rows)

# ============================================
# 4. AYLIK Г–DEME RAPORU
# ============================================
def payment_report():
    """AylДұk Г¶deme raporu hazДұrlar"""
    
    if not os.path.exists(TEAM_FILE):
        print("вҡ пёҸ Ekip listesi yok!")
        return
    
    with open(TEAM_FILE, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
        reader = csv.reader(f)
        rows = list(reader)
    
    if len(rows) <= 1:
        print("вҡ пёҸ Ekip Гјyesi yok!")
        return
    
    print("\n" + "="*80)
    print(f"рҹ’° AYLIK Г–DEME RAPORU - {datetime.now().strftime('%B %Y')}")
    print("="*80)
    
    total = 0
    for row in rows[1:]:
        print(f"рҹҶ” {row[0]} | {row[1]} | IBAN: {row[5]} | {row[8]} TL")
        total += float(row[8])
    
    print("="*80)
    print(f"TOPLAM Г–DEME: {total} TL")
    
    # Г–deme yapДұldДұktan sonra sДұfДұrla
    confirm = input("\nГ–demeler yapДұldДұ mДұ? (e/h): ")
    if confirm.lower() == 'e':
        for i in range(1, len(rows)):
            rows[i][8] = '0'
        
        with open(TEAM_FILE, 'w', newline='', encoding='utf-8') as f:
            writer = csv.writer(f)
            writer.writerows(rows)
        print("вң… Г–demeler yapДұldДұ, hesaplar sДұfДұrlandДұ!")

# ============================================
# 5. TEST KOMUTLARI
# ============================================
if __name__ == "__main__":
    print("рҹҡҖ ENGELLД° EKД°P YГ–NETД°M SД°STEMД°")
    print("="*40)
    
    while True:
        print("\n1пёҸвғЈ Yeni Гјye ekle")
        print("2пёҸвғЈ Ekip listesini gГ¶ster")

        print("4пёҸвғЈ AylДұk Г¶deme raporu")

        choice = input("\nSeГ§iminiz: ")

            platform = input("Platform: ")

            rate = float(input("Komisyon oranДұ (%): "))
            add_team_member(name, disability, platform, account, iban, rate)

            show_team()

            member_id = input("Гңye ID: ")
            amount = float(input("SatДұЕҹ tutarДұ (TL): "))
            add_commission(member_id, amount)

            payment_report()

            print("рҹ‘Ӣ GГ¶rГјЕҹmek Гјzere!")

# team_social_accounts.py
from team_manager import TeamManager

class TeamSocialAccounts:
    def __init__(self):
        self.team = TeamManager()
        self.ekip_hesaplari = []
    
    def ekip_hesabi_ekle(self, uye_id, platform, kullanici_adi, sifre):
        """Engelli ekip Гјyesinin sosyal medya hesabДұnДұ ekler"""
        
        self.ekip_hesaplari.append({
            'uye_id': uye_id,
            'platform': platform,
            'kullanici_adi': kullanici_adi,
            'sifre': sifre  # Еһifreler gГјvenli Еҹekilde saklanmalДұ!
        })
        print(f"вң… {platform} hesabДұ ekip Гјyesine baДҹlandДұ")
    
    def ekip_hesabiyla_paylas(self, platform, urun):
        """Belirli bir ekip Гјyesinin hesabДұndan paylaЕҹДұm yapar"""
        
        for hesap in self.ekip_hesaplari:
            if hesap['platform'] == platform:
                print(f"рҹ‘Ө {hesap['kullanici_adi']} hesabДұndan paylaЕҹДұlДұyor...")
                # PaylaЕҹДұm kodu burada olacak
                # Komisyon otomatik hesaplanacak
                return True
        return False

# ============================================
# AI DESTEKLД° TELEGRAM MГңЕһTERД° ASД°STANI
# Claude API ile akДұllДұ cevaplar
# ============================================

import os
import telebot
import anthropic
from dotenv import load_dotenv

load_dotenv()

TOKEN = os.getenv('TELEGRAM_BOT_TOKEN')
CLAUDE_API_KEY = os.getenv('CLAUDE_API_KEY')

bot = telebot.TeleBot(TOKEN)
claude = anthropic.Anthropic(api_key=CLAUDE_API_KEY)

@bot.message_handler(commands=['start', 'help'])
def send_welcome(message):
    welcome_text = (
        "рҹӨ– Merhaba! Ben TRM AI Asistan.\n\n"
        "Bana istediДҹin soruyu sorabilirsin: ГјrГјnler, fiyatlar, kargo, stok...\n"
        "Hemen cevaplayayДұm! рҹ’¬"
    )
    bot.reply_to(message, welcome_text)

@bot.message_handler(commands=['urunler'])
def send_products(message):
    # ГңrГјn listesini buraya ekleyebilirsin (isteДҹe baДҹlДұ)
    urunler = """
    рҹӣҚпёҸ PopГјler ГңrГјnlerimiz:
    - Xiaomi AkДұllДұ Bileklik - 449 TL
    - ChefMax DoДҹrayДұcДұ - 449 TL
    - Korkmaz Tava - 199 TL
    - Termal ГҮorap - 49 TL
    """
    bot.reply_to(message, urunler)

@bot.message_handler(func=lambda m: True)
def ai_responder(message):
    """Gelen her mesajДұ Claude'a sor ve cevap ver"""
    try:
        # KullanДұcДұ mesajДұnДұ al
        user_message = message.text
        
        # Claude'a sor
        prompt = f"""
        Bir mГјЕҹteri soru soruyor. Nazik, yardДұmsever ve kДұsa cevap ver.
        MГјЕҹteri: {user_message}
        
        Cevap:
        """
        
        response = claude.messages.create(
            model="claude-3-sonnet-20241022",
            max_tokens=300,
            temperature=0.7,
            messages=[{"role": "user", "content": prompt}]
        )
        
        answer = response.content[0].text.strip()
        
        # CevabДұ gГ¶nder
        bot.reply_to(message, answer)
        
    except Exception as e:
        bot.reply_to(message, "рҹҳ” Еһu anda teknik bir sorun var. LГјtfen daha sonra tekrar dene.")
        print(f"Hata: {e}")

print("рҹӨ– AI Asistan baЕҹlatДұldДұ...")
bot.infinity_polling()

#!/usr/bin/env python3
# -*- coding: utf-8 -*-
"""
TRM Telegram Dinleyici - TedarikГ§i gruplarДұndan ГјrГјn yakalama
"""

import asyncio
import logging
import re
import json
import os
from datetime import datetime
from typing import List, Dict, Optional

# Telethon import - eДҹer yoksa mock kullan
try:
    from telethon import TelegramClient, events
    from telethon.tl.types import MessageMediaPhoto, MessageMediaDocument
    TELETHON_AVAILABLE = True
except ImportError:
    TELETHON_AVAILABLE = False
    print("вҡ пёҸ Telethon kurulu deДҹil. Mock mod kullanДұlacak.")
    # Stub'lar - mock modda NameError olmamasДұ iГ§in
    class _StubEvents:
        class NewMessage: pass
    events = _StubEvents()
    class MessageMediaPhoto: pass
    class MessageMediaDocument: pass

logging.basicConfig(level=logging.INFO)
logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)

class MockTelegramClient:
    """Mock Telegram client for testing"""
    def __init__(self, *args, **kwargs):
        self.session_name = kwargs.get('session', 'mock_session')
        
    async def start(self, phone=None):
        logger.info(f"Mock Telegram client baЕҹlatДұldДұ: {self.session_name}")
        return True
        
    async def disconnect(self):
        logger.info("Mock Telegram client kapatДұldДұ")
        
    def add_event_handler(self, handler, event_type=None):
        logger.info("Mock event handler eklendi")
        
    async def run_until_disconnected(self):
        while True:
            await asyncio.sleep(10)
            logger.info("Mock Telegram dinliyor...")

class TelegramProductListener:
    def __init__(self, api_id=None, api_hash=None, phone=None, session_name="trm_session"):
        self.api_id = api_id or os.getenv("TELEGRAM_API_ID", "")
        self.api_hash = api_hash or os.getenv("TELEGRAM_API_HASH", "")
        self.phone = phone or os.getenv("TELEGRAM_PHONE", "")
        self.session_name = session_name
        
        if TELETHON_AVAILABLE and self.api_id and self.api_hash:
            self.client = TelegramClient(session_name, self.api_id, self.api_hash)
        else:
            self.client = MockTelegramClient(session=session_name)
            
        self.captured_products = []
        self.commission_keywords = [
            r"%\d+",  # %25, %30 gibi
            r"komisyon",
            r"indirim", 
            r"fДұrsat",
            r"kampanya",
            r"yГјzde",
            r"discount"
        ]
        
        # Telegram kaynak kanallarДұ
        self.telegram_sources = [
            "magazanolsunresmi",
            "trendyolkampanya",
            "trendyolindirimleri",
            "hepsiburadakampanya",
            "amazonturkiyefirsat",
            "n11kampanyalari",
            "akakce_kampanya",
            "urunlerim_affiliate",
            "komisyonlu_urunler",
            "afiliyet_marketing_tr",
            "trendurunler", 
            "ucuzurunler",
            "indirimkosesi",
            "trendurunlermarket"
        ]
        
    async def start(self):
        """Telegram client'ДұnДұ baЕҹlat"""
        try:
            await self.client.start(phone=self.phone)
            logger.info("Telegram client baЕҹlatДұldДұ")
            
            # Mesaj dinleyicilerini kur
            self.client.add_event_handler(self.handle_new_message, events.NewMessage)
            
            logger.info(f"Takip edilen kanallar: {self.telegram_sources}")
            
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Telegram baЕҹlatma hatasДұ: {e}")
            raise
    
    async def handle_new_message(self, event):
        """Yeni mesajlarДұ iЕҹle - gerГ§ek parser kullanarak"""
        from telegram_parser import parse_telegram_message
        from trm_tracking import record_product

        message = event.message
        text = message.text or ""

        # Kanal kontrolГј
        channel = "unknown"
        if hasattr(event, 'chat') and hasattr(event.chat, 'username'):
            channel = event.chat.username
            if channel not in self.telegram_sources:
                return
        elif hasattr(message, 'peer_id'):
            channel = str(getattr(message.peer_id, 'channel_id', 'unknown'))

        try:
            # Medya URL'lerini topla
            media_urls = []
            if hasattr(message, 'media') and message.media:
                if isinstance(message.media, MessageMediaPhoto):
                    media_urls.append(f"photo_{message.id}.jpg")
                elif isinstance(message.media, MessageMediaDocument):
                    media_urls.append(f"doc_{message.id}.mp4")

            # YENД°: GeliЕҹmiЕҹ parser
            product_data = parse_telegram_message(
                text=text,
                channel=channel,
                message_id=message.id,
                media_urls=media_urls
            )

            if not product_data:
                return  # ГңrГјn bilgisi yetersiz

            # YГјksek komisyonlu ГјrГјnleri logla
            if product_data['commission_rate'] >= 20.0:
                logger.info(
                    f"рҹ’° YГјksek komisyonlu ГјrГјn: {product_data['title'][:50]} "
                    f"(%{product_data['commission_rate']}, {product_data['price']} TL)"
                )

            self.captured_products.append(product_data)

            # SQLite tracking DB'ye kaydet
            product_id = record_product(product_data)
            if product_id:
                product_data['db_id'] = product_id
                logger.info(f"рҹ“Ҡ Tracking DB ID: {product_id}")

            # JSON kuyruДҹa da ekle (orchestrator iГ§in)
            await self.queue_product_for_processing(product_data)

        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Mesaj iЕҹleme hatasДұ: {e}", exc_info=True)
    
    async def extract_product_data(self, message) -> Optional[Dict]:
        """Mesajdan ГјrГјn bilgilerini Г§Дұkar"""
        if not message.text and not hasattr(message, 'media'):
            return None
            
        product_data = {
            'title': '',
            'description': '',
            'price': '',
            'media_urls': [],
            'links': []
        }
        
        # Metin iГ§eriДҹini iЕҹle
        text = message.text or ""
        
        # BaЕҹlДұДҹДұ Г§Дұkar (ilk satДұr genellikle baЕҹlДұktДұr)
        lines = text.split('\n')
        if lines:
            product_data['title'] = lines[0].strip()
            product_data['description'] = '\n'.join(lines[1:]).strip()
        
        # Fiyat bilgilerini Г§Дұkar
        price_patterns = [
            r'(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)\s*TL',
            r'(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)\s*вӮә',
            r'(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)\s*tГјrk lirasДұ',
            r'(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)\s*lira',
            r'(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)\s*try'
        ]
        
        for pattern in price_patterns:
            match = re.search(pattern, text, re.IGNORECASE)
            if match:
                product_data['price'] = match.group(1)
                break
        
        # Linkleri Г§Дұkar
        url_pattern = r'https?://[^\s<>"{}|\\^`[\]]+'
        urls = re.findall(url_pattern, text)
        product_data['links'] = urls
        
        # Medya dosyalarДұnДұ iЕҹle
        if hasattr(message, 'media') and message.media:
            if isinstance(message.media, MessageMediaPhoto):
                # FotoДҹraf iГ§in mock URL
                product_data['media_urls'].append(f"photo_{message.id}.jpg")
                
            elif isinstance(message.media, MessageMediaDocument):
                # Video veya diДҹer dosyalar iГ§in mock URL
                product_data['media_urls'].append(f"doc_{message.id}.mp4")
        
        return product_data if product_data['title'] else None
    
    def extract_commission_rate(self, text: str) -> Optional[float]:
        """Metinden komisyon oranДұnДұ Г§Дұkar"""
        text_lower = text.lower()
        
        for keyword in self.commission_keywords:
            if keyword in text_lower:
                # SayДұsal deДҹeri bul
                number_pattern = r'(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)'
                matches = re.findall(number_pattern, text)
                if matches:
                    try:
                        # YГјzde iЕҹareti varsa onu kullan
                        if '%' in text:
                            for match in matches:
                                if int(match) <= 100:  # %100'den kГјГ§Гјk olmalДұ
                                    return float(match)
                        else:
                            # Komisyon kelimesi geГ§iyorsa ilk sayДұyДұ al
                            return float(matches[0])
                    except ValueError:
                        continue
        return None
    
    async def queue_product_for_processing(self, product_data: Dict):
        """ГңrГјnГј iЕҹleme kuyruДҹuna ekle (file-lock korumalДұ)"""
        from trm_utils import safe_append_to_queue
        queue_file = "product_queue.json"

        if safe_append_to_queue(queue_file, product_data):
            logger.info(f"ГңrГјn iЕҹleme kuyruДҹuna eklendi: {product_data['title']}")
        else:
            logger.error(f"ГңrГјn kuyruДҹa eklenemedi: {product_data['title']}")
    
    async def run(self):
        """Ana Г§alДұЕҹma dГ¶ngГјsГј"""
        await self.start()
        logger.info("Telegram dinleyici Г§alДұЕҹДұyor...")
        
        try:
            await self.client.run_until_disconnected()
        except KeyboardInterrupt:
            logger.info("Telegram dinleyici durduruluyor")
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Telegram dinleyici hatasДұ: {e}")
        finally:
            if hasattr(self.client, 'disconnect'):
                await self.client.disconnect()

# Test ve Г¶rnek kullanДұm
async def test_telegram_listener():
    """Telegram dinleyiciyi test et"""
    listener = TelegramProductListener()
    logger.info("Telegram dinleyici test ediliyor...")
    
    # Test ГјrГјnГј ekle
    test_product = {
        'title': 'Test ГңrГјnГј - %25 Komisyon',
        'description': 'Harika bir test ГјrГјnГј',
        'price': '299 TL',
        'commission_rate': 25,
        'priority': 'high',
        'captured_at': datetime.now().isoformat(),
        'source': 'test',
        'message_id': 999
    }
    
    await listener.queue_product_for_processing(test_product)
    logger.info("Test ГјrГјnГј kuyruДҹa eklendi")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    asyncio.run(test_telegram_listener())


C:\Users\Habitat\Desktop\KURESEL_IMECE_DUNYASI>(echo.   & echo ==========================================   & echo DOSYA: telegram_parser.py   & echo ==========================================   & echo.   & type "telegram_parser.py"   & echo.)

#!/usr/bin/env python3
# -*- coding: utf-8 -*-
"""
TRM Telegram Mesaj Parser - v2.0 STABLE
GerГ§ek e-ticaret/affiliate kanallarДұnДұn mesaj formatlarДұnДұ parse eder.

DГјzeltmeler (v2.0):
  - Encoding: NFC normalize + cp1252вҶ’utf-8 otomatik onarДұm
  - Fiyat regex: binlik nokta (1.299 TL) vs kuruЕҹ virgГјl (1.299,50 TL) ayrДұmДұ
  - Komisyon regex: sДұkДұ baДҹlam вҖ” indirim yГјzdelerini yanlДұЕҹ eЕҹlemez
  - URL temizleme: trailing noktalama kaldДұrma
  - parse_old_price: eski/Г§izili fiyatДұ da Г§Дұkar
  - Г–ncelik: kazanГ§ potansiyeli = fiyat Г— komisyon/100
  - parse_batch: Г§oklu mesaj, Г¶ncelik sДұralamasДұ
"""

import re
import unicodedata
from datetime import datetime
from typing import Dict, List, Optional

# в”Җв”Җ REGEX PANELД° в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ

COMMISSION_PATTERNS = [
    re.compile(
        r'(?:komisyon|kazanГ§|kazanc|kГўr|kar)\s*[:\-]?\s*%?\s*(\d{1,2}(?:[.,]\d+)?)\s*%?',
        re.IGNORECASE | re.UNICODE,
    ),
    re.compile(
        r'%\s*(\d{1,2}(?:[.,]\d+)?)\s*(?:komisyon|kazanГ§|kazanc|kГўr)',
        re.IGNORECASE | re.UNICODE,
    ),
]

DISCOUNT_PATTERNS = [
    re.compile(
        r'(?:indirim|tasarruf|kampanya)\s*[:\-]?\s*%?\s*(\d{1,2})\s*%?',
        re.IGNORECASE | re.UNICODE,
    ),
    re.compile(
        r'%\s*(\d{1,2})\s*(?:indirim|Д°NDД°RД°M|kampanya|off)',
        re.IGNORECASE | re.UNICODE,
    ),
    re.compile(
        r'(?:^|\s)%(\d{1,2})\s+(?:indirim|Д°NDД°RД°M)',
        re.IGNORECASE | re.UNICODE | re.MULTILINE,
    ),
]

_AMOUNT = r'(\d{1,3}(?:[.\s]\d{3})*(?:,\d{1,2})?|\d+(?:,\d{1,2})?)'
PRICE_PATTERNS = [
    re.compile(_AMOUNT + r'\s*(?:tl|вӮә|try|tГјrk\s*lirasДұ|lira)\b', re.IGNORECASE | re.UNICODE),
    re.compile(r'(?:tl|вӮә|try)\s*' + _AMOUNT, re.IGNORECASE | re.UNICODE),
    re.compile(r'(?:fiyat|sadece|yalnДұzca|yalnizca)\s*[:\-]?\s*' + _AMOUNT, re.IGNORECASE | re.UNICODE),
]

OLD_PRICE_PATTERNS = [
    re.compile(r'(?:eski|normal|liste|was|before)\s*:?\s*' + _AMOUNT + r'\s*(?:tl|вӮә|try)?', re.IGNORECASE | re.UNICODE),
    re.compile(r'~~' + _AMOUNT + r'\s*(?:tl|вӮә|try)?~~', re.IGNORECASE | re.UNICODE),
    re.compile(r'\(' + _AMOUNT + r'\s*(?:tl|вӮә|try)\)', re.IGNORECASE | re.UNICODE),
]

URL_PATTERN  = re.compile(r'https?://[^\s<>"{}|\\^`\[\]]+')
TRAIL_PUNCT  = re.compile(r'[.,;!?)]+$')

ECOMMERCE_DOMAINS = [
    'trendyol.com', 'hepsiburada.com', 'n11.com', 'amazon.com.tr',
    'gittigidiyor.com', 'cimri.com', 'akakce.com', 'aliexpress.com',
    'tr.aliexpress.com', 'shopee.com', 'amazon.com', 'magazanolsun.com',
    'pttavm.com', 'ciceksepeti.com', 'ebay.com', 'sahibinden.com',
]

EMOJI_RE = re.compile(
    "[\U0001F300-\U0001F9FF\U0001FA00-\U0001FA9F\U00002600-\U000027BF\U0000FE00-\U0000FE0F]+",
    flags=re.UNICODE,
)

# в”Җв”Җ YARDIMCILAR в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ

def _normalize_amount(raw: str) -> Optional[float]:
    s = raw.strip().replace(' ', '')
    if ',' in s:
        int_part, dec_part = s.rsplit(',', 1)
        int_part = int_part.replace('.', '')
        s = f"{int_part}.{dec_part}"
    else:
        parts = s.split('.')
        if len(parts) == 2 and len(parts[1]) <= 2:
            pass  # gerГ§ek kuruЕҹ
        else:
            s = s.replace('.', '')
    try:
        return float(s)
    except ValueError:
        return None


def _clean_url(url: str) -> str:
    return TRAIL_PUNCT.sub('', url)


def safe_str(text: str) -> str:
    """UTF-8 gГјvenliДҹi + cp1252 bozulma onarДұmДұ + NFC normalize."""
    if not isinstance(text, str):
        try:
            text = text.decode('utf-8', errors='replace')
        except Exception:
            text = str(text)
    try:
        text = text.encode('latin-1').decode('utf-8')
    except (UnicodeEncodeError, UnicodeDecodeError):
        pass
    return unicodedata.normalize('NFC', text)

# в”Җв”Җ PARSE FONKSД°YONLARI в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ

def parse_price(text: str) -> Optional[float]:
    text = safe_str(text)
    candidates = []
    for pat in PRICE_PATTERNS:
        for m in pat.finditer(text):
            v = _normalize_amount(m.group(1))
            if v and 1.0 <= v <= 1_000_000.0:
                candidates.append(v)
    return min(candidates) if candidates else None


def parse_old_price(text: str) -> Optional[float]:
    text = safe_str(text)
    for pat in OLD_PRICE_PATTERNS:
        for m in pat.finditer(text):
            v = _normalize_amount(m.group(1))
            if v and 1.0 <= v <= 1_000_000.0:
                return v
    return None


def parse_commission(text: str) -> Optional[float]:
    text = safe_str(text)
    for pat in COMMISSION_PATTERNS:
        for m in pat.finditer(text):
            try:
                v = float(m.group(1).replace(',', '.'))
                if 1.0 <= v <= 99.0:
                    return v
            except ValueError:
                pass
    return None


def parse_discount(text: str) -> Optional[float]:
    text = safe_str(text)
    for pat in DISCOUNT_PATTERNS:
        for m in pat.finditer(text):
            try:
                v = float(m.group(1))
                if 1.0 <= v <= 99.0:
                    return v
            except ValueError:
                pass
    return None


def parse_urls(text: str) -> List[str]:
    text = safe_str(text)
    raw = URL_PATTERN.findall(text)
    cleaned = list(dict.fromkeys(_clean_url(u) for u in raw if len(_clean_url(u)) > 10))
    def _key(u):
        for i, d in enumerate(ECOMMERCE_DOMAINS):
            if d in u.lower():
                return i
        return 999
    return sorted(cleaned, key=_key)


def parse_title(text: str) -> str:
    text = safe_str(text)
    lines = [ln.strip() for ln in text.split('\n') if ln.strip()]
    if not lines:
        return ""
    def _clean(ln):
        ln = EMOJI_RE.sub('', ln).strip()
        ln = URL_PATTERN.sub('', ln).strip()
        ln = re.sub(r'\s+', ' ', ln)
        return ln.strip('в”ҖвҖ”-:|вҖўВ·').strip()
    for ln in lines:
        t = _clean(ln)
        if len(t) >= 5:
            return t[:250]
    return ""

# в”Җв”Җ ANA PARSE в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ

def parse_telegram_message(
    text: str,
    channel: str = "",
    message_id: int = 0,
    media_urls: Optional[List[str]] = None,
) -> Optional[Dict]:
    if not text or len(text.strip()) < 5:
        return None
    text = safe_str(text)
    title      = parse_title(text)
    price      = parse_price(text)
    old_price  = parse_old_price(text)
    commission = parse_commission(text)
    discount   = parse_discount(text)
    urls       = parse_urls(text)

    if not title:
        return None
    if not (price or commission or urls):
        return None

    desc_lines = []
    for ln in text.split('\n')[1:]:
        c = EMOJI_RE.sub('', ln).strip()
        c = URL_PATTERN.sub('', c).strip()
        if c:
            desc_lines.append(c)
    description = '\n'.join(desc_lines)[:1000]

    earning = round((price or 0) * (commission or 0) / 100, 2)

    if earning >= 200:
        priority = 'urgent'
    elif commission and commission >= 25:
        priority = 'high'
    elif commission and commission >= 15:
        priority = 'medium'
    elif discount and discount >= 50:
        priority = 'medium'
    else:
        priority = 'low'

    return {
        'title':             title,
        'description':       description,
        'price':             str(price) if price else '',
        'price_numeric':     price,
        'old_price_numeric': old_price,
        'currency':          'TRY',
        'commission_rate':   commission if commission else 0.0,
        'discount_rate':     discount if discount else 0.0,
        'earning_potential': earning,
        'links':             urls,
        'media_urls':        media_urls or [],
        'source':            channel or 'unknown',
        'message_id':        message_id,
        'captured_at':       datetime.now().isoformat(),
        'raw_text':          text,
        'priority':          priority,
    }


def parse_batch(messages: List[Dict]) -> List[Dict]:
    """ГҮoklu mesaj parse et, Г¶nceliДҹe gГ¶re sДұrala."""
    ORDER = {'urgent': 0, 'high': 1, 'medium': 2, 'low': 3}
    results = [
        r for r in (
            parse_telegram_message(
                text=m.get('text', ''),
                channel=m.get('channel', ''),
                message_id=m.get('message_id', 0),
                media_urls=m.get('media_urls'),
            )
            for m in messages
        ) if r
    ]
    return sorted(results, key=lambda x: ORDER.get(x['priority'], 9))


# в”Җв”Җ CLI TEST в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
if __name__ == "__main__":
    tests = [
        ("рҹ”Ҙ Bluetooth KulaklДұk SГјper Bass\nFiyat: 299 TL (eski 599 TL)\n%50 Д°NDД°RД°M!\nKomisyon: %25\nhttps://www.trendyol.com/kulaklik-p-12345",
         "magazanolsunresmi", 101),

#!/usr/bin/env python3
# -*- coding: utf-8 -*-
"""
TRM Sistem Birim Testleri
KullanДұm: pytest test_trm.py -v
"""

import os
import sys
import json
import asyncio
import tempfile
import pytest

# ModГјlleri ekle
sys.path.insert(0, os.path.dirname(__file__))

# Config'i en baЕҹta yГјkle
import config


# ============================================
# Config Testleri
# ============================================

def test_config_loads_secrets():
    """secrets.env okunup os.environ'a aktarДұlДұyor mu?
    Not: secrets.env henГјz doldurulmamДұЕҹsa bu test atlanДұr (beklenen durum).
    """
    api_id = os.environ.get("TELEGRAM_API_ID", "")
    openai_key = os.environ.get("OPENAI_API_KEY", "")
    if not api_id and not openai_key:
        pytest.skip("secrets.env henГјz doldurulmamДұЕҹ вҖ” anahtarlarДұ girdikten sonra Г§alДұЕҹtДұrДұn")
    assert api_id, "TELEGRAM_API_ID os.environ'a yazДұlmamДұЕҹ"
    assert openai_key, "OPENAI_API_KEY os.environ'a yazДұlmamДұЕҹ"


def test_config_validation():
    """Validation Г§alДұЕҹДұyor mu?"""
    v = config.config.validate_critical_configs()
    assert isinstance(v, dict)
    assert 'telegram' in v
    assert 'openai' in v

# ============================================

def test_commission_extraction_legitimate():
    """Komisyon regex'i gerГ§ek komisyon deДҹerlerini yakalДұyor mu?"""
    from web_scraper import WebScraper
    s = WebScraper()
    assert s.extract_commission_from_text("Bu ГјrГјn %25 komisyon veriyor") == 25.0
    assert s.extract_commission_from_text("Д°ndirim %30") == 30.0
    assert s.extract_commission_from_text("yГјzde 15 fДұrsat") == 15.0


def test_commission_extraction_ignores_random_numbers():
    """Telefon/fiyat gibi rastgele sayДұlarДұ komisyon sanmДұyor"""
    from web_scraper import WebScraper
    s = WebScraper()
    # Sadece fiyat var, komisyon yok вҶ’ 0 dГ¶nmeli
    result = s.extract_commission_from_text("Fiyat 1299 TL, telefon 0212 555 1234")
    assert result == 0.0, f"Beklenen 0.0, gelen {result}"

# ============================================
# File-lock Kuyruk Testleri
# ============================================

def test_safe_queue_append_and_read():
    """File-lock kuyruk doДҹru Г§alДұЕҹДұyor mu?"""
    from trm_utils import safe_append_to_queue, safe_read_queue, safe_write_queue

    with tempfile.NamedTemporaryFile(mode='w', suffix='.json', delete=False) as f:
        tmp = f.name
        json.dump([], f)

    try:
        # Append
        safe_append_to_queue(tmp, {'id': 1, 'title': 'A'})
        safe_append_to_queue(tmp, {'id': 2, 'title': 'B'})

        data = safe_read_queue(tmp)
        assert len(data) == 2
        assert data[0]['title'] == 'A'
        assert data[1]['title'] == 'B'

        # Write (overwrite)
        safe_write_queue(tmp, [])
        data = safe_read_queue(tmp)
        assert data == []
    finally:
        os.unlink(tmp)
        lock_file = f"{tmp}.lock"
        if os.path.exists(lock_file):
            os.unlink(lock_file)

def test_telegram_parser_real_message():
    """GerГ§ek bir Telegram mesajДұ parse edilebiliyor mu?"""
    from telegram_parser import parse_telegram_message
    msg = """рҹ”Ҙ Bluetooth KulaklДұk
Fiyat: 299 TL
Komisyon: %25
https://www.trendyol.com/test"""
    result = parse_telegram_message(msg, channel="magazanolsunresmi", message_id=1)
    assert result is not None
    assert "Bluetooth" in result['title']
    assert result['commission_rate'] == 25.0
    assert result['price_numeric'] == 299.0
    assert 'trendyol.com' in result['links'][0]
    assert result['priority'] == 'high'


def test_telegram_parser_rejects_garbage():
    """ГңrГјn bilgisi olmayan mesajlarДұ reddediyor mu?"""
    from telegram_parser import parse_telegram_message
    result = parse_telegram_message("Merhaba arkadaЕҹlar, hava gГјzel", channel="test")
    assert result is None


def test_telegram_parser_handles_emoji_decorations():
    """Emoji ve dekorasyonlar baЕҹlДұktan temizleniyor mu?"""
    from telegram_parser import parse_telegram_message
    msg = """вҡЎ AkДұllДұ Saat - Smartwatch X100
рҹ’° Sadece 1.299вӮә
рҹ“Ҡ %30 komisyon"""
    result = parse_telegram_message(msg, channel="test", message_id=2)
    assert result is not None
    assert "вҡЎ" not in result['title']
    assert "рҹ’°" not in result['title']
    assert result['commission_rate'] == 30.0

# Tracking DB (Para kazanma zinciri)
# ============================================

def test_tracking_full_chain():
    """Tam para kazanma zinciri (ГјrГјn вҶ’ AI вҶ’ paylaЕҹДұm вҶ’ satДұЕҹ) Г§alДұЕҹДұyor mu?"""
    from trm_tracking import (
        record_product, record_ai_content, record_social_post,
        record_sale, get_full_chain, get_summary
    )
    product = {
        'title': 'Test ГңrГјn - Birim Test',
        'price': '500',
        'commission_rate': 30.0,
        'source': 'test_channel',
        'message_id': 99999,
        'captured_at': '2026-01-01T00:00:00',
        'links': ['https://example.com/test']
    }
    pid = record_product(product)
    assert pid is not None

    cid = record_ai_content(pid, {'content': 'Test', 'ai_confidence': 0.9}, model='mock')
    assert cid is not None

    spid = record_social_post(pid, cid, 'facebook',
                              {'success': True, 'post_id': 'fb_123', 'url': 'http://fb.com/p/123'})
    assert spid is not None

    sid = record_sale(pid, sale_amount=500.0, commission=150.0, post_id=spid)
    assert sid is not None

    chain = get_full_chain(pid)
    assert chain['product']['title'] == 'Test ГңrГјn - Birim Test'
    assert len(chain['ai_contents']) >= 1
    assert len(chain['social_posts']) >= 1
    assert len(chain['sales']) >= 1
    assert chain['total_revenue'] >= 150.0

# ============================================
# TД°KTOK OTOMASYON BOTU
# Claude API ile yapay zeka destekli iГ§erik
# Video paylaЕҹДұmДұ, otomatik metin Гјretimi
# ============================================

import os
import time
import random
import requests
from datetime import datetime
import anthropic  # Claude API iГ§in

class TikTokBot:
    def __init__(self):
        self.username = os.getenv('TIKTOK_USERNAME', '')
        self.password = os.getenv('TIKTOK_PASSWORD', '')
        self.claude_api_key = os.getenv('CLAUDE_API_KEY', '')
        self.session = requests.Session()
        
        # Claude istemcisini baЕҹlat
        if self.claude_api_key:
            self.claude = anthropic.Anthropic(api_key=self.claude_api_key)
        else:
            self.claude = None
            print("вҡ пёҸ Claude API anahtarДұ bulunamadДұ, temel modda Г§alДұЕҹДұlacak.")
        
        # Г–rnek video kaynaklarДұ (gerГ§ekte video dosyalarДұn olacak)
        self.video_kaynaklari = [
            'videos/urun1.mp4',
            'videos/urun2.mp4',
            'videos/urun3.mp4'
        ]
    
    def giris_yap(self):
        """TikTok'a giriЕҹ yapar (simГјlasyon)"""
        print(f"рҹҺө TikTok: @{self.username} giriЕҹ yapДұlДұyor...")
        time.sleep(2)
        print(f"вң… TikTok giriЕҹ baЕҹarДұlДұ")
        return True
    
    def claude_ile_metin_uret(self, urun_bilgisi, platform="tiktok"):
        """Claude API ile ГјrГјn aГ§ДұklamasДұ ve hashtag Гјretir"""
        if not self.claude:
            return self.temel_metin_uret(urun_bilgisi)
        
        prompt = f"""
        Bir ГјrГјn tanДұtДұmДұ iГ§in {platform} platformunda kullanДұlacak kДұsa ve etkili bir metin yaz.
        ГңrГјn adДұ: {urun_bilgisi['ad']}
        Fiyat: {urun_bilgisi['fiyat']} TL
        AГ§Дұklama: {urun_bilgisi.get('aciklama', '')}
        Kategori: {urun_bilgisi.get('kategori', 'genel')}
        
        Metin 150 karakteri geГ§mesin, dikkat Г§ekici olsun, emoji kullan ve 5-10 arasДұ hashtag ekle.
        Sadece metni yaz, baЕҹka aГ§Дұklama ekleme.
        """
        
        try:
            response = self.claude.messages.create(
                model="claude-3-sonnet-20241022",
                max_tokens=150,
                temperature=0.7,
                messages=[{"role": "user", "content": prompt}]
            )
            return response.content[0].text.strip()
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"вқҢ Claude API hatasДұ: {e}")
            return self.temel_metin_uret(urun_bilgisi)
    
    def temel_metin_uret(self, urun_bilgisi):
        """API yoksa kullanДұlacak temel metin"""
        return f"""
{urun_bilgisi['ad']} - {urun_bilgisi['fiyat']} TL рҹ”Ҙ

{urun_bilgisi.get('aciklama', 'KaГ§Дұrma fДұrsatДұ!')}

#keЕҹfet #fyp #{urun_bilgisi.get('kategori', 'ГјrГјn')} #indirim #fДұrsat
        """.strip()
    
    def video_hazirla(self, urun_adi):
        """ГңrГјn iГ§in video hazДұrlar (simГјlasyon)"""
        print(f"рҹҺ¬ {urun_adi} iГ§in video hazДұrlanДұyor...")
        time.sleep(3)
        # GerГ§ek uygulamada video dГјzenleme veya seГ§me yapДұlДұr
        return random.choice(self.video_kaynaklari) if self.video_kaynaklari else "videos/default.mp4"
    
    def video_paylas(self, video_yolu, metin):
        """TikTok'a video yГјkler (simГјlasyon)"""
        print(f"рҹ“Ө TikTok: Video yГјkleniyor...")
        print(f"рҹ“қ Metin: {metin}")
        time.sleep(4)
        print(f"вң… TikTok video paylaЕҹДұldДұ!")
        return True
    
    def paylasim_hazirla(self, urun):
        """ГңrГјn bilgisiyle TikTok paylaЕҹДұmДұ hazДұrlar"""
        # Claude ile metin Гјret
        metin = self.claude_ile_metin_uret(urun)
        
        # Video hazДұrla (gerГ§ekte video dosyasДұ seГ§)
        video = self.video_hazirla(urun['ad'])
        
        # PaylaЕҹ
        return self.video_paylas(video, metin)


if __name__ == "__main__":
    # Test iГ§in
    bot = TikTokBot()
    bot.giris_yap()
    
    test_urun = {
        'ad': 'Xiaomi AkДұllДұ Bileklik',
        'fiyat': 449,
        'aciklama': 'Kalp atДұЕҹДұ takibi, adДұm sayar, 14 gГјn pil Г¶mrГј',
        'kategori': 'elektronik'
    }
    
    bot.paylasim_hazirla(test_urun)

# TREASURY_KEEPER_AGENT.py
class TreasuryKeeperAgent:
    def __init__(self):
        # Hesap bakiyeleri (Sistemsel simГјlasyon)
        self.balances = {"TL": 50000, "EURO": 2000, "USD": 2500}

    def request_approval_hybrid(self, expense_type, amount, currency):
        """Hibrit onay mekanizmasДұ: Buton veya Sesli komut iГ§in hazДұr."""
        print(f"[BД°LDД°RД°M] {expense_type} iГ§in {amount} {currency} Г¶deme onayДұ bekleniyor.")
        print("-> [BUTON] Panel Гјzerinden 'ONAYLA' tuЕҹuna basabilirsiniz.")
        print("-> [SESLД°] LГјtfen sesli olarak 'OnaylДұyorum' komutunu iletin.")
        return "WAITING_FOR_INPUT"

    def execute_payment(self, expense_type, amount, currency, confirmation):
        """Onay alДұndДұktan sonra Г¶demeyi gerГ§ekleЕҹtiren gГјvenli modГјl."""
        if confirmation.lower() in ["onaylДұyorum", "onayla", "evet"]:
            if self.balances.get(currency, 0) >= amount:
                self.balances[currency] -= amount
                print(f"[BAЕһARILI] {expense_type} Г¶demesi {currency} hesabДұndan yapДұldДұ. Kalan: {self.balances[currency]}")
                return True
            else:
                print(f"[HATA] {currency} hesabДұnda bakiye yetersiz.")
        else:
            print(f"[Д°PTAL] {expense_type} Г¶demesi onaylanmadДұ.")
        return False

if __name__ == "__main__":
    # Test Modu: Ajan hazДұr
    keeper = TreasuryKeeperAgent()
    status = keeper.request_approval_hybrid("Sunucu_Kirasi", 1200, "TL")
    if status == "WAITING_FOR_INPUT":
        # SimГјlasyon: Sesli veya butonlu komut geldiДҹini varsayalДұm
        keeper.execute_payment("Sunucu_Kirasi", 1200, "TL", "onaylДұyorum")

#!/usr/bin/env python3
# -*- coding: utf-8 -*-
"""
ULUSLARARASI TRM FULL OTOMASYON SД°STEMД° v3.0
Trend ГңrГјnler Market - Tam Otomasyon Motoru
24/7 Kesintisiz ГҮalДұЕҹma Sistemi
"""

import json
import time
import random
import threading
from datetime import datetime, timedelta
from http.server import HTTPServer, SimpleHTTPRequestHandler
import urllib.parse
import os

class TRMAutomationEngine:
    def __init__(self):
        self.running = True
        self.data = {
            "system_status": "AKTД°F",
            "uptime_start": datetime.now(),
            "daily_revenue": 12450,
            "target_revenue": 18000,
            "commission_rate": 25.8,
            "active_products": 247,
            "ai_status": "AKTД°F",
            "social_media_status": "AKTД°F",
            "bank_status": "AKTД°F",
            "notifications": [],
            "sales_data": [],
            "performance_metrics": {
                "cpu_usage": 45,
                "memory_usage": 2.3,
                "network_speed": 125,
                "requests_per_second": 1247,
                "response_time": 45,
                "uptime": 99.9
            },
            "ai_modules": {
                "deepseek": "AKTД°F",
                "claude": "AKTД°F",
                "analysis_engine": "AKTД°F",
                "decision_engine": "AKTД°F"
            },
            "social_platforms": {
                "facebook": "AKTД°F",
                "instagram": "AKTД°F", 
                "twitter": "AKTД°F",
                "linkedin": "AKTД°F",
                "tiktok": "AKTД°F",
                "youtube": "AKTД°F"
            },
            "notification_systems": {
                "messaging": "AKTД°F",
                "telegram": "AKTД°F",
                "email": "AKTД°F",
                "sms": "AKTД°F",
                "push": "AKTД°F"
            },
            "automation_rules": [
                "Komisyon %20+ olan ГјrГјnler otomatik seГ§ilir",
                "Stok durumu kontrol edilir",
                "Fiyat analizi yapДұlДұr",
                "Trend analizi uygulanДұr",
                "Sosyal medya paylaЕҹДұmДұ planlanДұr",
                "MГјЕҹteri bildirimleri gГ¶nderilir"
            ]
        }
        self.start_automation()

    def generate_notification(self):
        """Otomatik bildirim oluЕҹtur"""
        messages = [
            "рҹҡЁ YГјksek komisyonlu ГјrГјn tespit edildi!",
            "рҹ’° Yeni satДұЕҹ gerГ§ekleЕҹti - вӮә{} kazanДұldДұ".format(random.randint(500, 5000)),
            "рҹ“Ҳ SatДұЕҹ hedefine %{} ulaЕҹДұldДұ".format(random.randint(60, 95)),
            "рҹҺҜ Trend ГјrГјn tespiti tamamlandДұ",
            "рҹӨ– AI analizi gГјncellendi",
            "рҹ“ұ Sosyal medya paylaЕҹДұmДұ planlandДұ",
            "рҹҸҰ Banka iЕҹlemi baЕҹarДұyla tamamlandДұ",
            "вң… Otomasyon kuralДұ uygulandДұ"
        ]
        notification = {
            "id": len(self.data["notifications"]) + 1,
            "message": random.choice(messages),
            "timestamp": datetime.now().strftime("%H:%M:%S"),
            "type": random.choice(["info", "success", "warning", "alert"])
        }
        self.data["notifications"].append(notification)
        if len(self.data["notifications"]) > 10:
            self.data["notifications"] = self.data["notifications"][-10:]

    def update_revenue(self):
        """Gelir verilerini gГјncelle"""
        increase = random.randint(100, 800)
        self.data["daily_revenue"] += increase
        
        # SatДұЕҹ verisi ekle
        sale = {
            "amount": increase,
            "commission": round(increase * self.data["commission_rate"] / 100, 2),
            "time": datetime.now().strftime("%H:%M"),
            "product_category": random.choice(["Elektronik", "Giyim", "Ev", "Spor", "Teknoloji"])
        }
        self.data["sales_data"].append(sale)
        if len(self.data["sales_data"]) > 20:
            self.data["sales_data"] = self.data["sales_data"][-20:]

    def update_metrics(self):
        """Performans metriklerini gГјncelle"""
        self.data["performance_metrics"]["cpu_usage"] = max(20, min(80, 
            self.data["performance_metrics"]["cpu_usage"] + random.randint(-5, 5)))
        self.data["performance_metrics"]["memory_usage"] = max(1.5, min(4.0,
            self.data["performance_metrics"]["memory_usage"] + random.uniform(-0.2, 0.2)))
        self.data["performance_metrics"]["network_speed"] = max(80, min(150,
            self.data["performance_metrics"]["network_speed"] + random.randint(-10, 10)))
        self.data["performance_metrics"]["requests_per_second"] = max(800, min(2000,
            self.data["performance_metrics"]["requests_per_second"] + random.randint(-100, 100)))
        self.data["performance_metrics"]["response_time"] = max(20, min(80,
            self.data["performance_metrics"]["response_time"] + random.randint(-5, 5)))

    def automation_loop(self):
        """Ana otomasyon dГ¶ngГјsГј"""
        while self.running:
            try:
                # Her 5 saniyede bir bildirim oluЕҹtur
                self.generate_notification()
                
                # Her 10 saniyede bir gelir gГјncelle
                if int(time.time()) % 10 == 0:
                    self.update_revenue()
                
                # Her 15 saniyede bir metrikleri gГјncelle
                if int(time.time()) % 15 == 0:
                    self.update_metrics()
                
                # ГңrГјn sayДұsДұnДұ gГјncelle
                self.data["active_products"] = max(200, min(300, 
                    self.data["active_products"] + random.randint(-2, 2)))
                
                # Komisyon oranДұnДұ gГјncelle
                self.data["commission_rate"] = max(20, min(35, 
                    self.data["commission_rate"] + random.uniform(-0.5, 0.5)))
                
                time.sleep(5)
                
            except Exception as e:
                print(f"Otomasyon hatasДұ: {e}")
                time.sleep(5)

    def start_automation(self):
        """Otomasyonu baЕҹlat"""
        automation_thread = threading.Thread(target=self.automation_loop, daemon=True)
        automation_thread.start()

    def get_uptime(self):
        """ГҮalДұЕҹma sГјresini hesapla"""
        uptime = datetime.now() - self.data["uptime_start"]
        days = uptime.days
        hours, remainder = divmod(uptime.seconds, 3600)
        minutes, seconds = divmod(remainder, 60)
        return f"{days}g {hours}sa {minutes}dk {seconds}sn"

    def get_status_json(self):
        """JSON durum bilgisi dГ¶ndГјr"""
        return json.dumps({
            "system_status": self.data["system_status"],
            "uptime": self.get_uptime(),
            "daily_revenue": self.data["daily_revenue"],
            "target_revenue": self.data["target_revenue"],
            "commission_rate": self.data["commission_rate"],
            "active_products": self.data["active_products"],
            "ai_status": self.data["ai_status"],
            "social_media_status": self.data["social_media_status"],
            "bank_status": self.data["bank_status"],
            "notifications": self.data["notifications"][-5:],
            "performance_metrics": self.data["performance_metrics"],
            "ai_modules": self.data["ai_modules"],
            "social_platforms": self.data["social_platforms"],
            "notification_systems": self.data["notification_systems"],
            "automation_rules": self.data["automation_rules"],
            "sales_data": self.data["sales_data"][-10:]
        }, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2)

class TRMAPIHandler(SimpleHTTPRequestHandler):
    def __init__(self, *args, automation_engine=None, **kwargs):
        self.automation_engine = automation_engine
        super().__init__(*args, **kwargs)

    def do_GET(self):
        if self.path == '/':
            self.serve_html('ANA_PANEL.html')
        elif self.path == '/status':
            self.serve_json()
        elif self.path == '/sales':
            self.serve_html('SATIS_PANEL.html')
        elif self.path == '/advanced':
            self.serve_html('GELISMIS_PANEL.html')
        elif self.path.startswith('/api/'):
            self.handle_api()
        else:
            super().do_GET()

    def serve_html(self, filename):
        """HTML dosyasДұ sun"""
        try:
            with open(filename, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                content = f.read()
            
            # Dinamik iГ§erik gГјncelle
            content = self.update_dynamic_content(content)
            
            self.send_response(200)
            self.send_header('Content-type', 'text/html; charset=utf-8')
            self.end_headers()
            self.wfile.write(content.encode('utf-8'))
        except FileNotFoundError:
            self.send_error(404, "File not found")

    def serve_json(self):
        """JSON veri sun"""
        self.send_response(200)
        self.send_header('Content-type', 'application/json; charset=utf-8')
        self.send_header('Access-Control-Allow-Origin', '*')
        self.end_headers()
        self.wfile.write(self.automation_engine.get_status_json().encode('utf-8'))

    def handle_api(self):
        """API isteklerini yГ¶net"""
        path_parts = self.path.split('/')
        
        if len(path_parts) >= 3:
            action = path_parts[2]
            
            if action == 'start':
                self.automation_engine.running = True
                self.send_json_response({"status": "started", "message": "Sistem baЕҹlatДұldДұ"})
            elif action == 'stop':
                self.automation_engine.running = False
                self.send_json_response({"status": "stopped", "message": "Sistem durduruldu"})
            elif action == 'restart':
                self.automation_engine.running = True
                self.send_json_response({"status": "restarted", "message": "Sistem yeniden baЕҹlatДұldДұ"})
            elif action == 'notifications':
                self.send_json_response({"notifications": self.automation_engine.data["notifications"]})
            elif action == 'metrics':
                self.send_json_response({"metrics": self.automation_engine.data["performance_metrics"]})
            elif action == 'revenue':
                self.send_json_response({
                    "daily_revenue": self.automation_engine.data["daily_revenue"],
                    "target_revenue": self.automation_engine.data["target_revenue"],
                    "commission_rate": self.automation_engine.data["commission_rate"]
                })
            else:
                self.send_error(404, "API endpoint not found")

    def send_json_response(self, data):
        """JSON yanДұt gГ¶nder"""
        self.send_response(200)
        self.send_header('Content-type', 'application/json; charset=utf-8')
        self.send_header('Access-Control-Allow-Origin', '*')
        self.end_headers()
        self.wfile.write(json.dumps(data, ensure_ascii=False).encode('utf-8'))

    def update_dynamic_content(self, content):
        """HTML iГ§eriДҹini dinamik olarak gГјncelle"""
        data = self.automation_engine.data
        
        # ZamanДұ gГјncelle
        current_time = datetime.now().strftime("%d.%m.%Y %H:%M:%S")
        content = content.replace('<span id="time"></span>', current_time)
        
        # Gelir verilerini gГјncelle
        content = content.replace('вӮә12,450', f'вӮә{data["daily_revenue"]:,}')
        content = content.replace('%25.8', f'%{data["commission_rate"]:.1f}')
        content = content.replace('247', str(data["active_products"]))
        
        return content

    def do_POST(self):
        if self.path.startswith('/api/'):
            self.handle_api()
        else:
            self.send_error(404, "Endpoint not found")

def start_server(port, automation_engine):
    """Sunucu baЕҹlat"""
    handler = lambda *args, **kwargs: TRMAPIHandler(*args, automation_engine=automation_engine, **kwargs)
    server = HTTPServer(('localhost', port), handler)
    print(f"вң… Sunucu {port} portunda baЕҹlatДұldДұ")
    server.serve_forever()

def main():
    print("рҹҡҖ ULUSLARARASI TRM FULL OTOMASYON SД°STEMД° v3.0")
    print("рҹҢҗ Trend ГңrГјnler Market - Tam Otomasyon BaЕҹlatДұlДұyor")
    print("=" * 60)
    
    # Otomasyon motorunu baЕҹlat
    automation_engine = TRMAutomationEngine()
    
    # SunucularДұ farklДұ portlarda baЕҹlat
    ports = [9000, 9001, 9002, 9003]
    server_threads = []
    
    for port in ports:
        thread = threading.Thread(target=start_server, args=(port, automation_engine), daemon=True)
        thread.start()
        server_threads.append(thread)
        time.sleep(0.5)
    
    print("\nвң… TГјm Sunucular BaЕҹlatДұldДұ!")
    print("рҹҢҗ Paneller:")
    print("   вҖў Ana Panel: http://localhost:9000")
    print("   вҖў Status API: http://localhost:9001/status")
    print("   вҖў SatДұЕҹ Paneli: http://localhost:9002")
    print("   вҖў GeliЕҹmiЕҹ Panel: http://localhost:9003")
    print("\nрҹӨ– Tam Otomasyon Aktif - 24/7 ГҮalДұЕҹДұyor")
    print("рҹ’° Para Kazanma Modu: AKTД°F")
    print("рҹ“ұ Bildirimler: AKTД°F")
    print("рҹ”„ Otomatik GГјncellemeler: AKTД°F")
    print("\nрҹ‘Ӣ Durdurmak iГ§in Ctrl+C")
    
    try:
        while True:
            time.sleep(1)
    except KeyboardInterrupt:
        print("\nрҹ‘Ӣ Sistem durduruluyor...")
        automation_engine.running = False
        print("вң… Otomasyon durduruldu")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

# -*- coding: utf-8 -*-
"""
Merkezi yol Г§Г¶zГјmlemesi вҖ” pathlib tabanlДұ, sabit kullanДұcДұ yolu iГ§ermez.

Д°steДҹe baДҹlДұ ortam deДҹiЕҹkenleri (boЕҹ bДұrakДұlДұrsa proje kГ¶kГј kullanДұlДұr):
  TRM_PROJECT_ROOT вҖ” proje kГ¶k dizini
  TRM_HTML_DIR     вҖ” HTML panellerinin bulunduДҹu dizin (varsayДұlan: proje kГ¶kГј)
  TRM_LOGS_DIR     вҖ” gГјnlГјk dizini (varsayДұlan: <proje kГ¶kГј>/logs)
  TRM_DATA_DIR     вҖ” veri dizini (varsayДұlan: <proje kГ¶kГј>/data)
  TRM_FLASH_ROOT   вҖ” flash / harici ayna senkron kГ¶kГј (yok veya geГ§ersizse geriye dГ¶nГјk G: yolu)

flash_sync_root():
  TRM_FLASH_ROOT geГ§erliyse onu dГ¶ndГјrГјr; aksi halde Г¶nceki DRIVE_FLASH_SYNC varsayДұlanДұ (G:/...) kullanДұlДұr.
  Д°lk kullanДұmda INFO veya WARNING ile aГ§Дұk log Гјretir (sessiz dГјЕҹГјЕҹ yok).
"""

from __future__ import annotations

import logging
import os
from pathlib import Path

_log = logging.getLogger(__name__)

# DRIVE_FLASH_SYNC Г¶ncesi sabit varsayДұlan (davranДұЕҹ korunur).
_LEGACY_FLASH_SYNC_ROOT = Path("G:/Uluslararasi-TRM-Full-Otomasyon-Sistemi")
_LEGACY_PAZARLAMA_ROOT = Path("G:/PAZARLAMA")

_warned_invalid_trm_flash_root = False
_warned_invalid_trm_pazarlama_root = False
_logged_missing_trm_flash_root = False
_logged_pazarlama_discovery = False


def project_root() -> Path:
    """Proje kГ¶kГј: TRM_PROJECT_ROOT geГ§erliyse onu, deДҹilse bu dosyanДұn bulunduДҹu dizini dГ¶ndГјrГјr."""
    override = os.environ.get("TRM_PROJECT_ROOT", "").strip()
    if override:
        candidate = Path(override).expanduser().resolve()
        if candidate.is_dir():
            return candidate
    return Path(__file__).resolve().parent


PROJECT_ROOT: Path = project_root()


def html_dir() -> Path:
    """HTML panelleri dizini; TRM_HTML_DIR geГ§erliyse onu, deДҹilse proje kГ¶kГјnГј dГ¶ndГјrГјr."""
    override = os.environ.get("TRM_HTML_DIR", "").strip()
    if override:
        candidate = Path(override).expanduser().resolve()
        if candidate.is_dir():
            return candidate
    return project_root()


def logs_dir() -> Path:
    """GГјnlГјk dizini; TRM_LOGS_DIR tanДұmlДұysa onu, deДҹilse <proje kГ¶kГј>/logs dГ¶ndГјrГјr."""
    override = os.environ.get("TRM_LOGS_DIR", "").strip()
    if override:
        return Path(override).expanduser().resolve()
    return project_root() / "logs"


def data_dir() -> Path:
    """Veri dizini; TRM_DATA_DIR tanДұmlДұysa onu, deДҹilse <proje kГ¶kГј>/data dГ¶ndГјrГјr."""
    override = os.environ.get("TRM_DATA_DIR", "").strip()
    if override:
        return Path(override).expanduser().resolve()
    return project_root() / "data"


def flash_sync_root() -> Path:
    """
    Flash / harici ayna senkron kГ¶k dizini.

    Г–ncelik: TRM_FLASH_ROOT mevcut bir dizin ise.
    TanДұmlДұ ama geГ§ersiz: bir kez WARNING, ardДұndan geriye dГ¶nГјk varsayДұlan.
    TanДұmsДұz: bir kez INFO, ardДұndan geriye dГ¶nГјk varsayДұlan (Г¶nceki G: yolu).
    """
    global _warned_invalid_trm_flash_root, _logged_missing_trm_flash_root

    override = os.environ.get("TRM_FLASH_ROOT", "").strip()
    if override:
        candidate = Path(override).expanduser().resolve()
        if candidate.is_dir():
            return candidate
        if not _warned_invalid_trm_flash_root:
            _log.warning(
                "TRM_FLASH_ROOT geГ§ersiz veya dizin yok (%r). "
                "Flash senkron kГ¶kГј geriye dГ¶nГјk varsayДұlan olarak kullanДұlДұyor: %s",
                override,
                _LEGACY_FLASH_SYNC_ROOT,
            )
            _warned_invalid_trm_flash_root = True
        return _LEGACY_FLASH_SYNC_ROOT

    if not _logged_missing_trm_flash_root:
        _log.info(
            "TRM_FLASH_ROOT tanДұmlДұ deДҹil; flash senkron kГ¶kГј geriye dГ¶nГјk varsayДұlan: %s. "
            "KalДұcДұ yol iГ§in TRM_FLASH_ROOT ortam deДҹiЕҹkenini ayarlayДұn.",
            _LEGACY_FLASH_SYNC_ROOT,
        )
        _logged_missing_trm_flash_root = True
    return _LEGACY_FLASH_SYNC_ROOT


def pazarlama_root() -> Path:
    """
    PAZARLAMA sistemi kГ¶k dizini.

    Г–ncelik:
    1. TRM_PAZARLAMA_ROOT ortam deДҹiЕҹkeni (geГ§erli bir dizin ise).
    2. Otomatik KeЕҹif: Proje klasГ¶rГјnГјn kardeЕҹi (sibling) olan 'PAZARLAMA' klasГ¶rГј.
    3. Geriye DГ¶nГјk VarsayДұlan: G:/PAZARLAMA (legacy fallback).
    """
    global _warned_invalid_trm_pazarlama_root, _logged_pazarlama_discovery

    # 1. Ortam DeДҹiЕҹkeni
    override = os.environ.get("TRM_PAZARLAMA_ROOT", "").strip()
    if override:
        candidate = Path(override).expanduser().resolve()
        if candidate.is_dir():
            return candidate
        if not _warned_invalid_trm_pazarlama_root:
            _log.warning(
                "TRM_PAZARLAMA_ROOT geГ§ersiz veya dizin yok (%r). "
                "DiДҹer yГ¶ntemler deneniyor.",
                override,
            )
            _warned_invalid_trm_pazarlama_root = True

    # 2. Otomatik KeЕҹif (Sibling Folder)
    sibling = PROJECT_ROOT.parent / "PAZARLAMA"
    if sibling.is_dir():
        if not _logged_pazarlama_discovery:
            _log.info("PAZARLAMA sistemi otomatik keЕҹfedildi: %s", sibling)
            _logged_pazarlama_discovery = True
        return sibling

    # 3. Legacy Fallback
    if not _logged_pazarlama_discovery:
        _log.info(
            "PAZARLAMA sistemi iГ§in geriye dГ¶nГјk varsayДұlan yol kullanДұlДұyor: %s",
            _LEGACY_PAZARLAMA_ROOT,
        )
        _logged_pazarlama_discovery = True
    return _LEGACY_PAZARLAMA_ROOT

#!/usr/bin/env python3
# -*- coding: utf-8 -*-
"""
TRM Tracking Database - Para kazanma kanДұt zinciri iГ§in SQLite tabanlДұ takip

AkДұЕҹ: Telegram ГјrГјn вҶ’ AI iГ§erik вҶ’ Sosyal paylaЕҹДұm вҶ’ SatДұЕҹ linki вҶ’ Komisyon takibi
TГјm aЕҹamalarДұ kayДұt altДұna alДұr, raporlanabilir hale getirir.
"""

import sqlite3
import logging
import json
from contextlib import contextmanager
from datetime import datetime
from pathlib import Path
from typing import Dict, List, Optional

logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)

DB_PATH = Path(__file__).parent / "data" / "trm_tracking.db"


def init_db():
    """VeritabanДұnДұ ve tablolarДұ oluЕҹtur"""
    DB_PATH.parent.mkdir(exist_ok=True)
    with get_conn() as conn:
        c = conn.cursor()
        c.executescript("""
        CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS products (
            id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
            source TEXT NOT NULL,                -- telegram kanal adДұ / web url
            source_message_id TEXT,              -- Telegram message_id
            title TEXT NOT NULL,
            description TEXT,
            price REAL,
            currency TEXT DEFAULT 'TRY',
            commission_rate REAL,                -- yГјzde olarak (Г¶rn 25.0)
            product_url TEXT,                    -- satДұЕҹ/affiliate linki
            image_urls TEXT,                     -- JSON liste
            raw_message TEXT,                    -- orijinal Telegram mesajДұ
            captured_at TEXT NOT NULL,
            status TEXT DEFAULT 'captured',      -- captured/processed/published/sold
            UNIQUE(source, source_message_id, title)
        );

        CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS ai_content (
            id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
            product_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
            content_text TEXT NOT NULL,
            hashtags TEXT,
            ai_model TEXT,                       -- deepseek/claude/mock
            ai_confidence REAL,
            created_at TEXT NOT NULL,
            FOREIGN KEY(product_id) REFERENCES products(id)
        );

        CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS social_posts (
            id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
            product_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
            content_id INTEGER,
            platform TEXT NOT NULL,              -- facebook/instagram/twitter/youtube/tiktok/blog
            post_id TEXT,                        -- platform tarafДұndaki post id
            post_url TEXT,
            success INTEGER NOT NULL,            -- 0/1
            error_message TEXT,
            published_at TEXT NOT NULL,
            FOREIGN KEY(product_id) REFERENCES products(id),
            FOREIGN KEY(content_id) REFERENCES ai_content(id)
        );

        CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS sales_events (
            id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
            product_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
            post_id INTEGER,                     -- referrer social post
            sale_amount REAL NOT NULL,
            commission_earned REAL NOT NULL,
            currency TEXT DEFAULT 'TRY',
            buyer_info TEXT,                     -- isteДҹe baДҹlДұ (anonim)
            sold_at TEXT NOT NULL,
            FOREIGN KEY(product_id) REFERENCES products(id),
            FOREIGN KEY(post_id) REFERENCES social_posts(id)
        );

        CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_products_status ON products(status);
        CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_products_captured ON products(captured_at);
        CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_sales_sold_at ON sales_events(sold_at);
        """)
        conn.commit()
    logger.info(f"рҹ“Ҡ Tracking DB hazДұr: {DB_PATH}")


@contextmanager
def get_conn():
    """BaДҹlantДұ context manager (otomatik commit/close)"""
    conn = sqlite3.connect(str(DB_PATH))
    conn.row_factory = sqlite3.Row
    try:
        yield conn
        conn.commit()
    finally:
        conn.close()


# ============================================
# ГңrГјn KaydДұ
# ============================================

def record_product(product_data: Dict) -> Optional[int]:
    """Yeni ГјrГјn kaydet, ID dГ¶ndГјr. AynДұ ГјrГјn varsa mevcut ID'yi dГ¶ndГјr."""
    try:
        with get_conn() as conn:
            c = conn.cursor()
            # Г–nce var mДұ kontrol et
            c.execute("""
                SELECT id FROM products
                WHERE source=? AND source_message_id=? AND title=?
            """, (
                product_data.get('source', ''),
                str(product_data.get('message_id', '')),
                product_data.get('title', '')
            ))
            row = c.fetchone()
            if row:
                return row['id']

            # FiyatДұ numeric'e Г§evir
            price = product_data.get('price', '')
            try:
                price_num = float(''.join(ch for ch in str(price) if ch.isdigit() or ch == '.'))
            except (ValueError, TypeError):
                price_num = 0.0

            c.execute("""
                INSERT INTO products (source, source_message_id, title, description, price,
                                      commission_rate, product_url, image_urls, raw_message,
                                      captured_at, status)
                VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, 'captured')
            """, (
                product_data.get('source', ''),
                str(product_data.get('message_id', '')),
                product_data.get('title', '')[:500],
                product_data.get('description', ''),
                price_num,
                float(product_data.get('commission_rate', 0)),
                (product_data.get('links') or [None])[0] if isinstance(product_data.get('links'), list) else product_data.get('url', ''),
                json.dumps(product_data.get('media_urls', []), ensure_ascii=False),
                product_data.get('raw_text', ''),
                product_data.get('captured_at', datetime.now().isoformat())
            ))
            return c.lastrowid
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"ГңrГјn kayДұt hatasДұ: {e}")
        return None


def record_ai_content(product_id: int, content: Dict, model: str = "mock") -> Optional[int]:
    """AI tarafДұndan Гјretilen iГ§eriДҹi kaydet"""
    try:
        with get_conn() as conn:
            c = conn.cursor()
            c.execute("""
                INSERT INTO ai_content (product_id, content_text, hashtags, ai_model,
                                        ai_confidence, created_at)
                VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?)
            """, (
                product_id,
                content.get('content', ''),
                json.dumps(content.get('hashtags', []), ensure_ascii=False),
                model,
                float(content.get('ai_confidence', 0)),
                datetime.now().isoformat()
            ))
            # ГңrГјn durumunu gГјncelle
            c.execute("UPDATE products SET status='processed' WHERE id=?", (product_id,))
            return c.lastrowid
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"AI iГ§erik kayДұt hatasДұ: {e}")
        return None


def record_social_post(product_id: int, content_id: Optional[int], platform: str, result: Dict) -> Optional[int]:
    """Sosyal medya paylaЕҹДұmДұnДұ kaydet"""
    try:
        with get_conn() as conn:
            c = conn.cursor()
            c.execute("""
                INSERT INTO social_posts (product_id, content_id, platform, post_id, post_url,
                                          success, error_message, published_at)
                VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?)
            """, (
                product_id,
                content_id,
                platform,
                result.get('post_id', ''),
                result.get('url', ''),
                1 if result.get('success') else 0,
                result.get('error', '') or result.get('message', '') if not result.get('success') else None,
                datetime.now().isoformat()
            ))
            if result.get('success'):
                c.execute("UPDATE products SET status='published' WHERE id=?", (product_id,))
            return c.lastrowid
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"Sosyal medya kayДұt hatasДұ: {e}")
        return None


def record_sale(product_id: int, sale_amount: float, commission: float,
                post_id: Optional[int] = None, buyer_info: str = "") -> Optional[int]:
    """SatДұЕҹ olayДұnДұ kaydet"""
    try:
        with get_conn() as conn:
            c = conn.cursor()
            c.execute("""
                INSERT INTO sales_events (product_id, post_id, sale_amount, commission_earned,
                                          buyer_info, sold_at)
                VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?)
            """, (product_id, post_id, sale_amount, commission, buyer_info,
                  datetime.now().isoformat()))
            c.execute("UPDATE products SET status='sold' WHERE id=?", (product_id,))
            return c.lastrowid
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"SatДұЕҹ kayДұt hatasДұ: {e}")
        return None


# ============================================
# Raporlama
# ============================================

def get_full_chain(product_id: int) -> Dict:
    """Bir ГјrГјnГјn tam zinciri: ГјrГјn вҶ’ AI iГ§erik вҶ’ paylaЕҹДұmlar вҶ’ satДұЕҹlar"""
    with get_conn() as conn:
        c = conn.cursor()
        product = c.execute("SELECT * FROM products WHERE id=?", (product_id,)).fetchone()
        if not product:
            return {}
        contents = c.execute("SELECT * FROM ai_content WHERE product_id=?", (product_id,)).fetchall()
        posts = c.execute("SELECT * FROM social_posts WHERE product_id=?", (product_id,)).fetchall()
        sales = c.execute("SELECT * FROM sales_events WHERE product_id=?", (product_id,)).fetchall()

        return {
            'product': dict(product),
            'ai_contents': [dict(r) for r in contents],
            'social_posts': [dict(r) for r in posts],
            'sales': [dict(r) for r in sales],
            'total_revenue': sum(s['commission_earned'] for s in sales)
        }


def get_summary(days: int = 7) -> Dict:
    """Son N gГјn iГ§in Г¶zet"""
    with get_conn() as conn:
        c = conn.cursor()
        cutoff = datetime.now().isoformat()[:10]

        total_products = c.execute("SELECT COUNT(*) c FROM products").fetchone()['c']
        published = c.execute("SELECT COUNT(*) c FROM products WHERE status IN ('published','sold')").fetchone()['c']
        sold = c.execute("SELECT COUNT(*) c FROM products WHERE status='sold'").fetchone()['c']
        total_revenue = c.execute("SELECT COALESCE(SUM(commission_earned),0) r FROM sales_events").fetchone()['r']

        # Platform bazДұnda baЕҹarДұ
        platform_stats = c.execute("""
            SELECT platform,
                   SUM(CASE WHEN success=1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) ok,
                   COUNT(*) total
            FROM social_posts GROUP BY platform
        """).fetchall()

        # En Г§ok kazandДұran ГјrГјnler
        top_products = c.execute("""
            SELECT p.id, p.title, p.commission_rate,
                   COALESCE(SUM(s.commission_earned),0) revenue,
                   COUNT(s.id) sales_count
            FROM products p
            LEFT JOIN sales_events s ON s.product_id = p.id
            GROUP BY p.id
            ORDER BY revenue DESC
            LIMIT 5
        """).fetchall()

        return {
            'as_of': cutoff,
            'total_products_captured': total_products,
            'total_published': published,
            'total_sold': sold,
            'conversion_rate_pct': round((sold / total_products * 100) if total_products else 0, 2),
            'total_revenue_try': round(total_revenue, 2),
            'platform_stats': [dict(r) for r in platform_stats],
            'top_products': [dict(r) for r in top_products],
        }


def list_recent_products(limit: int = 20) -> List[Dict]:
    """Son ГјrГјnleri listele"""
    with get_conn() as conn:
        c = conn.cursor()
        rows = c.execute(
            "SELECT * FROM products ORDER BY captured_at DESC LIMIT ?", (limit,)
        ).fetchall()
        return [dict(r) for r in rows]


# Д°lk import'ta DB'yi hazДұrla
init_db()


if __name__ == "__main__":
    # CLI: Г¶zet raporu yazdДұr
    summary = get_summary()
    print("\n" + "=" * 60)
    print("рҹ“Ҡ TRM PARA KAZANMA RAPORU")
    print("=" * 60)
    print(f"Toplam Yakalanan ГңrГјn: {summary['total_products_captured']}")
    print(f"YayДұnlanan:            {summary['total_published']}")
    print(f"SatДұlan:               {summary['total_sold']}")
    print(f"DГ¶nГјЕҹГјm OranДұ:         %{summary['conversion_rate_pct']}")
    print(f"Toplam Komisyon:       {summary['total_revenue_try']} TL")
    print("\nPlatform PerformansДұ:")
    for p in summary['platform_stats']:
        print(f"  {p['platform']:12s} вҶ’ {p['ok']}/{p['total']}")
    print("\nEn ГҮok KazandДұran ГңrГјnler:")
    for p in summary['top_products']:
        print(f"  [{p['id']}] {p['title'][:40]:40s} вҶ’ {p['revenue']:.2f} TL ({p['sales_count']} satДұЕҹ)")
    print("=" * 60)

#!/usr/bin/env python3
# -*- coding: utf-8 -*-
"""
TRM Ortak YardДұmcДұ ModГјlГј
- Log rotasyonu
- File-lock korumalДұ JSON kuyruk iЕҹlemleri
- Retry decorator
"""

import json
import logging
import os
from logging.handlers import RotatingFileHandler
from typing import List, Dict, Any

try:
    from filelock import FileLock
    FILELOCK_AVAILABLE = True
except ImportError:
    FILELOCK_AVAILABLE = False

try:
    from tenacity import retry, stop_after_attempt, wait_exponential, retry_if_exception_type
    TENACITY_AVAILABLE = True
except ImportError:
    TENACITY_AVAILABLE = False


def setup_logging(log_file: str = "logs/trm.log", level=logging.INFO):
    """Rotasyonlu log kurulumu (10 MB Г— 5 dosya)"""
    os.makedirs(os.path.dirname(log_file) or ".", exist_ok=True)

    handler = RotatingFileHandler(
        log_file,
        maxBytes=10 * 1024 * 1024,  # 10 MB
        backupCount=5,
        encoding='utf-8'
    )
    formatter = logging.Formatter(
        '%(asctime)s - %(name)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s'
    )
    handler.setFormatter(formatter)

    root = logging.getLogger()
    root.setLevel(level)
    # Var olan handler'larДұ temizle (duplicate Г¶nle)
    root.handlers = [h for h in root.handlers if not isinstance(h, logging.FileHandler)]
    root.addHandler(handler)

    # Konsola da yaz
    console = logging.StreamHandler()
    console.setFormatter(formatter)
    if not any(isinstance(h, logging.StreamHandler) and not isinstance(h, logging.FileHandler)
               for h in root.handlers):
        root.addHandler(console)


def safe_read_queue(queue_file: str) -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:
    """File-lock korumalДұ JSON kuyruk okuma"""
    if not os.path.exists(queue_file):
        return []

    lock_path = f"{queue_file}.lock"

    def _read():
        try:
            with open(queue_file, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                return json.load(f)
        except (FileNotFoundError, json.JSONDecodeError):
            return []

    if FILELOCK_AVAILABLE:
        with FileLock(lock_path, timeout=10):
            return _read()
    return _read()


def safe_write_queue(queue_file: str, data: List[Dict[str, Any]]) -> bool:
    """File-lock korumalДұ JSON kuyruk yazma"""
    lock_path = f"{queue_file}.lock"

    def _write():
        # Atomic write: Г¶nce tmp'ye, sonra rename
        tmp_path = f"{queue_file}.tmp"
        with open(tmp_path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
            json.dump(data, f, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2)
        os.replace(tmp_path, queue_file)
        return True

    try:
        if FILELOCK_AVAILABLE:
            with FileLock(lock_path, timeout=10):
                return _write()
        return _write()
    except Exception as e:
        logging.getLogger(__name__).error(f"Kuyruk yazma hatasДұ ({queue_file}): {e}")
        return False


def safe_append_to_queue(queue_file: str, item: Dict[str, Any]) -> bool:
    """File-lock korumalДұ kuyruk append (read+append+write tek lock altДұnda)"""
    lock_path = f"{queue_file}.lock"

    def _append():
        try:
            with open(queue_file, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                queue = json.load(f)
        except (FileNotFoundError, json.JSONDecodeError):
            queue = []

        queue.append(item)

        tmp_path = f"{queue_file}.tmp"
        with open(tmp_path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
            json.dump(queue, f, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2)
        os.replace(tmp_path, queue_file)
        return True

    try:
        if FILELOCK_AVAILABLE:
            with FileLock(lock_path, timeout=10):
                return _append()
        return _append()
    except Exception as e:
        logging.getLogger(__name__).error(f"Kuyruk append hatasДұ ({queue_file}): {e}")
        return False


# Retry decorator - API Г§aДҹrДұlarДұnda kullan
if TENACITY_AVAILABLE:
    def with_retry(max_attempts=3, min_wait=1, max_wait=10):
        """API Г§aДҹrДұlarДұ iГ§in exponential backoff retry"""
        return retry(
            stop=stop_after_attempt(max_attempts),
            wait=wait_exponential(multiplier=min_wait, max=max_wait),
            retry=retry_if_exception_type((ConnectionError, TimeoutError, OSError)),
            reraise=True
        )
else:
    def with_retry(max_attempts=3, min_wait=1, max_wait=10):
        """Tenacity yok - no-op decorator"""
        def decorator(func):
            return func
        return decorator
